tathā vikalpamukure dhyānapūjārcanātmani
ātmānaṃ bhairavaṃ paśyannacirāt tanmayībhavet
tanmayībhavanaṃ nāma prāptiḥ sānuttarātmani
pūrṇatvasya parā kāṣṭhā setyatra na phalāntaram
phalaṃ sarvamapūrṇatve tatra tatra prakalpitam
akalpite hi pūrṇatve phalamanyatkimucyatām
eṣa yāgavidhiḥ ko 'pi kasyāpi hṛdi vartate
yasya prasīdecciccakraṃ drāg apaścimajanmanaḥ
atra yāge gato rūḍhiṃ kaivalyamadhigacchati
lokairālokyamāno hi dehabandhavidhau sthitaḥ
atra nāthaḥ samācāraṃ paṭale 'ṣṭādaśe 'bhyadhāt
nātra śuddhirna cāśuddhirna bhakṣyādivicāraṇam
na dvaitaṃ nāpi cādvaitaṃ liṅgapūjādikaṃ na ca
na cāpi tatparityāgo niṣparigrahatāpi vā
saparigrahatā vāpi jaṭābhasmādisaṃgrahaḥ
tattyāgo na vratādīnāṃ caraṇācaraṇaṃ ca yat
kṣetrādisaṃpraveśaśca samayādiprapālanam
parasvarūpaliṅgādi nāmagotrādikaṃ ca yat
nāsminvidhīyate kiṃcinna cāpi pratiṣidhyate
vihitaṃ sarvamevātra pratiṣiddhamathāpi ca
kiṃ tvetadatra deveśi niyamena vidhīyate
tattve cetaḥ sthirīkāryaṃ suprasannena yoginā
tacca yasya yathaiva syātsa tathaiva samācaret
tattve niścalacittastu bhuñjāno viṣayānapi
na saṃspṛśyeta doṣaiḥ sa padmapatramivāmbhasā
viṣāpahārimantrādisaṃnaddho bhakṣayannapi
viṣaṃ na muhyate tena tadvadyogī mahāmatiḥ
aśuddhaṃ hi kathaṃ nāma dehādyaṃ pāñcabhautikam
prakāśatātirikte kiṃ śuddhyaśuddhī hi vastunaḥ
aśuddhasya ca bhāvasya śuddhiḥ syāttādṛśaiva kim
anyonyāśrayavaiyarthyānavasthā itthamatra hi
pṛthivī jalataḥ śudhyejjalaṃ dharaṇitastathā
anyonyāśrayatā seyamaśuddhatve 'pyayaṃ kramaḥ
aśuddhājjalataḥ śudhyeddhareti vyarthatā bhavet
vāyuto vāriṇo vāyostejasastasya vānyataḥ
bahurūpādikā mantrāḥ pāvanātteṣu śuddhatā
mantrāḥ svabhāvataḥ śuddhā yadi te 'pi na kiṃ tathā
śivātmatā teṣu śuddhiryadi tatrāpi sā na kim
śivātmatvāparijñānaṃ na mantreṣu dharādivat
te tena śuddhā iti cettajjñaptistarhi śuddhatā
yoginaṃ prati sā cāsti bhāveṣviti viśuddhatā
nanu codanayā śuddhyaśuddhyādikaviniścayaḥ
itthamastu tathāpyeṣā codanaiva śivoditā
kā syātsatīti cedetadanyatra pravitānitam
vaidikyā bādhiteyaṃ cedviparītaṃ na kiṃ bhavet
samyakcenmanyase bādho viśiṣṭaviṣayatvataḥ
apavādena kartavyaḥ sāmānyavihite vidhau
śuddhyaśuddhī ca sāmānyavihite tattvabodhini
puṃsi te bādhite eva tathā cātreti varṇitam
nārthavādādiśaṅkā ca vākye māheśvare bhavet
abuddhipūrvaṃ hi tathā saṃsthite satataṃ bhavet
vyomādirūpe nigame śaṅkā mithyārthatāṃ prati
anavacchinnavijñānavaiśvarūpyasunirbharaḥ
śāstrātmanā sthito devo mithyātvaṃ kvāpi nārhati
icchāvānbhāvarūpeṇa yathā tiṣṭhāsur īśvaraḥ
tatsvarūpābhidhānena tiṣṭhāsuḥ sa tathā sthitaḥ
arthavādo 'pi yatrānyavidhyādimukhamīkṣate
tatrāstvasatyaḥ svātantrye sa eva tu vidhāyakaḥ
vidhivākyāntare gacchannaṅgabhāvamathāpi vā
na nirarthakaṃ evāyaṃ saṃnidher gajaḍādivat
svārthapratyāyanaṃ cāsya svasaṃvittyaiva bhāsate
tadapahnavanaṃ kartuṃ śakyaṃ vidhiniṣedhayoḥ
yuktiścātrāsti vākyeṣu svasaṃviccāpyabādhitā
yā samagrārthamāṇikyatattvaniścayakāriṇī
mṛtadehe 'tha dehotthe yā cāśuddhiḥ prakīrtitā
anyatra neti buddhyantām aśuddhaṃ saṃvidaścyutam
saṃvittādātmyamāpannaṃ sarvaṃ śuddhamataḥ sthitam
śrīmadvīrāvalau coktaṃ śuddhyaśuddhinirūpaṇe
sarveṣāṃ vāhako jīvo nāsti kiṃcid ajīvakam
yatkiṃcijjīvarahitamaśuddhaṃ tadvijānata
tasmādyatsaṃvido nātidūre tacchuddhim āvahet
avikalpena bhāvena munayo 'pi tathābhavan
lokasaṃrakṣaṇārthaṃ tu tattattvaṃ taiḥ pragopitam
bahiḥ satsvapi bhāveṣu śuddhyaśuddhī na nīlavat
pramātṛdharma evāyaṃ cidaikyānaikyavedanāt
yadi vā vastudharmo 'pi mātrapekṣānibandhanaḥ
sautrāmaṇyāṃ surā hotuḥ śuddhānyasya viparyayaḥ
anena codanānāṃ ca svavākyairapi bādhanam
kvacitsaṃdarśitaṃ brahmahatyāvidhiniṣedhavat
bhakṣyādividhayo 'pyenaṃ nyāyamāśritya carcitāḥ
sarvajñānottarādau ca bhāṣate sma maheśvaraḥ
nararṣidevadruhiṇaviṣṇurudrādyudīritam
uttarottaravaiśiṣṭyāt pūrvapūrvaprabādhakam
na śaivaṃ vaiṣṇavairvākyairbādhanīyaṃ kadācana
vaiṣṇavaṃ brahmasambhūtairnetyādi paricarcayet
bādhate yo vaiparītyātsamūḍhaḥ pāpabhāgbhavet
tasmānmukhyatayā skanda lokadharmānna cācaret
nānyaśāstrasamuddiṣṭaṃ srotasyuktaṃ nije caret
yato yadyapi devena vedādyapi nirūpitam
tathāpi kila saṃkocabhāvābhāvavikalpataḥ
saṃkocatāratamyena pāśavaṃ jñānamīritam
vikāsatāratamyena patijñānaṃ tu bādhakam
idaṃ dvaitamidaṃ neti parasparaniṣedhataḥ
māyīyabhedakﾱptaṃ tatsyād akālpanike katham
uktaṃ bhargaśikhāyāṃ ca mṛtyukālakalādikam
dvaitādvaitavikalpotthaṃ grasate kṛtadhīriti
siddhānte liṅgapūjoktā viśvādhvamayatāvide
kulādiṣu niṣiddhāsau dehe viśvātmatāvide
iha sarvātmake kasmāttadvidhipratiṣedhane
niyamānupraveśena tādātmyapratipattaye
jaṭādi kaule tyāgo 'sya sukhopāyopadeśataḥ
vratacaryā ca mantrārthatādātmyapratipattaye
tanniṣedhastu mantrārthasārvātmyapratipattaye
kṣetrapīṭhopapīṭheṣu praveśo vighnaśāntaye
mantrādyārādhakasyātha tallābhāyopadiśyate
kṣetrādigamanābhāvavidhistu svātmanastathā
vaiśvarūpyeṇa pūrṇatvaṃ jñātumityapi varṇitam
samayācārasadbhāvaḥ pālyatvenopadiśyate
bhedaprāṇatayā tattattyāgāttattvaviśuddhaye
samayādiniṣedhastu mataśāstreṣu kathyate
nirmaryādaṃ svasaṃbodhaṃ sampūrṇaṃ budhyatāmiti
parakīyamidaṃ rūpaṃ dhyeyametattu me nijam
jvālādiliṅgaṃ cānyasya kapālādi tu me nijam
ādiśabdāttapaścaryāvelātithyādi kathyate
nāma śaktiśivādyantametasya mama nānyathā
gotraṃ ca gurusaṃtāno maṭhikākulaśabditaḥ
śrīsaṃtatistryambakākhyā tadardhāmardasaṃjñitā
itthamardhacatasro 'tra maṭhikāḥ śāṃkare krame
yugakrameṇa kūrmādyā mīnāntā siddhasaṃtatiḥ
ādiśabdena ca gharaṃ pallī pīṭhopapīṭhakam
mudrā chummeti teṣāṃ ca vidhānaṃ svaparasthitam
tādātmyapratipattyai hi svaṃ saṃtānaṃ samāśrayet
bhuñjīta pūjayeccakraṃ parasaṃtāninā nahi
etacca mataśāstreṣu niṣiddhaṃ khaṇḍanā yataḥ
akhaṇḍe 'pi pare tattve bhedenānena jāyate
evaṃ kṣetrapraveśādi saṃtānaniyamāntataḥ
nāsminvidhīyate taddhi sākṣānnaupayikaṃ śive
na tasya ca niṣedho yanna tattattvasya khaṇḍanam
viśvātmano hi nāthasya svasminrūpe vikalpitau
vidhirniṣedho vā śaktau na svarūpasya khaṇḍane
paratattvapraveśe tu yameva nikaṭaṃ yadā
upāyaṃ vetti sa grāhyastadā tyājyo 'tha vā kvacit
na yantraṇātra kāryeti proktaṃ śrītrikaśāsane
samatā sarvadevānām ovallīmantravarṇayoḥ
āgamānāṃ gatīnāṃ ca sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ yataḥ
sa hyakhaṇḍitasadbhāvaṃ śivatattvaṃ prapaśyati
yo hyakhaṇḍitasadbhāvamātmatattvaṃ prapadyate
ketakīkusumasaurabhe bhṛśaṃ bhṛṅga eva rasiko na makṣikā
bhairavīyaparamādvayārcane ko 'pi rajyati maheśacoditaḥ
asmiṃśca yoge viśrāntiṃ kurvatāṃ bhavaḍambaraḥ
himānīva mahāgrīṣme svayameva vilīyate
alaṃ vātiprasaṅgena bhūyasātiprapañcite
yogyo 'bhinavagupto 'sminko 'pi yāgavidhau budhaḥ
ityanuttarapadapravikāse śāktamaupayikamadya viviktam
āṇavena vidhinā paradhāma prepsatāmatha nirūpyata etat
vikalpasyaiva saṃskāre jāte niṣpratiyogini
abhīṣṭe vastuni prāptirniścitā bhogamokṣayoḥ
vikalpaḥ kasyacitsvātmasvātantryādeva susthiraḥ
upāyāntarasāpekṣyaviyogenaiva jāyate
kasyacittu vikalpo 'sau svātmasaṃskaraṇaṃ prati
upāyāntarasāpekṣastatroktaḥ pūrvako vidhiḥ
vikalpo nāma cinmātrasvabhāvo yadyapi sthitaḥ
tathāpi niścayātmāsāvaṇoḥ svātantryayojakaḥ
niścayo bahudhā caiṣa tatropāyāśca bhedinaḥ
aṇuśabdena te coktā dūrāntikavibhedataḥ
tatra buddhau tathā prāṇe dehe cāpi pramātari
apāramārthike 'pyasmin paramārthaḥ prakāśate
yataḥ prakāśāccinmātrāt prāṇādyavyatirekavat
tasyaiva tu svatantratvāddviguṇaṃ jaḍacidvapuḥ
uktaṃ traiśirase caitaddevyai candrārdhamaulinā
jīvaḥ śaktiḥ śivasyaiva sarvatraiva sthitāpi sā
svarūpapratyaye rūḍhā jñānasyonmīlanātparā
tasya cidrūpatāṃ satyāṃ svātantryollāsakalpanāt
paśyañjaḍātmatābhāgaṃ tirodhāyādvayo bhavet
tatra svātantryadṛṣṭyā vā darpaṇe mukhabimbavat
viśuddhaṃ nijacaitanyaṃ niścinotyatadātmakam
buddhiprāṇādito bhinnaṃ caitanyaṃ niścitaṃ balāt
satyatastadabhinnaṃ syāttasyānyonyavibhedataḥ
viśvarūpāvibheditvaṃ śuddhatvādeva jāyate
niṣṭhitaikasphuranmūrtermūrtyantaravirodhataḥ
antaḥ saṃvidi satsarvaṃ yadyapyaparathā dhiyi
prāṇe dehe 'thavā kasmātsaṃkrāmetkena vā katham
tathāpi nirvikalpe 'sminvikalpo nāsti taṃ vinā
dṛṣṭe 'pyadṛṣṭakalpatvaṃ vikalpena tu niścayaḥ
buddhiprāṇaśarīreṣu pāramaiśvaryam añjasā
vikalpyaṃ śūnyarūpe na pramātari vikalpanam
buddhirdhyānamayī tatra prāṇa uccāraṇātmakaḥ
uccāraṇaṃ ca prāṇādyā vyānāntāḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ
ādyā tu prāṇanābhikhyāparoccārātmikā bhavet
śarīrasyākṣaviṣayaitatpiṇḍatvena saṃsthitiḥ
tatra dhyānamayaṃ tāvadanuttaramihocyate
yaḥ prakāśaḥ svatantro 'yaṃ citsvabhāvo hṛdi sthitaḥ
sarvatattvamayaḥ proktametacca triśiromate
kadalīsaṃpuṭākāraṃ sabāhyābhyantarāntaram
īkṣate hṛdayāntaḥsthaṃ tatpuṣpamiva tattvavit
somasūryāgnisaṃghaṭṭaṃ tatra dhyāyed ananyadhīḥ
taddhyānāraṇisaṃkṣobhānmahābhairavahavyabhuk
hṛdayākhye mahākuṇḍe jājvalan sphītatāṃ vrajet
tasya śaktimataḥ sphītaśakterbhairavatejasaḥ
mātṛmānaprameyākhyaṃ dhāmābhedena bhāvayet
vahnyarkasomaśaktīnāṃ tadeva tritayaṃ bhavet
parā parāparā ceyamaparā ca sadoditā
sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhāraistāsāṃ pratyekatastridhā
caturthaṃ cānavacchinnaṃ rūpamāsāmakalpitam
evaṃ dvādaśa tā devyaḥ sūryabimbavadāsthitāḥ
ekaikamāsāṃ vahnyarkasomatacchāntibhāsanam
etad ānuttaraṃ cakraṃ hṛdayāccakṣurādibhiḥ
vyomabhirniḥsaratyeva tattadviṣayagocare
taccakrabhābhistatrārthe sṛṣṭisthitilayakramāt
somasūryāgnibhāsātma rūpaṃ samavatiṣṭhate
evaṃ śabdādiviṣaye śrotrādivyomavartmanā
cakreṇānena patatā tādātmyaṃ paribhāvayet
anena kramayogena yatra yatra patatyadaḥ
cakraṃ sarvātmakaṃ tattatsārvabhaumamahīśavat
itthaṃ viśvādhvapaṭalamayatnenaiva līyate
bhairavīyamahācakre saṃvittiparivārite
tataḥ saṃskāramātreṇa viśvasyāpi parikṣaye
svātmocchalattayā bhrāmyaccakraṃ saṃcintayenmahat
tatastaddāhyavilayāt tatsaṃskāraparikṣayāt
praśāmyadbhāvayeccakraṃ tataḥ śāntaṃ tataḥ śamam
anena dhyānayogena viśvaṃ cakre vilīyate
tatsaṃvidi tataḥ saṃvidvilīnārthaiva bhāsate
citsvābhāvyāt tato bhūyaḥ sṛṣṭiryaccinmaheśvarī
evaṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ viśvaṃ svasaṃvidi vilāpayan
visṛjaṃśca tato bhūyaḥ śaśvadbhairavatāṃ vrajet
evaṃ triśūlāt prabhṛti catuṣpañcārakakramāt
pañcāśadaraparyantaṃ cakraṃ yogī vibhāvayet
catuṣṣaṣṭiśatāraṃ vā sahasrāram athāpi vā
asaṃkhyārasahasraṃ vā cakraṃ dhyāyed ananyadhīḥ
saṃvinnāthasya mahato devasyollāsisaṃvidaḥ
naivāsti kācitkalanā viśvaśaktermaheśituḥ
śaktayo 'sya jagat kṛtsnaṃ śaktimāṃstu maheśvaraḥ
iti māṅgalaśāstre tu śrīśrīkaṇṭho nyarūpayat
ityetat prathamopāyarūpaṃ dhyānaṃ nyarūpayat
śrīśaṃbhunātho me tuṣṭastasmai śrīsumatiprabhuḥ
anayaiva diśānyāni dhyānānyapi samāśrayet
anuttaropāyadhurāṃ yānyāyānti kramaṃ vinā
atha prāṇasya yā vṛttiḥ prāṇanādyā nirūpitā
tadupāyatayā brūmo 'nuttarapravikāsanam
nijānande pramātraṃśamātre hṛdi purā sthitaḥ
śūnyatāmātraviśrānternirānandaṃ vibhāvayet
prāṇodaye prameye tu parānandaṃ vibhāvayet
tatrānantaprameyāṃśapūraṇāpānanirvṛtaḥ
parānandagatastiṣṭhedapānaśaśiśobhitaḥ
tato 'nantasphuranmeyasaṃghaṭṭaikāntanirvṛtaḥ
samānabhūmimāgatya brahmānandamayo bhavet
tato 'pi mānameyaughakalanāgrāsatatparaḥ
udānavahnau viśrānto mahānandaṃ vibhāvayet
tatra viśrāntimabhyetya śāmyatyasminmahārciṣi
nirupādhirmahāvyāptirvyānākhyopādhivarjitā
tadā khalu cidānando yo jaḍānupabṛṃhitaḥ
nahyatra saṃsthitiḥ kāpi vibhaktā jaḍarūpiṇaḥ
yatra ko 'pi vyavacchedo nāsti yadviśvataḥ sphurat
yadanāhatasaṃvitti paramāmṛtabṛṃhitam
yatrāsti bhāvanādīnāṃ na mukhyā kāpi saṃgatiḥ
tadeva jagadānandamasmabhyaṃ śaṃbhurūcivān
tatra viśrāntirādheyā hṛdayoccārayogataḥ
yā tatra samyagviśrāntiḥ sānuttaramayī sthitiḥ
ityetaddhṛdayādyekasvabhāve 'pi svadhāmani
ṣaṭprāṇoccārajaṃ rūpamatha vyāptyā taducyate
prāṇadaṇḍaprayogena pūrvāparasamīkṛteḥ
catuṣkikāmbujālambilambikāsaudhamāśrayet
triśūlabhūmiṃ krāntvāto nāḍitritayasaṅgatām
icchājñānakriyāśaktisamatve praviśet sudhīḥ
ekāṃ vikāsinīṃ bhūyastvasaṃkocāṃ vikasvarām
śrayed bhrūbindunādāntaśaktisopānamālikām
tatrordhvakuṇḍalībhūmau spandanodarasundaraḥ
visargastatra viśrāmyenmatsyodaradaśājuṣi
rāsabhī vaḍavā yadvatsvadhāmānandamandiram
vikāsasaṃkocamayaṃ praviśya hṛdi hṛṣyati
tadvanmuhurlīnasṛṣṭabhāvavrātasunirbharām
śrayedvikāsasaṃkocarūḍhabhairavayāmalām
ekīkṛtamahāmūlaśūlavaisargike hṛdi
parasminneti viśrāntiṃ sarvāpūraṇayogataḥ
atra tatpūrṇavṛttyaiva viśvāveśamayaṃ sthitam
prakāśasyātmaviśrāntāvahamityeva dṛśyatām
anuttaravimarśe prāgvyāpārādivivarjite
cidvimarśaparāhaṃkṛt prathamollāsinī sphuret
tata udyogasaktena sa dvādaśakalātmanā
sūryeṇābhāsayedbhāvaṃ pūrayedatha carcayet
athenduḥ ṣoḍaśakalo visargagrāsamantharaḥ
saṃjīvanyamṛtaṃ bodhavahnau visṛjati sphuran
icchājñānakriyāśaktisūkṣmarandhrasrugagragam
tadevamamṛtaṃ divyaṃ saṃviddevīṣu tarpakam
visargāmṛtametāvad bodhākhye hutabhojini
visṛṣṭaṃ cedbhavetsarvaṃ hutaṃ ṣoḍhādhvamaṇḍalam
yato 'nuttaranāthasya visargaḥ kulanāyikā
tatkṣobhaḥ kādihāntaṃ tatprasarastattvapaddhatiḥ
aṃa iti kuleśvaryā sahito hi kuleśitā
paro visargaviśleṣastanmayaṃ viśvamucyate
vitprāṇaguṇadehāntarbahirdravyamayīmimām
arcayejjuhuyāddhyāyeditthaṃ saṃjīvanīṃ kalām
ānandanāḍīyugalaspandanāvahitau sthitaḥ
enāṃ visarganiḥṣyandasaudhabhūmiṃ prapadyate
śākte kṣobhe kulāveśe sarvanāḍyagragocare
vyāptau sarvātmasaṃkoce hṛdayaṃ praviśetsudhīḥ
somasūryakalājālaparasparanigharṣataḥ
agnīṣomātmake dhāmni visargānanda unmiṣet
alaṃ rahasyakathayā guptametatsvabhāvataḥ
yoginīhṛdayaṃ tatra viśrāntaḥ syātkṛtī budhaḥ
hānādānatiraskāravṛttau rūḍhimupāgataḥ
abhedavṛttitaḥ paśyedviśvaṃ citicamatkṛteḥ
arthakriyārthitādainyaṃ tyaktvā bāhyāntarātmani
kharūpe nirvṛtiṃ prāpya phullāṃ nādadaśāṃ śrayet
vaktramantastayā samyak saṃvidaḥ pravikāsayet
saṃvidakṣamaruccakraṃ jñeyābhinnaṃ tato bhavet
tajjñeyaṃ saṃvidākhyena vahninā pravilīyate
vilīnaṃ tat trikoṇe 'smiñśaktivahnau vilīyate
tatra saṃvedanodārabindusattāsunirvṛtaḥ
saṃhārabījaviśrānto yogī paramayo bhavet
antarbāhye dvaye vāpi sāmānyetarasundaraḥ
saṃvitspandastriśaktyātmā saṃkocapravikāsavān
asaṃkocavikāso 'pi tadābhāsanatastathā
antarlakṣyo bahirdṛṣṭiḥ paramaṃ padamaśnute
tataḥ svātantryanirmeye vicitrārthakriyākṛti
vimarśanaṃ viśeṣākhyaḥ spanda aunmukhyasaṃjñitaḥ
tatra viśrāntimāgacchedyadvīryaṃ mantramaṇḍale
śāntyādisiddhayastattadrūpatādātmyato yataḥ
divyo yaścākṣasaṃgho 'yaṃ bodhasvātantryasaṃjñakaḥ
so 'nimīlita evaitat kuryātsvātmamayaṃ jagat
mahāsāhasasaṃyogavilīnākhilavṛttikaḥ
puñjībhūte svaraśmyoghe nirbharībhūya tiṣṭhati
akiṃciccintakastatra spaṣṭadṛgyāti saṃvidam
yadvisphuliṅgāḥ saṃsārabhasmadāhaikahetavaḥ
taduktaṃ parameśena triśirobhairavāgame
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi mantrabhūmyāṃ praveśanam
madhyanāḍyordhvagamanaṃ taddharmaprāptilakṣaṇam
visargāntapadātītaṃ prāntakoṭinirūpitam
adhaḥpravāhasaṃrodhādūrdhvakṣepavivarjanāt
mahāprakāśamudayajñānavyaktipradāyakam
anubhūya pare dhāmni mātrāvṛttyā puraṃ viśet
nistaraṅgāvatīrṇā sā vṛttirekā śivātmikā
catuṣṣaḍdvirdviguṇitacakraṣaṭkasamujjvalā
tatsthaṃ vicārayet khaṃ khaṃ khasthaṃ khasthena saṃviśet
khaṃ khaṃ tyaktvā khamāruhya khasthaṃ khaṃ coccarediti
khamadhyāsyādhikāreṇa padasthāścinmarīcayaḥ
bhāvayedbhāvamantaḥsthaṃ bhāvastho bhāvaniḥspṛhaḥ
bhāvābhāvagatī ruddhvā bhāvābhāvāvarodhadṛk
ātmāṇukulamūlāni śaktirbhūtiścitī ratiḥ
śaktitrayaṃ draṣṭṛdṛśyoparaktaṃ tadvivarjitam
etatkhaṃ daśadhā proktamuccāroccāralakṣaṇam
dhāmasthaṃ dhāmamadhyasthaṃ dhāmodarapuṭīkṛtam
dhāmnā tu bodhayeddhāma dhāma dhāmāntagaṃ kuru
taddhāma dhāmagatyā tu bhedyaṃ dhāmāntamāntaram
bhedopabhedabhedena bhedaḥ kāryastu madhyataḥ
iti praveśopāyo 'yamāṇavaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
śrīmaheśvaranāthena yo hṛtsthena mamoditaḥ
śrībrahmayāmale coktaṃ śrīmān rāvo daśātmakaḥ
sthūlaḥ sūkṣmaḥ paro hṛdyaḥ kaṇṭhyastālavya eva ca
sarvataśca vibhuryo 'sau vibhutvapadadāyakaḥ
jitarāvo mahāyogī saṃkrāmetparadehagaḥ
parāṃ ca vindati vyāptiṃ pratyahaṃ hyabhyaseta tam
tāvadyāvad arāve sā rāvāllīyeta rāviṇī
atra bhāvanayā dehagatopāyaiḥ pare pathi
vivikṣoḥ pūrṇatāsparśātprāgānandaḥ prajāyate
tato 'pi vidyudāpātasadṛśe dehavarjite
dhāmni kṣaṇaṃ samāveśādudbhavaḥ prasphuṭaṃ plutiḥ
jalapāṃsuvadabhyastasaṃviddehaikyahānitaḥ
svabalākramaṇāddehaśaithilyāt kampamāpnuyāt
galite dehatādātmyaniścaye 'ntarmukhatvataḥ
nidrāyate purā yāvanna rūḍhaḥ saṃvidātmani
tataḥ satyapade rūḍho viśvātmatvena saṃvidam
saṃvidan ghūrṇate ghūrṇirmahāvyāptiryataḥ smṛtā
ātmanyanātmābhimatau satyāmeva hyanātmani
ātmābhimāno dehādau bandho muktistu tallayaḥ
ādāvanātmanyātmatve līne labdhe nijātmani
ātmanyanātmatānāśe mahāvyāptiḥ pravartate
ānanda udbhavaḥ kampo nidrā ghūrṇiśca pañcakam
ityuktamata eva śrīmālinīvijayottare
pradarśite 'smin ānandaprabhṛtau pañcake yadā
yogī viśettadā tattaccakreśatvaṃ haṭhādvrajet
yathā sarveśinā bodhenākrāntāpi tanuḥ kvacit
kiṃcitkartuṃ prabhavati cakṣuṣā rūpasaṃvidam
tathaiva cakre kutrāpi praveśātko 'pi sambhavet
ānandacakraṃ vahnyaśri kanda udbhava ucyate
kampo hṛttālu nidrā ca ghūrṇiḥ syādūrdhvakuṇḍalī
etacca sphuṭamevoktaṃ śrīmattraiśirase mate
evaṃ pradarśitoccāraviśrāntihṛdayaṃ param
yattadavyaktaliṅgaṃ nṛśivaśaktyavibhāgavat
atra viśvamidaṃ līnamatrāntaḥsthaṃ ca gamyate
idaṃ tallakṣaṇaṃ pūrṇaśaktibhairavasaṃvidaḥ
dehagādhvasamunmeṣe samāveśastu yaḥ sphuṭaḥ
ahaṃtācchāditonmeṣibhāvedaṃbhāvayuk sa ca
vyaktāvyaktamidaṃ liṅgaṃ mantravīryaṃ parāparam
naraśaktisamunmeṣi śivarūpādvibheditam
yannyakkṛtaśivāhantāsamāveśaṃ vibhedavat
viśeṣaspandarūpaṃ tad vyaktaṃ liṅgaṃ cidātmakam
vyaktātsiddhiprasavo vyaktāvyaktāddvayaṃ vimokṣaśca
avyaktādbalamādyaṃ parasya nānuttare tviyaṃ carcā
ātmākhyaṃ yadvyaktaṃ naraliṅgaṃ tatra viśvamarpayataḥ
vyaktāvyaktaṃ tasmādgalite tasmiṃstadavyaktam
tenātmaliṅgametat parame śivaśaktyaṇusvabhāvamaye
avyakte viśrāmyati nānuttaradhāmagā tviyaṃ carcā
ekasya spandanasyaiṣā traidhaṃ bhedavyavasthitiḥ
atra liṅge sadā tiṣṭhet pūjāviśrāntitatparaḥ
yoginīhṛdayaṃ liṅgamidamānandasundaram
bījayonisamāpattyā sūte kāmapi saṃvidam
atra prayāsavirahātsarvo 'sau devatāgaṇaḥ
ānandapūrṇe dhāmnyāste nityoditacidātmakaḥ
atra bhairavanāthasya sasaṃkocavikāsikā
bhāsate durghaṭā śaktir asaṃkocavikāsinaḥ
etalliṅgasamāpattivisargānandadhārayā
siktaṃ tadeva sadviśvaṃ śaśvan navanavāyate
anuttare 'bhyupāyo 'tra tādrūpyādeva varṇitaḥ
jvaliteṣvapi dīpeṣu gharmāṃśuḥ kiṃ na bhāsate
artheṣu tadbhogavidhau tadutthe duḥkhe sukhe vā galitābhiśaṅkam
anāviśanto 'pi nimagnacittā jānanti vṛttikṣayasaukhyamantaḥ
satyevātmani citsvabhāvamahasi svānte tathopakriyāṃ tasmai kurvati tatpracāravivaśe satyakṣavarge 'pi ca
satsvartheṣu sukhādiṣu sphuṭataraṃ yadbhedavandhyodayaṃ yogī tiṣṭhati pūrṇaraśmivibhavas tattattvam ācīyatām
ityuccāravidhiḥ proktaḥ karaṇaṃ pravivicyate
taccetthaṃ triśiraḥśāstre parameśena bhāṣitam
grāhyagrāhakacidvyāptityāgākṣepaniveśanaiḥ
karaṇaṃ saptadhā prāhurabhyāsaṃ bodhapūrvakam
tadvyāptipūrvamākṣepe karaṇaṃ svapratiṣṭhatā
guruvaktrācca boddhavyaṃ karaṇaṃ yadyapi sphuṭam
tathāpyāgamarakṣārthaṃ tadagre varṇayiṣyate
ukto ya eṣa uccārastatra yo 'sau sphuran sthitaḥ
avyaktānukṛtiprāyo dhvanirvarṇaḥ sa kathyate
sṛṣṭisaṃhārabījaṃ ca tasya mukhyaṃ vapurviduḥ
tadabhyāsavaśādyāti kramādyogī cidātmatām
tathā hyanacke sācke vā kādau sānte punaḥpunaḥ
smṛte proccārite vāpi sā sā saṃvit prasūyate
bāhyārthasamayāpekṣā ghaṭādyā dhvanayo 'pi ye
te 'pyarthabhāvanāṃ kuryurmanorājyavadātmani
taduktaṃ parameśena bhairavo vyāpako 'khile
iti bhairavaśabdasya saṃtatoccāraṇācchivaḥ
śrīmattraiśirase 'pyuktaṃ mantroddhārasya pūrvataḥ
smṛtiśca smaraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ sarvabhāveṣu vastutaḥ
mantrasvarūpaṃ tadbhāvyasvarūpāpattiyojakam
smṛtiḥ svarūpajanikā sarvabhāveṣu rañjikā
anekākārarūpeṇa sarvatrāvasthitena tu
svasvabhāvasya saṃprāptiḥ saṃvittiḥ paramārthataḥ
vyaktiniṣṭhā tato viddhi sattā sā kīrtitā parā
kiṃ punaḥ samayāpekṣāṃ vinā ye bījapiṇḍakāḥ
saṃvidaṃ spandayantyete neyuḥ saṃvidupāyatām
vācyābhāvād udāsīnasaṃvitspandāt svadhāmataḥ
prāṇollāsanirodhābhyāṃ bījapiṇḍeṣu pūrṇatā
sukhasītkārasatsamyaksāmyaprathamasaṃvidaḥ
saṃvedanaṃ hi prathamaṃ sparśo 'nuttarasaṃvidaḥ
hṛtkaṇṭhyoṣṭhyatridhāmāntarnitarāṃ pravikāsini
caturdaśaḥ praveśo ya ekīkṛtatadātmakaḥ
tato visargoccārāṃśe dvādaśāntapathāvubhau
hṛdayena sahaikadhyaṃ nayate japatatparaḥ
kandahṛtkaṇṭhatālvagrakauṇḍilīprakriyāntataḥ
ānandamadhyanāḍyantaḥ spandanaṃ bījamāvahet
saṃhārabījaṃ khaṃ hṛtsthamoṣṭhyaṃ phullaṃ svamūrdhani
tejastryaśraṃ tālukaṇṭhe bindurūrdhvapade sthitaḥ
ityenayā budho yuktyā varṇajapyaparāyaṇaḥ
anuttaraṃ paraṃ dhāma praviśedacirāt sudhīḥ
varṇaśabdena nīlādi yadvā dīkṣottare yathā
saṃhāranragnimaruto rudrabinduyutānsmaret
hṛdaye tanmayo lakṣyaṃ paśyetsaptadinādatha
visphuliṅgāgnivan nīlapītaraktādicitritam
jājvalīti hṛdambhoje bījadīpaprabodhitam
dīpavajjvalito bindurbhāsate vighanārkavat
svayambhāsātmanānena tādātmyaṃ yāty ananyadhīḥ
śivena hematāṃ yadvattāmraṃ sūtena vedhitam
upalakṣaṇametacca sarvamantreṣu lakṣayet
yadyatsaṃkalpasambhūtaṃ varṇajālaṃ hi bhautikam
tat saṃvidādhikyavaśādabhautikamiva sthitam
atastathāvidhe rūpe rūḍho rohati saṃvidi
anācchāditarūpāyām anupādhau prasannadhīḥ
nīle pīte sukhe duḥkhe saṃvidrūpamakhaṇḍitam
gurubhirbhāṣitaṃ tasmādupāyeṣu vicitratā
uccārakaraṇadhyānavarṇairebhiḥ pradarśitaḥ
anuttarapadaprāptāvabhyupāyavidhikramaḥ
akiṃciccintanaṃ vīryaṃ bhāvanāyāṃ ca sā punaḥ
dhyāne tadapi coccāre karaṇe so 'pi taddhvanau
sa sthānakalpane bāhyamiti kramamupāśrayet
laṅghanena paro yogī mandabuddhiḥ krameṇa tu
vīryaṃ vinā yathā ṣaṇṭhastasyāpyastyatha vā balam
mṛtadeha iveyaṃ syādbāhyāntaḥparikalpanā
ityāṇave 'nuttaratābhyupāyaḥ prokto nayaḥ spaṣṭapathena bāhyaḥ
sthānaprakalpākhyatayā sphuṭastu bāhyo 'bhyupāyaḥ pravivicyate 'tha
sthānabhedastridhā proktaḥ prāṇe dehe bahistathā
prāṇaśca pañcadhā dehe dvidhā bāhyāntaratvataḥ
maṇḍalaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ pātramakṣasūtraṃ sapustakam
liṅgaṃ tūraṃ paṭaḥ pustaṃ pratimā mūrtireva ca
ityekādaśadhā bāhyaṃ punastadbahudhā bhavet
tatra prāṇāśrayaṃ tāvadvidhānamupadiśyate
adhvā samasta evāyaṃ ṣaḍvidho 'pyativistṛtaḥ
yo vakṣyate sa ekatra prāṇe tāvatpratiṣṭhitaḥ
adhvanaḥ kalanaṃ yattatkramākramatayā sthitam
kramākramau hi citraikakalanā bhāvagocare
kramākramātmā kālaśca paraḥ saṃvidi vartate
kālī nāma parā śaktiḥ saiva devasya gīyate
saiva saṃvidbahiḥ svātmagarbhībhūtau kramākramau
sphuṭayantī praroheṇa prāṇavṛttiriti sthitā
saṃvinmātraṃ hi yacchuddhaṃ prakāśaparamārthakam
tanmeyamātmanaḥ projjhya viviktaṃ bhāsate nabhaḥ
tadeva śūnyarūpatvaṃ saṃvidaḥ parigīyate
neti neti vimarśena yogināṃ sā parā daśā
sa eva khātmā meye 'sminbhedite svīkriyonmukhaḥ
patansamucchalattvena prāṇaspandormisaṃjñitaḥ
tenāhuḥ kila saṃvitprākprāṇe pariṇatā tathā
antaḥkaraṇatattvasya vāyurāśrayatāṃ gataḥ
iyaṃ sā prāṇanāśaktirāntarodyogadohadā
spandaḥ sphurattā viśrāntirjīvo hṛtpratibhā matā
sā prāṇavṛttiḥ prāṇādyai rūpaiḥ pañcabhirātmasāt
dehaṃ yatkurute saṃvitpūrṇastenaiṣa bhāsate
prāṇanāvṛttitādātmyasaṃvitkhacitadehajām
ceṣṭāṃ paśyantyato mugdhā nāstyanyaditi manvate
tāmeva bālamūrkhastrīprāyaveditṛsaṃśritām
matiṃ pramāṇīkurvantaścārvākās tattvadarśinaḥ
teṣāṃ tathā bhāvanā ced dārḍhyameti nirantaram
taddehabhaṅge suptāḥ syur ātādṛgvāsanākṣayāt
tadvāsanākṣaye tveṣāmakṣīṇaṃ vāsanāntaram
buddhaṃ kutaścitsaṃsūte vicitrāṃ phalasampadam
adārḍhyaśaṅkanāt prācyavāsanātādavasthyataḥ
anyakartavyaśaithilyātsaṃbhāvyānuśayatvataḥ
atadrūḍhānyajanatākartavyaparilopanāt
nāstikyavāsanāmāhuḥ pāpātpāpīyasīmimām
alamaprastutenātha prakṛtaṃ pravivicyate
yāvānsamasta evāyamadhvā prāṇe pratiṣṭhitaḥ
dvidhā ca so 'dhvā kriyayā mūrtyā ca pravibhajyate
prāṇa eva śikhā śrīmattriśirasyuditā hi sā
baddhā yāgādikāle tu niṣkalatvācchivātmikā
yato 'horātramadhye 'syāścaturviṃśatidhā gatiḥ
prāṇavikṣeparandhrākhyaśataiścitraphalapradā
kṣapā śaśī tathāpāno nāda ekatra tiṣṭhati
jīvādityo na codgacchettuṭyardhaṃ sāndhyamīdṛśam
ūrdhvavaktro raviścandro 'dhomukho vahnirantare
mādhyāhnikī mokṣadā syādvyomamadhyasthito raviḥ
anastamitasāro hi jantucakraprabodhakaḥ
binduḥ prāṇo hyahaścaiva ravirekatra tiṣṭhati
mahāsandhyā tṛtīyā tu supraśāntātmikā sthitā
evaṃ baddhā śikhā yatra tattatphalaniyojikā
ataḥ saṃvidi sarvo 'yamadhvā viśramya tiṣṭhati
amūrtāyāḥ sarvagatvānniṣkriyāyāśca saṃvidaḥ
mūrtikriyābhāsanaṃ yatsa evādhvā maheśituḥ
adhvā krameṇa yātavye pade saṃprāptikāraṇam
dvaitināṃ bhogyabhāvāttu prabuddhānāṃ yato 'dyate
iha sarvatra śabdānāmanvarthaṃ carcayedyataḥ
uktaṃ śrīmanniśācāre saṃjñātra trividhā matā
naimittikī prasiddhā ca tathānyā pāribhāṣikī
pūrvatve vā pradhānaṃ syāttatrāntarbhāvayettataḥ
ato 'dhvaśabdasyokteyaṃ niruktirnoditāpi cet
kvacitsvabuddhyā sāpyūhyā kiyallekhyaṃ hi pustake
tatra kriyābhāsanaṃ yatso 'dhvā kālāhva ucyate
varṇamantrapadābhikhyamatrāste 'dhvatrayaṃ sphuṭam
yastu mūrtyavabhāsāṃśaḥ sa deśādhvā nigadyate
kalātattvapurābhikhyamantarbhūtamiha trayam
trikadvaye 'tra pratyekaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ paraṃ vapuḥ
yato 'sti tena sarvo 'yamadhvā ṣaḍvidha ucyate
ṣaḍvidhādadhvanaḥ prācyaṃ yadetattritayaṃ punaḥ
eṣa eva sa kālādhvā prāṇe spaṣṭaṃ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
tattvamadhyasthitātkālādanyo 'yaṃ kāla ucyate
eṣa kālo hi devasya viśvābhāsanakāriṇī
kriyāśaktiḥ samastānāṃ tattvānāṃ ca paraṃ vapuḥ
etadīśvaratattvaṃ tacchivasya vapurucyate
udriktābhogakāryātmaviśvaikātmyamidaṃ yataḥ
etadīśvararūpatvaṃ paramātmani yatkila
tatpramātari māyīye kālatattvaṃ nigadyate
śivādiśuddhavidyāntaṃ yacchivasya svakaṃ vapuḥ
tadeva puṃso māyādirāgāntaṃ kañcukībhavet
anāśritaṃ yato māyā kalāvidye sadāśivaḥ
īśvaraḥ kālaniyatī sadvidyā rāga ucyate
anāśritaḥ śūnyamātā buddhimātā sadāśivaḥ
īśvaraḥ prāṇamātā ca vidyā dehapramātṛtā
anāśrayo hi śūnyatvaṃ jñānameva hi buddhitā
viśvātmatā ca prāṇatvaṃ dehe vedyaikatānatā
tena prāṇapathe viśvā kalaneyaṃ virājate
yena rūpeṇa tadvacmaḥ sadbhistadavadhīyatām
dvādaśāntāvadhāvasmindehe yadyapi sarvataḥ
otaprotātmakaḥ prāṇastathāpītthaṃ na susphuṭaḥ
yatno jīvanamātrātmā tatparaśca dvidhā mataḥ
saṃvedyaścāpy asaṃvedyo dvidhetthaṃ bhidyate punaḥ
sphuṭāsphuṭatvāddvaividhyaṃ pratyekaṃ paribhāvayet
saṃvedyajīvanābhikhyaprayatnaspandasundaraḥ
prāṇaḥ kandātprabhṛtyeva tathāpyatra na susphuṭaḥ
kandādhārātprabhṛtyeva vyavasthā tena kathyate
svacchandaśāstre nāḍīnāṃ vāyvādhāratayā sphuṭam
tatrāpi tu prayatno 'sau na saṃvedyatayā sthitaḥ
vedyayatnāttu hṛdayātprāṇacāro vibhajyate
prabhoḥ śivasya yā śaktirvāmā jyeṣṭhā ca raudrikā
satadanyatamāvātmaprāṇau yatnavidhāyinau
prabhuśaktiḥ kvacinmukhyā yathāṅgamarudīraṇe
ātmaśaktiḥ kvacitkandasaṃkocaspandane yathā
prāṇaśaktiḥ kvacitprāṇacāre hārde yathā sphuṭam
trayaṃ dvayaṃ vā mukhyaṃ syādyogināmavadhāninām
avadhānād adṛṣṭāṃśād balavattvād atheraṇāt
viparyayo 'pi prāṇātmaśaktīnāṃ mukhyatāṃ prati
vāmā saṃsāriṇāmīśā prabhuśaktirvidhāyinī
jyeṣṭhā tu suprabuddhānāṃ bubhutsūnāṃ ca raudrikā
vāmā saṃsāravamanā jyeṣṭhā śivamayī yataḥ
drāvayitrī rujāṃ raudrī roddhrī cākhilakarmaṇām
sṛṣṭyāditattvam ajñātvā na mukto nāpi mocayet
uktaṃ ca śrīyogacāre mokṣaḥ sarvaprakāśanāt
utpattisthitisaṃhārān ye na jānanti yoginaḥ
na muktāste tadajñānabandhanaikādhivāsitāḥ
sṛṣṭyādayaśca te sarve kālādhīnā na saṃśayaḥ
sa ca prāṇātmakastasmāduccāraḥ kathyate sphuṭaḥ
hṛdayātprāṇacāraśca nāsikyadvādaśāntataḥ
ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulo jantoḥ sarvasya svāṅgulakramāt
kṣodiṣṭhe vā mahiṣṭhe vā dehe tādṛśa eva hi
vīryamojo balaṃ spandaḥ prāṇacāraḥ samaṃ tataḥ
ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgule cāre yadgamāgamayugmakam
nālikātithimāsābdatatsaṅgho 'tra sphuṭaṃ sthitaḥ
tuṭiḥ sapādāṅgulayukprāṇastāḥ ṣoḍaśocchvasan
niḥśvasaṃścātra caṣakaḥ sapañcāṃśe 'ṅgule 'ṅgule
śvāsapraśvāsayornālī proktāhorātra ucyate
navāṅgulāmbudhituṭau praharāste 'bdhayo dinam
nirgame 'ntarniśenendū tayoḥ saṃdhye tuṭerdale
ketuḥ sūrye vidhau rāhurbhaumādervārabhāginaḥ
praharadvayamanyeṣāṃ grahāṇāmudayo 'ntarā
siddhirdavīyasī mokṣo 'bhicāraḥ pāralaukikī
aihikī dūranaikaṭyātiśayā praharāṣṭake
madhyāhnamadhyaniśayorabhijinmokṣabhogadā
nakṣatrāṇāṃ tadanyeṣāmudayo madhyataḥ kramāt
nāgā lokeśamūrtīśā gaṇeśā jalatattvataḥ
pradhānāntaṃ nāyakāśca vidyātattvādhināyakāḥ
sakalādyāśca kaṇṭhyoṣṭhyaparyantā bhairavāstathā
śaktayaḥ pārameśvaryo vāmeśā vīranāyakāḥ
aṣṭāvaṣṭau ye ya itthaṃ vyāpyavyāpakatājuṣaḥ
sthūlasūkṣmāḥ kramātteṣāmudayaḥ praharāṣṭake
dine krūrāṇi saumyāni rātrau karmāṇyasaṃśayam
krūratā saumyatā vābhisandherapi nirūpitā
dinarātrikṣaye muktiḥ sā vyāptidhyānayogataḥ
te coktāḥ parameśena śrīmadvīrāvalīkule
sitāsitau dīrghahrasvau dharmādharmau dinakṣape
kṣīyete yadi taddīkṣā vyāptyā dhyānena yogataḥ
ahorātraḥ prāṇacāre kathito māsa ucyate
dinaṃ kṛṣṇo niśā śuklaḥ pakṣau karmasu pūrvavat
yāḥ ṣoḍaśoktāstithayastāsu ye pūrvapaścime
tayostu viśramo 'rdhe 'rdhe tithyaḥ pañcadaśetarāḥ
sapāde dvyaṅgule tithyā ahorātro vibhajyate
prakāśaviśramavaśāttāveva hi dinakṣape
saṃvitpratikṣaṇaṃ yasmātprakāśānandayoginī
tau kﾱptau yāvati tayā tāvatyeva dinakṣape
yāvatyeva hi saṃvittiruditoditasusphuṭā
tāvāneva kṣaṇaḥ kalpo nimeṣo vā tadastvapi
yāvānevodayo vittervedyaikagrahatatparaḥ
tāvadevāstamayanaṃ veditṛsvātmacarvaṇam
vedye ca bahirantarvā dvaye vātha dvayojjhite
sarvathā tanmayībhūtirdinaṃ vettṛsthatā niśā
veditā vedyaviśrānto vettā tvantarmukhasthitiḥ
purā vicārayanpaścātsattāmātrasvarūpakaḥ
jāgradveditṛtā svapno vettṛbhāvaḥ purātanaḥ
paraḥ suptaṃ kṣaye rātridinayosturyamadvayam
kadācidvastuviśrāntisāmyenātmani carvaṇam
vedyavedakasāmyaṃ tat sā rātridinatulyatā
vedye viśrāntiradhikā dinadairghyāya tatra tu
nyūnā syātsvātmaviśrāntirviparīte viparyayaḥ
svātmautsukye prabuddhe hi vedyaviśrāntiralpikā
itthameva divārātrinyūnādhikyakramaṃ vadet
yathā deheṣvahorātranyūnādhikyādi no samam
tathā pureṣvapītyevaṃ tadviśeṣeṇa noditam
śrītraiyambakasantānavitatāmbarabhāskaraḥ
dinarātrikramaṃ me śrīśaṃbhur ittham apaprathat
śrīsantānagurustvāha sthānaṃ buddhāprabuddhayoḥ
hṛda ārabhya yattena rātriṃdivavibhājanam
tadasatsitapakṣe 'ntaḥ praveśollāsabhāgini
abuddhasthānamevaitaddinatvena kathaṃ bhavet
alaṃ vānena nedaṃ vā mama prāṅmatamatsaraḥ
heye tu darśite śiṣyāḥ satpathaikāntadarśinaḥ
vyākhyātaḥ kṛṣṇapakṣo yastatra prāṇagataḥ śaśī
āpyāyanātmanaikaikāṃ kalāṃ pratitithi tyajet
dvādaśāntasamīpe tu yāsau pañcadaśī tuṭiḥ
sāmāvasyātra sa kṣīṇaścandraḥ prāṇārkamāviśet
uktaṃ śrīkāmikāyāṃ ca nordhve 'dhaḥ prakṛtiḥ parā
ardhārdhe kramate māyā dvikhaṇḍā śivarūpiṇī
candrasūryātmanā dehaṃ pūrayet pravilāpayet
amṛtaṃ candrarūpeṇa dvidhā ṣoḍaśadhā punaḥ
pibanti ca surāḥ sarve daśapañca parāḥ kalāḥ
amā śeṣaguhāntaḥsthāmāvāsyā viśvatarpiṇī
evaṃ kalāḥ pañcadaśa kṣīyante śaśinaḥ kramāt
āpyāyinyamṛtābrūpatādātmyātṣoḍaśī na tu
tatra pañcadaśī yāsau tuṭiḥ prakṣīṇacandramāḥ
tadūrdhvagaṃ yattuṭyardhaṃ pakṣasaṃdhiḥ sa kīrtitaḥ
tasmādviśramatuṭyardhādāmāvasyaṃ purādalam
paraṃ prātipadaṃ cārdhamiti saṃdhiḥ sa kalpyate
tatra prātipade tasmiṃstuṭyardhārdhe purādalam
āmāvasyaṃ tithicchedātkuryātsūryagrahaṃ viśat
tatrārkamaṇḍale līnaḥ śaśī sravati yanmadhu
taptatvāttatpibedindusahabhūḥ siṃhikāsutaḥ
arkaḥ pramāṇaṃ somastu meyaṃ jñānakriyātmakau
rāhurmāyāpramātā syāttadācchādanakovidaḥ
tata eva tamorūpo vilāpayitumakṣamaḥ
tatsaṃghaṭṭādvayollāso mukhyo mātā vilāpakaḥ
arkendurāhusaṃghaṭṭāt pramāṇaṃ vedyavedakau
advayena tatastena puṇya eṣa mahāgrahaḥ
amāvasyāṃ vināpyeṣa saṃghaṭṭaścenmahāgrahaḥ
yathārke meṣage rāhāvaśvinīsthe 'śvinīdine
āmāvāsyaṃ yadā tvardhaṃ līnaṃ prātipade dale
pratipacca viśuddhā syāttanmokṣo dūrage vidhau
grāsamokṣāntare snānadhyānahomajapādikam
laukikālaukikaṃ bhūyaḥphalaṃ syātpāralaukikam
grāsyagrāsakatākṣobhaprakṣaye kṣaṇamāviśan
mokṣabhāgdhyānapūjādi kurvaṃścandrārkayorgrahe
tithiccheda ṛṇaṃ kāso vṛddhirniḥśvasanaṃ dhanam
ayatnajaṃ yatnajaṃ tu recanādatha rodhanāt
evaṃ prāṇe viśati citsūrya induṃ sudhāmayam
ekaikadhyena bodhāṃśuṃ kalayā paripūrayet
kramasampūraṇāśāliśaśāṅkāmṛtasundarāḥ
tuṭyaḥ pañcadaśaitāḥ syustithayaḥ sitapakṣagāḥ
antyāyāṃ pūrṇamastuṭyāṃ pūrvavatpakṣasandhitā
indugrahaśca pratipatsandhau pūrvapraveśataḥ
aihikaṃ grahaṇe cātra sādhakānāṃ mahāphalam
prāgvadanyadayaṃ māsaḥ prāṇacāre 'bda ucyate
ṣaṭsu ṣaṭsvaṅguleṣvarko hṛdayānmakarādiṣu
tiṣṭhan māghādikaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ kuryāttaccottarāyaṇam
saṃkrāntitritaye vṛtte bhukte cāṣṭādaśāṅgule
meṣaṃ prāpte ravau puṇyaṃ viṣuvatpāralaukikam
praveśe tu tulāsthe 'rke tadeva viṣuvadbhavet
iha siddhipradaṃ caitaddakṣiṇāyanagaṃ tataḥ
garbhatā prodbubhūṣiṣyadbhāvaś cāthodbubhūṣutā
udbhaviṣyattvamudbhūtiprārambho 'pyudbhavasthitiḥ
janma sattā pariṇatirvṛddhirhrāsaḥ kṣayaḥ kramāt
makarādīni tenātra kriyā sūte sadṛkphalam
āmutrike jhaṣaḥ kumbho mantrādeḥ pūrvasevane
catuṣkaṃ kila mīnādyamantikaṃ cottarottaram
praveśe khalu tatraiva śāntipuṣṭyādisundaram
karma syādaihikaṃ tacca dūradūraphalaṃ kramāt
nirgame dinavṛddhiḥ syādviparīte viparyayaḥ
varṣe 'smiṃstithayaḥ pañca pratyaṅgulamiti kramaḥ
tatrāpyahorātravidhiriti sarvaṃ hi pūrvavat
prāṇīye varṣa etasminkārtikādiṣu dakṣataḥ
pitāmahāntaṃ rudrāḥ syurdvādaśāgre 'tra bhāvinaḥ
prāṇe varṣodayaḥ prokto dvādaśābdodayo 'dhunā
kharasāstithya ekasmin ekasmin aṅgule kramāt
dvādaśābdodaye te ca caitrādyā dvādaśoditāḥ
caitre mantroditiḥ so 'pi tālunyukto 'dhunā punaḥ
hṛdi caitroditistena tatra mantrodayo 'pi hi
pratyaṅgulaṃ tithīnāṃ tu triśate parikalpite
sapañcāṃśāṅgule 'bdaḥ syātprāṇe ṣaṣṭyabdatā punaḥ
śatāni ṣaṭ sahasrāṇi caikaviṃśatirityayam
vibhāgaḥ prāṇagaḥ ṣaṣṭivarṣāhorātra ucyate
praharāharniśāmāsaṛtvabdaraviṣaṣṭigaḥ
yaśchedastatra yaḥ sandhiḥ sa puṇyo dhyānapūjane
iti prāṇodaye yo 'yaṃ kālaḥ śaktyekavigrahaḥ
viśvātmāntaḥsthitastasya bāhye rūpaṃ nirūpyate
ṣaṭ prāṇāścaṣakasteṣāṃ ṣaṣṭirnālī ca tāstathā
tithistattriṃśatā māsaste dvādaśa tu vatsaraḥ
abdaṃ pitryastvahorātra udagdakṣiṇato 'yanāt
pitṝṇāṃ yatsvamānena varṣaṃ taddivyamucyate
ṣaṣṭyadhikaṃ ca triśataṃ varṣāṇāmatra mānuṣam
tacca dvādaśabhirhatvā māsasaṃkhyātra labhyate
tāṃ punastriṃśatā hatvāhorātrakalpanā vadet
hatvā tāṃ caikaviṃśatyā sahasraiḥ ṣaṭśatena ca
prāṇasaṃkhyāṃ vadettatra ṣaṣṭyādyabdodayaṃ punaḥ
uktaṃ ca gurubhiḥ śrīmadrauravādisvavṛttiṣu
devānāṃ yadahorātraṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ sa hāyanaḥ
śatatrayeṇa ṣaṣṭyā ca nṝṇāṃ vibudhavatsaraḥ
śrīmatsvacchandaśāstre ca tadeva matamīkṣyate
pitṝṇāṃ tadahorātramityupakramya pṛṣṭhataḥ
evaṃ daivastvahorātra iti hyaikyopasaṃhṛtiḥ
tena ye guravaḥ śrīmatsvacchandoktidvayāditaḥ
pitryaṃ varṣaṃ divyadinamūcurbhrāntā hi te mudhā
divyārkābdasahasrāṇi yugeṣu caturāditaḥ
ekaikahānyā tāvadbhiḥ śataisteṣvaṣṭa saṃdhayaḥ
caturyugaikasaptatyā manvantaste caturdaśa
brahmaṇo 'hastatra cendrāḥ kramādyānti caturdaśa
brahmāho 'nte kālavahnerjvālā yojanalakṣiṇī
dagdhvā lokatrayaṃ dhūmāttvanyatprasvāpayettrayam
nirayebhyaḥ purā kālavahnervyaktiryatastataḥ
vibhuradhaḥsthito 'pīśa iti śrīrauravaṃ matam
brahmaniḥśvāsanirdhūte bhasmani svedavāriṇā
tadīyenāplutaṃ viśvaṃ tiṣṭhettāvanniśāgame
tasminniśāvadhau sarve pudgalāḥ sūkṣmadehagāḥ
agnivegeritā loke jane syurlayakevalāḥ
kūṣmāṇḍahāṭakādyāstu krīḍanti mahadālaye
niśākṣaye punaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ kurute tāmasāditaḥ
svakavarṣaśatānte 'sya kṣayastadvaiṣṇavaṃ dinam
rātriśca tāvatītyevaṃ viṣṇurudraśatābhidhāḥ
kramātsvasvaśatānteṣu naśyantyatrāṇḍalopataḥ
abādyavyaktatattvānteṣvitthaṃ varṣaśataṃ kramāt
dinarātrivibhāgaḥ syāt svasvāyuḥśatamānataḥ
brahmaṇaḥ pralayollāsasahasraistu rasāgnibhiḥ
avyaktastheṣu rudreṣu dinaṃ rātriśca tāvatī
tadā śrīkaṇṭha eva syātsākṣātsaṃhārakṛtprabhuḥ
sarve rudrāstathā mūle māyāgarbhādhikāriṇaḥ
avyaktākhye hyāviriñcācchrīkaṇṭhena sahāsate
nivṛttādhaḥsthakarmā hi brahmā tatrādhare dhiyaḥ
na bhoktā jño 'dhikāre tu vṛtta eva śivībhavet
sa eṣo 'vāntaralayastatkṣaye sṛṣṭirucyate
sāṃkhyavedādisaṃsiddhāñchrīkaṇṭhas tadaharmukhe
sṛjatyeva punastena na samyaṅmuktirīdṛśī
pradhāne yadahorātraṃ tajjaṃ varṣaśataṃ vibhoḥ
śrīkaṇṭhasyāyuretacca dinaṃ kañcukavāsinām
tatkramānniyatiḥ kālo rāgo vidyā kaletyamī
yāntyanyonyaṃ layaṃ teṣām āyur gāhanikaṃ dinam
taddinaprakṣaye viśvaṃ māyāyāṃ pravilīyate
kṣīṇāyāṃ niśi tāvatyāṃ gahaneśaḥ sṛjetpunaḥ
evamavyaktakālaṃ tu parārdhairdaśabhirjahi
māyāhastāvatī rātrirbhavetpralaya eṣa saḥ
māyākālaṃ parārdhānāṃ guṇayitvā śatena tu
aiśvaro divaso nādaḥ prāṇātmātra sṛjejjagat
tāvatī caiśvarī rātriryatra prāṇaḥ praśāmyati
prāṇagarbhasthamapyatra viśvaṃ sauṣumnavartmanā
prāṇe brahmabile śānte saṃvidyāpyavaśiṣyate
aṃśāṃśikāto 'pyetasyāḥ sūkṣmasūkṣmataro layaḥ
guṇayitvaiśvaraṃ kālaṃ parārdhānāṃ śatena tu
sādāśivaṃ dinaṃ rātrirmahāpralaya eva ca
sadāśivaḥ svakālānte bindvardhendunirodhikāḥ
ākramya nāde līyeta gṛhītvā sacarācaram
nādo nādāntavṛttyā tu bhittvā brahmabilaṃ haṭhāt
śaktitattve layaṃ yāti nijakālaparikṣaye
etāvacchaktitattve tu vijñeyaṃ khalvaharniśam
śaktiḥ svakālavilaye vyāpinyāṃ līyate punaḥ
vyāpinyā taddivārātraṃ līyate sāpyanāśrite
parārdhakoṭyā hatvāpi śaktikālamanāśrite
dinaṃ rātriśca tatkāle parārdhaguṇite 'pi ca
so 'pi yāti layaṃ sāmyasaṃjñe sāmanase pade
sa kālaḥ sāmyasaṃjñaḥ syānnityo 'kalyaḥ kalātmakaḥ
yattatsāmanasaṃ rūpaṃ tatsāmyaṃ brahma viśvagam
ataḥ sāmanasāt kālānnimeṣonmeṣamātrataḥ
tuṭyādikaṃ parārdhāntaṃ sūte saivātra niṣṭhitam
daśaśatasahasramayutaṃ lakṣaniyutakoṭi sārbudaṃ vṛndam
kharvanikharve śaṃkhābjajaladhimadhyāntamatha parārdhaṃ ca
ityekasmātprabhṛti hi daśadhā daśadhā krameṇa kalayitvā
ekādiparārdhānteṣvaṣṭādaśasu sthitiṃ brūyāt
catvāra ete pralayā mukhyāḥ sargāśca tatkalāḥ
bhūmūlanaiśaśaktisthāstadevāṇḍacatuṣṭayam
kālāgnirbhuvi saṃhartā māyānte kālatattvarāṭ
śrīkaṇṭho mūla ekatra sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakaḥ
tallayo vāntarastasmādekaḥ sṛṣṭilayeśitā
śrīmānaghoraḥ śaktyante saṃhartā sṛṣṭikṛcca saḥ
tatsṛṣṭau sṛṣṭisaṃhārā niḥsaṃkhyā jagatāṃ yataḥ
antarbhūtāstataḥ śāktī mahāsṛṣṭirudāhṛtā
laye brahmā harī rudraśatānyaṣṭakapañcakam
ityanyonyaṃ kramādyānti layaṃ māyāntake 'dhvani
māyātattvalaye tvete prayānti paramaṃ padam
māyordhve ye sitādhvasthāsteṣāṃ paraśive layaḥ
tatrāpyaupādhikādbhedāllaye bhedaṃ pare viduḥ
evaṃ tāttveśvare varge līne sṛṣṭau punaḥ pare
tatsādhakāḥ śiveṣṭā vā tatsthānamadhiśerate
brāhmī nāma parasyaiva śaktistāṃ yatra pātayet
sa brahmā viṣṇurudrādyā vaiṣṇavyāderataḥ kramāt
śaktimantaṃ vihāyānyaṃ śaktiḥ kiṃ yāti nedṛśam
chāditaprathitāśeṣaṃ śaktirekaḥ śivastathā
evaṃ visṛṣṭipralayāḥ prāṇa ekatra niṣṭhitāḥ
so 'pi saṃvidi saṃvicca cinmātre jñeyavarjite
cinmātrameva devī ca sā parā parameśvarī
aṣṭātriṃśaṃ ca tattattvaṃ hṛdayaṃ tatparāparam
tena saṃvittvamevaitatspandamānaṃ svabhāvataḥ
layodayā iti prāṇe ṣaṣṭyabdodayakīrtanam
icchāmātrapratiṣṭheyaṃ kriyāvaicitryacarcanā
kālaśaktistato bāhye naitasyā niyataṃ vapuḥ
svapnasvapne tathā svapne supte saṃkalpagocare
samādhau viśvasaṃhārasṛṣṭikramavivecane
mito 'pi kila kālāṃśo vitatatvena bhāsate
pramātrabhede bhede 'tha citro vitatimāpyasau
evaṃ prāṇe yathā kālaḥ kriyāvaicitryaśaktijaḥ
tathāpāne 'pi hṛdayānmūlapīṭhavisarpiṇi
mūlābhidhamahāpīṭhasaṅkocapravikāsayoḥ
brahmādyanāśritāntānāṃ cinute sṛṣṭisaṃhṛtī
śaśvadyadyapyapāno 'yam itthaṃ vahati kiṃtvasau
avedyayatno yatnena yogibhiḥ samupāsyate
hṛtkandānandasaṃkocavikāsadvādaśāntagāḥ
brahmādayo 'nāśritāntāḥ sevyante 'tra suyogibhiḥ
ete ca parameśānaśaktitvādviśvavartinaḥ
dehamapyaśnuvānāstatkāraṇānīti kāmike
bālyayauvanavṛddhatvanidhaneṣu punarbhave
muktau ca dehe brahmādyāḥ ṣaḍadhiṣṭhānakāriṇaḥ
tasyānte tu parā devī yatra yukto na jāyate
anena jñātamātreṇa dīkṣānugrahakṛdbhavet
samastakāraṇollāsapade suvidite yataḥ
akāraṇaṃ śivaṃ vindedyattadviśvasya kāraṇam
adhovaktraṃ tvidaṃ dvaitakalaṅkaikāntaśātanam
kṣīyate tadupāsāyāṃ yenordhvādharaḍambaraḥ
atrāpānodaye prāgvatṣaṣṭyabdodayayojanām
yāvatkurvīta tuṭyāderyuktāṅgulavibhāgataḥ
evaṃ samāne 'pi vidhiḥ sa hi hārdīṣu nāḍiṣu
saṃcaransarvatodikkaṃ daśadhaiva vibhāvyate
daśa mukhyā mahānāḍīḥ pūrayanneṣa tadgatāḥ
nāḍyantaraśritā nāḍīḥ krāmandehe samasthitiḥ
aṣṭāsu digdaleṣveṣa krāmaṃstaddikpateḥ kramāt
ceṣṭitānyanukurvāṇo raudraḥ saumyaśca bhāsate
sa eva nāḍītritaye vāmadakṣiṇamadhyage
indvarkāgnimaye mukhye caraṃstiṣṭhatyaharniśam
sārdhanālīdvayaṃ prāṇaśatāni nava yatsthitam
tāvadvahannahorātraṃ caturviṃśatidhā caret
viṣuvadvāsare prātaḥ sāṃśāṃ nālīṃ sa madhyagaḥ
vāmetarodaksavyānyair yāvat saṃkrāntipañcakam
evaṃ kṣīṇāsu pādonacaturdaśasu nāliṣu
madhyāhne dakṣaviṣuvannavaprāṇaśatīṃ vahet
dakṣodaganyodagdakṣaiḥ punaḥ saṃkrāntipañcakam
navāsu śatamekaikaṃ tato viṣuvaduttaram
pañcake pañcake 'tīte saṃkrānterviṣuvadbahiḥ
yadvattathāntaḥ saṅkrāntirnavaprāṇaśatāni sā
evaṃ rātrāvapītyevaṃ viṣuvaddivasātsamāt
ārabhyāharniśāvṛddhihrāsasaṅkrāntigo 'pyasau
rātryantadinapūrvāṃśau madhyāhno divasakṣayaḥ
sa śarvaryudayo madhyamudakto viṣutedṛśī
vyāptau viṣer yato vṛttiḥ sāmyaṃ ca vyāptirucyate
tadarhati ca yaḥ kālo viṣuvattadihoditaḥ
viṣuvatprabhṛti hrāsavṛddhī ye dinarātrige
tatkrameṇaiva saṃkrāntihrāsavṛddhī divāniśoḥ
itthaṃ samānamaruto varṣadvayavikalpanam
cāra ekatra nahyatra śvāsapraśvāsacarcanam
samāne 'pi tuṭeḥ pūrvaṃ yāvatṣaṣṭyabdagocaram
kālasaṃkhyā susūkṣmaikacāragā gaṇyate budhaiḥ
saṃdhyāpūrvāhṇamadhyāhnamadhyarātrādi yatkila
antaḥsaṃkrāntigaṃ grāhyaṃ tanmukhyaṃ tatphaloditeḥ
uktaḥ samānagaḥ kāla udāne tu nirūpyate
prāṇavyāptau yaduktaṃ tadudāne 'pyatra kevalam
nāsāśaktyantayoḥ sthāne brahmarandhrordhvadhāmanī
tenodāne 'tra hṛdayānmūrdhanyadvādaśāntagam
tuṭyādiṣaṣṭivarṣāntaṃ viśvaṃ kālaṃ vicārayet
vyāne tu viśvātmamaye vyāpake kramavarjite
sūkṣmasūkṣmocchaladrūpamātraḥ kālo vyavasthitaḥ
sṛṣṭiḥ pravilayaḥ sthemā saṃhāro 'nugraho yataḥ
kramātprāṇādike kāle taṃ taṃ tatrāśrayettataḥ
prāṇacāre 'tra yo varṇapadamantrodayaḥ sthitaḥ
yatnajo 'yatnajaḥ sūkṣmaḥ paraḥ sthūlaḥ sa kathyate
eko nādātmako varṇaḥ sarvavarṇāvibhāgavān
so 'nastamitarūpatvād anāhata ihoditaḥ
sa tu bhairavasadbhāvo mātṛsadbhāva eṣa saḥ
parā saikākṣarā devī yatra līnaṃ carācaram
hrasvārṇatrayamekaikaṃ ravyaṅgulamathetarat
praveśa iti ṣaḍvarṇāḥ sūryendupathagāḥ kramāt
ikārokārayorādisandhau saṃdhyakṣaradvayam
eo iti praveśe tu aiau iti dvayaṃ viduḥ
ṣaṇṭhārṇāni praveśe tu dvādaśāntalalāṭayoḥ
gale hṛdi ca bindvarṇavisargau paritaḥsthitau
kādipañcakamādyasya varṇasyāntaḥ sadoditam
evaṃ sasthānavarṇānāmantaḥ sā sārṇasantatiḥ
hṛdyeṣa prāṇarūpastu sakāro jīvanātmakaḥ
binduḥ prakāśo hārṇaśca pūraṇātmatayā sthitaḥ
uktaḥ paro 'yamudayo varṇānāṃ sūkṣma ucyate
praveśe ṣoḍaśaunmukhye ravayaḥ ṣaṇṭhavarjitāḥ
tadevendvarkamatrānye varṇāḥ sūkṣmodayastvayam
kālo 'rdhamātraḥ kādīnāṃ trayastriṃśata ucyate
mātrā hrasvāḥ pañca dīrghāṣṭakaṃ dvistriḥ plutaṃ tu ﾱ
ekāśītimimām ardhamātrāṇām āha no guruḥ
yadvaśādbhagavān ekāśītikaṃ mantramabhyadhāt
ekāśītipadā devī śaktiḥ proktā śivātmikā
śrīmātaṅge tathā dharmasaṃghātātmā śivo yataḥ
tathā tathā parāmarśaśakticakreśvaraḥ prabhuḥ
sthūlaikāśītipadajaparāmarśair vibhāvyate
tata eva parāmarśo yāvatyekaḥ samāpyate
tāvattatpadamuktaṃ no suptiṅniyamayantritam
ekāśītipadodāravimarśakramabṛṃhitaḥ
sthūlopāyaḥ paropāyastveṣa mātrākṛto layaḥ
ardhamātrā nava nava syuścaturṣu caturṣu yat
aṅguleṣviti ṣaṭtriṃśatyekāśītipadodayaḥ
aṅgule navabhāgena vibhakte navamāṃśakāḥ
vedā mātrārdhamanyattu dvicatuḥṣaḍguṇaṃ trayam
evamaṅgularandhrāṃśacatuṣkadvayagaṃ laghu
dīrghaṃ plutaṃ kramāddvitriguṇamardhaṃ tato 'pi hal
kṣakārastryardhamātrātmā mātrikaḥ satathāntarā
viśrāntāvardhamātrāsya tasmiṃstu kalite sati
aṅgulārdhe 'dribhāgena tvardhamātrā purā punaḥ
kṣakāraḥ sarvasaṃyogagrahaṇātmā tu sarvagaḥ
sarvavarṇodayādyantasandhiṣūdayabhāgvibhuḥ
itthaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśake cāre varṇānāmudayaḥ phale
krūre saumye vilomena hādi yāvadapaścimam
hṛdyakāro dvādaśānte hakārastadidaṃ viduḥ
ahamātmakamadvaitaṃ yaḥ prakāśātmaviśramaḥ
śivaśaktyavibhāgena mātraikāśītikā tviyam
dvāsaptatāvaṅguleṣu dviguṇatvena saṃsaret
uktaḥ sūkṣmodayastraidhaṃ dvidhoktastu parodayaḥ
atha sthūlodayo 'rṇānāṃ bhaṇyate guruṇoditaḥ
ekaikamardhapraharaṃ dine vargāṣṭakodayaḥ
rātrau ca hrāsavṛddhyatra kecidāhurna ke 'pi tu
eṣa vargodayo rātrau divā cāpy ardhayāmagaḥ
prāṇatrayodaśaśatī pañcāśadadhikā ca sā
adhyardhā kila saṃkrāntirvarge varge divāniśoḥ
tadaikye tūdayaścāraśatānāṃ saptaviṃśatiḥ
nava vargāṃstu ye prāhusteṣāṃ prāṇaśatī ravīn
satribhāgaiva saṃkrāntirvarge pratyekamucyate
aharniśaṃ tadaikye tu śatānāṃ śruticakṣuṣī
sthūlo vargodayaḥ so 'yamathārṇodaya ucyate
ekaikavarṇe prāṇānāṃ dviśataṃ ṣoḍaśādhikam
bahiścaṣakaṣaṭtriṃśaddina itthaṃ tathāniśi
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tatra raudraṃ śāktamathottaram
yāmalasthitiyoge tu rudraśaktyavibhāgitā
dinarātryavibhāge tu dṛgvahnyabdhyasucāraṇāḥ
sapañcamāṃśā nāḍī ca bahirvarṇodayaḥ smṛtaḥ
iti pañcāśikā seyaṃ varṇānāṃ paricarcitā
ekonāṃ ye tu tāmāhustanmataṃ sampracakṣmahe
vedāścārāḥ pañcamāṃśanyūnaṃ cārārdhamekaśaḥ
varṇe 'dhikaṃ taddviguṇamavibhāge divāniśoḥ
sthūlo varṇodayaḥ so 'yaṃ purā sūkṣmo nigadyate
iti kālatattvamuditaṃ śāstramukhāgamanijānubhavasiddham
atha paramarahasyo 'yaṃ cakrāṇāṃ bhaṇyate 'bhyudayaḥ
ityayatnajamākhyātaṃ yatnajaṃ tu nigadyate
bījapiṇḍātmakaṃ sarvaṃ saṃvidaḥ spandanātmatām
vidadhatparasaṃvittāvupāya iti varṇitam
yathāraghaṭṭacakrāgraghaṭīyantraughavāhanam
ekānusaṃdhiyatnena citraṃ yantrodayaṃ bhajet
ekānusaṃdhānabalājjāte mantrodaye 'niśam
tanmantradevatā yatnāttādātmyena prasīdati
khe rasaikākṣi nityotthe tadardhaṃ dvikapiṇḍake
trike sapta sahasrāṇi dviśatītyudayo mataḥ
catuṣke tu sahasrāṇi pañca caiva catuḥśatī
pañcārṇe 'bdhisahasrāṇi triśatī viṃśatistathā
ṣaṭke sahasratritayaṃ ṣaṭśatī codayo bhavet
saptake trisahasraṃ tu ṣaḍaśītyadhikaṃ smṛtam
śataistu saptaviṃśatyā varṇāṣṭakavikalpite
caturviṃśatiśatyā tu navārṇeṣūdayo bhavet
adhiṣaṣṭyekaviṃśatyā śatānāṃ daśavarṇake
ekānnaviṃśatiśataṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ śivārṇake
aṣṭādaśa śatāni syurudayo dvādaśārṇake
trayodaśārṇe dvāṣaṣṭyā śatāni kila ṣoḍaśa
tricatvāriṃśatā pañcadaśeti bhuvanārṇake
caturdaśaśatī khābdhiḥ syātpañcadaśavarṇake
trayodaśaśatī sārdhā ṣoḍaśārṇe tu kathyate
śatadvādaśikā saptadaśārṇe saikasaptatiḥ
aṣṭādaśārṇe vijñeyā śatadvādaśikā budhaiḥ
caturviṃśatisaṃkhyāke cakre navaśatī bhavet
saptaviṃśatisaṃkhyāte tūdayo 'ṣṭaśatātmakaḥ
dvātriṃśake mahācakre ṣaṭśatī pañcasaptatiḥ
dvicaturviṃśake cakre sārdhāṃ śatacatuṣṭayīm
udayaṃ piṇḍayogajñaḥ piṇḍamantreṣu lakṣayet
catuṣpañcāśake cakre śatānāṃ tu catuṣṭayam
saptatriṃśatsahārdhena triśatyaṣṭāṣṭake bhavet
ardhamardhatribhāgaśca ṣaṭṣaṣṭirdviśatī bhavet
ekāśītipade cakre udayaḥ prāṇacāragaḥ
cakre tu ṣaṇṇavatyākhye sapādā dviśatī bhavet
aṣṭottaraśate cakre dviśatastūdayo bhavet
krameṇetthamidaṃ cakraṃ ṣaṭkṛtvo dviguṇaṃ yadā
tato 'pi dviguṇe 'ṣṭāṃśasyārdhamadhyardhamekakam
tato 'pi sūkṣmakuśalair ardhārdhādiprakalpane
bhāgaṣoḍaśakasthityā sūkṣmaścāro 'bhilakṣyate
evaṃ prayatnasaṃruddhaprāṇacārasya yoginaḥ
krameṇa prāṇacārasya grāsa evopajāyate
prāṇagrāsakramāvāptakālasaṃkarṣaṇasthitiḥ
saṃvidekaiva pūrṇā syājjñānabhedavyapohanāt
tathā hi prāṇacārasya navasyānudaye sati
na kālabhedajanito jñānabhedaḥ prakalpate
saṃvedyabhedānna jñānaṃ bhinnaṃ śikharivṛttavat
kālastu bhedakastasya sa tu sūkṣmaḥ kṣaṇo mataḥ
saukṣmyasya cāvadhirjñānaṃ yāvattiṣṭhati sa kṣaṇaḥ
anyathā na sa nirvaktuṃ nipuṇairapi pāryate
jñānaṃ kiyadbhavettāvattadabhāvo na bhāsate
tadabhāvaśca no tāvadyāvattatrākṣavartmani
arthe vātmapradeśe vā na saṃyogavibhāgitā
sā cedudayate spandamayī tatprāṇagā dhruvam
bhavedeva tataḥ prāṇaspandābhāve na sā bhavet
tadabhāvānna vijñānābhāvaḥ saivaṃ tu saiva dhīḥ
na cāsau vastuto dīrghā kālabhedavyapohanāt
vastuto hyata eveyaṃ kālaṃ saṃvinna saṃspṛśet
ata ekaiva saṃvittirnānārūpe tathātathā
vindānā nirvikalpāpi vikalpo bhāvagocare
spandāntaraṃ na yāvattaduditaṃ tāvadeva saḥ
tāvāneko vikalpaḥ syādvividhaṃ vastu kalpayan
ye tvitthaṃ na vidusteṣāṃ vikalpo nopapadyate
sa hyeko na bhavetkaścit trijagatyapi jātucit
śabdārūṣaṇayā jñānaṃ vikalpaḥ kila kathyate
sā ca syātkramikaivetthaṃ kiṃ kathaṃ ko vikalpayet
ghaṭa ityapi neyānsyādvikalpaḥ kā kathā sthitau
na vikalpaśca ko 'pyasti yo mātrāmātraniṣṭhitaḥ
na ca jñānasamūho 'sti teṣāmayugapatsthiteḥ
tenāsaṃgata evaiṣa vyavahāro vikalpajaḥ
tasmātspandāntaraṃ yāvannodiyāttāvadekakam
vijñānaṃ tadvikalpātmadharmakoṭīrapi spṛśet
ekāśītipadodāraśaktyāmarśātmakas tataḥ
vikalpaḥ śivatādāyī pūrvameva nirūpitaḥ
yathā karṇau nartayāmītyevaṃ yatnāttathā bhavet
cakracāragatādyatnāttadvattaccakragaiva dhīḥ
japahomārcanādīnāṃ prāṇasāmyamato vidhiḥ
siddhāmate kuṇḍalinīśaktiḥ prāṇasamonmanā
uktaṃ ca yoginīkaule tadetatparameśinā
padamantrākṣare cakre vibhāgaṃ śaktitattvagam
padeṣu kṛtvā mantrajño japādau phalabhāgbhavet
dvitrisaptāṣṭasaṃkhyātaṃ lopayecchatikodayam
iti śaktisthitā mantrā vidyā vā cakranāyakāḥ
padapiṇḍasvarūpeṇa jñātvā yojyāḥ sadā priye
nityodaye mahātattve udayasthe sadāśive
ayuktāḥ śaktimārge tu na japtāścodayena ye
te na sidhyanti yatnena japtāḥ koṭiśatairapi
mālāmantreṣu sarveṣu mānaso japa ucyate
upāṃśurvā śaktyudayaṃ teṣāṃ na parikalpayet
padamantreṣu sarveṣu yāvattatpadaśaktigam
śakyate satataṃ yuktaistāvajjapyaṃ tu sādhakaiḥ
tāvatī teṣu vai saṃkhyā padeṣu padasaṃjñitā
tāvantamudayaṃ kṛtvā tripadoktyāditaḥ kramāt
dvādaśākhye dvādaśite cakre sārdhaṃ śataṃ bhavet
udayastaddhi sacatuścatvāriṃśacchataṃ bhavet
ṣoḍaśākhye dvādaśite dvānavatyadhike śate
cārārdhena samaṃ proktaṃ śataṃ dvādaśakādhikam
ṣoḍaśākhye ṣoḍaśite bhaveccaturaśītigaḥ
udayo dviśataṃ taddhi ṣaṭpañcāśatsamuttaram
cārāṣṭabhāgāṃstrīnatra kathayantyadhikānbudhāḥ
aṣṭāṣṭake dvādaśite pādārdhaṃ viṃśatiṃ vasūn
udayaḥ saptaśatikā sāṣṭā ṣaṣṭiryato hi saḥ
eṣa cakrodayaḥ proktaḥ sādhakānāṃ hitāvahaḥ
nirudhya mānasīrvṛttīścakre viśrāntimāgataḥ
vyutthāya yāvadviśrāmyettāvaccārodayo hyayam
pūrṇe samudaye tvatra praveśaikātmyanirgamāḥ
traya ityata evoktaḥ siddhau madhyodayo varaḥ
ādyantodayanirmuktā madhyamodayasaṃyutāḥ
mantravidyācakragaṇāḥ siddhibhājo bhavanti hi
mantracakrodayajñastu vidyācakrodayārthavit
kṣipraṃ sidhyediti proktaṃ śrīmaddviṃśatike trike
dvistriścaturvā mātrābhirvidyāṃ vā cakrameva vā
tattvodayayutaṃ nityaṃ pṛthagbhūtaṃ japetsadā
piṇḍākṣarapadairmantramekaikaṃ śaktitattvagam
bahvakṣarastu yo mantro vidyā vā cakrameva vā
śaktisthaṃ naiva taṃ tatra vibhāgastvoṃnamo'ntagaḥ
asmiṃstattvodaye tasmādahorātrastriśastriśaḥ
vibhajyate vibhāgaśca punareva triśastriśaḥ
pūrvodaye tu viśramya dvitīyenollasedyadā
viśeccārdhardhikāyogāt tadoktārdhodayo bhavet
yadā pūrṇodayātmā tu samaḥ kālastrike sphuret
praveśaviśrāntyullāse syātsvatryaṃśodayastadā
etyeṣa kālavibhavaḥ prāṇa eva pratiṣṭhitaḥ
sa spade khe sa taccityāṃ tenāsyāṃ viśvaniṣṭhitiḥ
ataḥ saṃvitpratiṣṭhānau yato viśvalayodayau
śaktyante 'dhvani tatspandāsaṃkhyātā vāstavī tataḥ
uktaṃ śrīmālinītantre gātre yatraiva kutracit
vikāra upajāyeta tattattvaṃ tattvamuttamam
prāṇe pratiṣṭhitaḥ kālastadāviṣṭā ca yattanuḥ
dehe pratiṣṭhitasyāsya tato rūpaṃ nirūpyate
citspandaprāṇavṛttīnāmantyā yā sthūlatā suṣiḥ
sā nāḍīrūpatāmetya dehaṃ saṃtānayedimam
śrīsvacchande 'ta evoktaṃ yathā parṇaṃ svatantubhiḥ
vyāptaṃ tadvattanurdvāradvāribhāvena nāḍibhiḥ
pādāṅguṣṭhādikordhvasthabrahmakuṇḍalikāntagaḥ
kālaḥ samastaścaturaśītāvevāṅguleṣvitaḥ
dvādaśāntāvadhiṃ kiṃcitsūkṣmakālasthitiṃ viduḥ
ṣaṇṇavatyāmadhaḥ ṣaḍdvikramāccāṣṭottaraṃ śatam
atra madhyamasaṃcāriprāṇodayalayāntare
viśve sṛṣṭilayāste tu citrā vāyvantarakramāt
ityeṣa sūkṣmaparimarśanaśīlanīyaścakrodayo 'nubhavaśāstradṛśā mayoktaḥ
deśādhvano 'pyatha samāsavikāsayogātsaṃgīyate vidhirayaṃ śivaśāstradṛṣṭaḥ
vicārito 'yaṃ kālādhvā kriyāśaktimayaḥ prabhoḥ
mūrtivaicitryajastajjo deśādhvātha nirūpyate
adhvā samasta evāyaṃ cinmātre sampratiṣṭhitaḥ
yattatra nahi viśrāntaṃ tan nabhaḥkusumāyate
saṃviddvāreṇa tatsṛṣṭe śūnye dhiyi marutsu ca
nāḍīcakrānucakreṣu barhirdehe 'dhvasaṃsthitiḥ
tatrādhvaivaṃ nirūpyo 'yaṃ yatastatprakriyākramam
anusaṃdadhadeva drāg yogī bhairavatāṃ vrajet
didṛkṣayaiva sarvārthān yadā vyāpyāvatiṣṭhate
tadā kiṃ bahunoktena ityuktaṃ spandaśāsane
jñātvā samastamadhvānaṃ tadīśeṣu vilāpayet
tān dehaprāṇadhīcakre pūrvavad gālayetkramāt
tatsamastaṃ svasaṃvittau sā saṃvidbharitātmikā
upāsyamānā saṃsārasāgarapralayānalaḥ
śrīmahīkṣottare caitānadhveśān gururabravīt
brahmānantātpradhānāntaṃ viṣṇuḥ puṃsaḥ kalāntagam
rudro granthau ca māyāyāmīśaḥ sādākhyagocare
anāśritaḥ śivastasmādvyāptā tadvyāpakaḥ paraḥ
evaṃ śivatvamāpannamiti matvā nyarūpyata
na prakriyāparaṃ jñānamiti svacchandaśāsane
triśiraḥśāsane bodho mūlamadhyāgrakalpitaḥ
ṣaṭtriṃśattattvasaṃrambhaḥ smṛtirbhedavikalpanā
avyāhatavibhāgo 'smibhāvo mūlaṃ tu bodhagam
samastatattvabhāvo 'yaṃ svātmanyevāvibhāgakaḥ
bodhamadhyaṃ bhavetkiṃcidādhārādheyalakṣaṇam
tattvabhedavibhāgena svabhāvasthitilakṣaṇam
bodhāgraṃ tattu vidbodhaṃ nistaraṅgaṃ bṛhatsukham
saṃvidekātmatānītabhūtabhāvapurādikaḥ
avyavacchinnasaṃvittirbhairavaḥ parameśvaraḥ
śrīdevyāyāmale coktaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśattattvasundaram
adhvānaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ dhyāyansadyaḥ śivamayo bhavet
yadyapyamuṣya nāthasya saṃvittyanatirekiṇaḥ
pūrṇasyordhvādimadhyāntavyavasthā nāsti vāstavī
tathāpi pratipattṝṇāṃ pratipādayitustathā
svasvarūpānusāreṇa madhyāditvādikalpanāḥ
tataḥ pramātṛsaṃkalpaniyamāt pārthivaṃ viduḥ
tattvaṃ sarvāntarālasthaṃ yatsarvāvaraṇairvṛtam
tadatra pārthive tattve kathyate bhuvanasthitiḥ
netā kaṭāharudrāṇāmanantaḥ kāmasevinām
potārūḍho jalasyāntarmadyapānavighūrṇitaḥ
sa devaṃ bhairavaṃ dhyāyan nāgaiśca parivāritaḥ
kālāgnerbhuvanaṃ cordhve koṭiyojanamucchritam
lokānāṃ bhasmasādbhāvabhayānnordhvaṃ sa vīkṣate
sa ca vyāptāpi viśvasya yasmātpluṣyannimāṃ bhuvam
narakebhyaḥ purā vyaktastenāsau tadadho mataḥ
daśa koṭyo vibhorjvālā tadardhaṃ śūnyamūrdhvataḥ
tadūrdhve narakādhīśāḥ kramādduḥkhaikavedanāḥ
adho madhye tadūrdhve ca sthitā bhedāntarairvṛtāḥ
avīcikumbhīpākākhyarauravāsteṣvanukramāt
ekādaśaikādaśa ca daśetyantaḥ śarāgni tat
pratyekameṣāmekonā koṭirucchritirantaram
lakṣamatra khavedāsyasaṃkhyānāmantarā sthitiḥ
kūṣmāṇḍa ūrdhve lakṣonakoṭisthānastadīśitā
śāstraviruddhācaraṇāt kṛṣṇaṃ ye karma vidadhate
tatra bhīmairlokapuruṣaiḥ pīḍyante bhogaparyantam
ye sakṛdapi parameśaṃ śivamekāgreṇa cetasā śaraṇam
yānti na te narakayujaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ teṣāṃ sukhālpatādāyi
sahasranavakotsedhamekāntaramatha kramāt
pātālāṣṭakamekaikamaṣṭame hāṭakaḥ prabhuḥ
pratilokaṃ niyuktātmā śrīkaṇṭho haṭhato bahūḥ
siddhīrdadātyasāvevaṃ śrīmadrauravaśāsane
vratino ye vikarmasthā niṣiddhācārakāriṇaḥ
dīkṣitā api ye luptasamayā naca kurvate
prāyaścittāṃstathā tatsthā vāmācārasya dūṣakāḥ
devāgnidravyavṛttyaṃśajīvinaścottamasthitāḥ
adhaḥsthagāruḍādyanyamantrasevāparāyaṇāḥ
te hāṭakavibhoragre kiṅkarā vividhātmakāḥ
te tu tatrāpi deveśaṃ bhaktyā cetparyupāsate
tadīśatattve līyante kramācca parame śive
anyathā ye tu vartante tadbhoganiratātmakāḥ
te kālavahnisaṃtāpadīnākrandaparāyaṇāḥ
guṇatattve nilīyante tataḥ sṛṣṭimukhe punaḥ
pātyante mātṛbhirghorayātanaughapurassaram
adhamādhamadeheṣu nijakarmānurūpataḥ
mānuṣānteṣu tatrāpi kecinmantravidaḥ kramāt
mucyante 'nye tu badhyante pūrvakṛtyānusārataḥ
ityeṣa gaṇavṛttānto nāmnā hulahulādinā
proktaṃ bhagavatā śrīmadānandādhikaśāsane
pātālordhve sahasrāṇi viṃśatirbhūkaṭāhakaḥ
siddhātantre tu pātālapṛṣṭhe yakṣīsamāvṛtam
bhadrakālyāḥ puraṃ yatra tābhiḥ krīḍanti sādhakāḥ
tatastamastaptabhūmistataḥśūnyaṃ tato 'hayaḥ
etāni yātanāsthānaṃ gurumantrādidūṣiṇām
tato bhūmyūrdhvato meruḥ sahasrāṇi sa ṣoḍaśa
magnastanmūlavistārastaddvayenordhvavistṛtiḥ
sahasrābdhivasūcchrāyo haimaḥ sarvāmarālayaḥ
madhyordhvādhaḥ samudvṛttaśarāvacaturaśrakaḥ
bhairavīyaṃ ca talliṅgaṃ dharaṇī cāsya pīṭhikā
sarve devā nilīnā hi tatra tatpūjitaṃ sadā
madhye merusabhā dhātustadīśadiśi ketanam
jyotiṣkaśikharaṃ śaṃbhoḥ śrīkaṇṭhāṃśaśca sa prabhuḥ
avaruhya sahasrāṇi manovatyāścaturdaśa
cakravāṭaścaturdikko meruratra tu lokapāḥ
amarāvatikendrasya pūrvasyāṃ dakṣiṇena tām
apsaraḥsiddhasādhyās tāmuttareṇa vināyakāḥ
tejovatī svadiśyagneḥ purī tāṃ paścimena tu
viśvedevā viśvakarmā kramāttadanugāśca ye
yāmyāṃ saṃyamanī tāṃ tu paścimena kramāt sthitāḥ
mātṛnandā svasaṃkhyātā rudrāstatsādhakāstathā
kṛṣṇāṅgārā nirṛtiśca tāṃ pūrveṇa piśācakāḥ
rakṣāṃsi siddhagandharvāstūttareṇottareṇa tām
vāruṇī śuddhavatyākhyā bhūtaugho dakṣiṇena tām
uttareṇottareṇaināṃ vasuvidyādharāḥ kramāt
vāyorgandhavatī tasyā dakṣiṇe kinnarāḥ punaḥ
vīṇāsarasvatī devī nāradastumburustathā
mahodayendorguhyāḥ syuḥ paścime 'syāḥ punaḥ punaḥ
kuberaḥ karmadevāśca tathā tatsādhakā api
yaśasvinī maheśasya tasyāḥ paścimato hariḥ
dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇe brahmāśvinau dhanvantariḥ kramāt
mairave cakravāṭe 'smin evaṃ mukhyāḥ puro 'ṣṭadhā
antarālagatāstvanyāḥ punaḥ ṣaḍviṃśatiḥ smṛtāḥ
iṣṭāpūrtaratāḥ puṇye varṣe ye bhārate narāḥ
te merugāḥ sakṛcchambhuṃ ye vārcanti yathocitam
meroḥ pradakṣiṇāpyodagdikṣu viṣkambhaparvatāḥ
mandaro gandhamādaśca vipulo 'tha supārśvakaḥ
sitapītanīlaraktāste kramātpādaparvatāḥ
etairbhuvamavaṣṭabhya merustiṣṭhati niścalaḥ
caitrarathanandanākhye vaibhrājaṃ pitṛvanaṃ vanānyāhuḥ
raktodamānasasitaṃ bhadraṃ caitaccatuṣṭayaṃ sarasām
vṛkṣāḥ kadambajambvaśvatthanyagrodhakāḥ kramaśaḥ
eṣu ca caturṣvacaleṣu trayaṃ trayaṃ kramaśa etadāmnātam
mervadho lavaṇābdhyantaṃ jambudvīpaḥ samantataḥ
lakṣamātraḥ sa navadhā jāto maryādaparvataiḥ
niṣadho hemakūṭaśca himavāndakṣiṇe trayaḥ
lakṣaṃ sahasranavatistadaśītiriti kramāt
nīlaḥ śvetastriśṛṅgaśca tāvantaḥ savyataḥ punaḥ
meroḥ ṣaḍete maryādācalāḥ pūrvāparāyatāḥ
pūrvato mālyavānpaścādgandhamādanasaṃjñitaḥ
savyottarāyatau tau tu catustriṃśatsahasrakau
aṣṭāvete tato 'pyanyau dvau dvau pūrvādiṣu kramāt
jāṭharaḥ kūṭahimavadyātrajārudhiśṛṅgiṇaḥ
evaṃ sthito vibhāgo 'tra varṣasiddhyai nirūpyate
samantāccakravāṭādho 'narkendu caturaśrakam
sahasranavavistīrṇamilākhyaṃ trimukhāyuṣam
meroḥ paścimato gandhamādo yastasya paścime
ketumālaṃ kulādrīṇāṃ saptakena vibhūṣitam
meroḥ pūrvaṃ mālyavānyo bhadrāśvastasya pūrvataḥ
sahasradaśakāyustatsapañcakulaparvatam
pūrvapaścimataḥ savyottarataśca kramādime
dvātriṃśacca catustriṃśatsahasrāṇi nirūpite
merorudak śṛṅgavānyastadbahiḥ kuruvarṣakam
cāpavannavasāhasramāyustatra trayodaśa
kuruvarṣasyottare 'tha vāyavye 'bdhau kramāccharāḥ
daśa ceti sahasrāṇi dvīpau candro 'tha bhadrakaḥ
yau śvetaśṛṅgiṇau merorvāme madhye hiraṇmayam
tayornavakavistīrṇamāyuś cārdhatrayodaśa
tatra vai vāmataḥ śvetanīlayo ramyako 'ntare
sahasranavavistīrṇamāyurdvādaśa tāni ca
merordakṣiṇato hemaniṣadhau yau tadantare
haryākhyaṃ navasāhasraṃ tatsahasrādhikāyuṣam
tatraiva dakṣiṇe hemahimavaddvitayāntare
kainnaraṃ navasāhasraṃ tatsahasrādhikāyuṣam
tatraiva dakṣiṇe merorhimavānyasya dakṣiṇe
bhārataṃ navasāhasraṃ cāpavatkarmabhogabhūḥ
ilāvṛtaṃ ketubhadraṃ kuruhairaṇyaramyakam
harikinnaravarṣe ca bhogabhūrna tu karmabhūḥ
atra bāhulyataḥ karmabhūbhāvo 'trāpyakarmaṇām
paśūnāṃ karmasaṃskāraḥ syāttādṛgdṛḍhasaṃskṛteḥ
sambhavantyapyasaṃskārā bhārate 'nyatra cāpi hi
dṛḍhaprāktanasaṃskārādīśecchātaḥ śubhāśubham
sthānāntare 'pi karmāsti dṛṣṭaṃ tacca purātane
tatra tretā sadā kālo bhārate tu caturyugam
bhārate navakhaṇḍaṃ ca sāmudreṇāmbhasātra ca
sthalaṃ pañcaśatī tadvajjalaṃ ceti vibhajyate
indraḥ kaśerustāmrābho nāgīyaḥ prāggabhastimān
saumyagāndharvavārāhāḥ kanyākhyaṃ cāsamudrataḥ
kanyādvīpe ca navame dakṣiṇenābdhimadhyagāḥ
upadvīpāḥ ṣaṭ kulādrisaptakena vibhūṣite
aṅgayavamalayaśaṅkuḥ kumudavarāhau ca malayago 'gastya
tatraiva ca trikūṭe laṅkā ṣaḍamī hyupadvīpāḥ
dvīpopadvīpagāḥ prāyo mlecchā nānāvidhā janāḥ
muktākāñcanaratnāḍhyā iti śrīruruśāsane
bhārate yatkṛtaṃ karma kṣapitaṃ vāpyavīcitaḥ
śivāntaṃ tena muktirvā kanyākhye tu viśeṣataḥ
mahākālādikā rudrakoṭiratraiva bhārate
gaṅgādipañcaśatikā janma tenātra durlabham
anyavarṣeṣu paśuvad bhogātkarmātivāhanam
prāpyaṃ manorathātītamapi bhāratajanmanām
nānāvarṇāśramācārasukhaduḥkhavicitratā
kanyādvīpe yatastena karmabhūḥ seyamuttamā
puṃsāṃ sitāsitānyatra kurvatāṃ kila sidhyataḥ
parāparau svarnirayāviti rauravavārtike
evaṃ meroradho jambūrabhito yaḥ sa vistarāt
syāt saptadaśadhā khaṇḍairnavabhistu samāsataḥ
manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasyāsan sutā daśa tatastrayaḥ
prāvrajannatha jambvākhye rājā yo 'gnīdhranāmakaḥ
tasyābhavannava sutāstato 'yaṃ navakhaṇḍakaḥ
nābhiryo navamastasya naptā bharata ārṣabhiḥ
tasyāṣṭau tanayāḥ sākaṃ kanyayā navamo 'ṃśakaḥ
bhuktaistairnavadhā tasmāllakṣayojanamātrakāt
lakṣaikamātro lavaṇastadbāhye 'sya puro 'drayaḥ
ṛṣabho dundubhirdhūmraḥ kaṅkadroṇendavo hyudak
varāhanandanāśokāḥ paścāt sahabalāhakau
dakṣiṇa cakramainākau vāḍavo 'ntastayoḥ sthitaḥ
abdherdakṣiṇataḥ khākṣisahasrātikramād giriḥ
vidyutvāṃstrisahasrocchridāyāmo 'tra phalāśinaḥ
maladigdhā dīrghakeśaśmaśravo gosadharmakāḥ
nagnāḥ saṃvatsarāśītijīvinastṛṇabhojinaḥ
niryantrāṇi sadā tatra dvārāṇi bilasiddhaye
ityetad gurubhirgītaṃ śrīmadrauravaśāsane
itthaṃ ya eṣa lavaṇasamudraḥ pratipāditaḥ
tadbahiḥ ṣaḍamī dvīpāḥ pratyekaṃ svārṇavairvṛtāḥ
kramadviguṇitāḥ ṣaḍbhirmanuputrairadhiṣṭhitāḥ
śākakuśakrauñcāḥ śalmaligomedhābjamiti ṣaḍdvīpāḥ
kṣīradadhisarpiraikṣavamadirāmadhurāmbukāḥ ṣaḍambudhayaḥ
medhātithirvapuṣmāñjyotiṣmāndyutimatā havī rājā
saṃvara iti śākādiṣu jambudvīpe nyarūpi cāgnīdhraḥ
girisaptakaparikalpitatāvatkhaṇḍāstu pañca śākādyāḥ
puṣkarasaṃjño dvidalo hariyamavaruṇendavo 'tra pūrvādau
tripañcāśacca lakṣāṇi dvikoṭyayutapañcakam
svādvarṇavāntaṃ mervardhād yojananām iyaṃ pramā
saptamajaladherbāhye haimī bhūḥ koṭidaśakamatha lakṣam
ucchrityā vistārādayutaṃ loketarācalaḥ kathitaḥ
lokālokadigaṣṭakasaṃsthaṃ rudrāṣṭakaṃ salokeśam
kevalamityapi kecillokālokāntare ravirna bahiḥ
pitṛdevapathāvasyodagdakṣiṇagau svajātpare vīthyau
bhānoruttaradakṣiṇamayanadvayametadeva kathayanti
sarveṣāmuttaro merurlokālokaśca dakṣiṇaḥ
udayāstamayāvitthaṃ sūryasya paribhāvayet
ardharātro 'marāvatyāṃ yāmyāyāmastameva ca
madhyandinaṃ tadvāruṇyāṃ saumye sūryodayaḥ smṛtaḥ
udayo yo 'marāvatyāṃ so 'rdharātro yamālaye
ke 'staṃ saumye ca madhyāhna itthaṃ sūryagatāgate
pañcatriṃśatkoṭisaṃkhyā lakṣāṇyekonaviṃśatiḥ
catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi dhvāntaṃ lokācalādbahiḥ
saptasāgaramānastu garbhodākhyaḥ samudrarāṭ
lokālokasya parato yadgarbhe nikhilaiva bhūḥ
siddhātantre 'tra garbhābdhestīre kauśeyasaṃjñitam
maṇḍalaṃ garuḍastatra siddhapakṣasamāvṛtaḥ
krīḍanti parvatāgre te nava cātra kulādrayaḥ
tata uṣṇodakās triṃśannadyaḥ pātālagāstataḥ
caturdiṅnaimirodyānaṃ yoginīsevitaṃ sadā
tato merustato nāgā meghā hemāṇḍakaṃ tataḥ
brahmaṇo 'ṇḍakaṭāhena merorardhena koṭayaḥ
pañcāśadevaṃ daśasu dikṣu bhūrlokasaṃjñitam
paśukhagamṛgatarumānuṣasarīsṛpaiḥ ṣaḍbhireṣa bhūrlokaḥ
vyāptaḥ piśācarakṣogandharvāṇāṃ sayakṣāṇām
vidyābhṛtāṃ ca kiṃ vā bahunā sarvasya bhūtasargasya
abhimānato yatheṣṭaṃ bhogasthānaṃ nivāsaśca
bhuvarlokastathā tvārkāllakṣamekaṃ tadantare
daśa vāyupathāste ca pratyekamayutāntarāḥ
ādyo vāyupathastatra vitataḥ paricarcyate
pañcāśadyojanordhve syādṛtarddhirnāma mārutaḥ
āpyāyakaḥ sa jantūnāṃ tataḥ prācetaso bhavet
pañcāśadyojanādūrdhvaṃ tasmādūrdhvaṃ śatena tu
senānīvāyur atraite mūkameghāstaḍinmucaḥ
ye mahyāḥ krośamātreṇa tiṣṭhanti jalavarṣiṇaḥ
tebhya ūrdhvaṃ śatānmeghā bhekādiprāṇivarṣiṇaḥ
pañcāśadūrdhvamogho 'tra viṣavāripravarṣiṇaḥ
meghāḥ skandodbhavāścānye piśācā oghamārute
tataḥ pañcāśadūrdhvaṃ syurmeghā mārakasaṃjñakāḥ
tatra sthāne mahādevajanmānaste vināyakāḥ
ye haranti kṛtaṃ karma narāṇāmakṛtātmanām
pañcāśadūrdhvaṃ vajrāṅko vāyuratropalāmbudāḥ
vidyādharādhamāścātra vajrāṅke sampratiṣṭhitāḥ
ye vidyāpauruṣe ye ca śmaśānādiprasādhane
mṛtāstatsiddhisiddhāste vajrāṅke maruti sthitāḥ
pañcāśadūrdhvaṃ vajrāṃkādvaidyuto 'śanivarṣiṇaḥ
abdā apsarasaścātra ye ca puṇyakṛto narāḥ
bhṛgau vahnau jale ye ca saṃgrāme cānivartinaḥ
gograhe vadhyamokṣe vā mṛtāste vaidyute sthitāḥ
vaidyutādraivatastāvāṃstatra puṣṭivahāmbudāḥ
ūrdhvaṃ ca rogāmbumucaḥ saṃvartāstadanantare
rocanāñjanabhasmādisiddhāstatraiva raivate
krodhodakamucāṃ sthānaṃ viṣāvartaḥ sa mārutaḥ
pañcāśadūrdhvaṃ tatraiva durdinābdā hutāśajāḥ
vidyādharaviśeṣāśca tathā ye parameśvaram
gāndharveṇa sadārcanti viṣāvarte 'tha te sthitāḥ
viṣāvartācchatādūrdhvaṃ durjayaḥ śvāsasaṃbhavaḥ
brahmaṇo 'tra sthitā meghāḥ pralaye vātakāriṇaḥ
puṣkarābdā vāyugamā gandharvāśca parāvahe
jīmūtameghāstatsaṃjñāstathā vidyādharottamāḥ
ye ca rūpavratā lokā āvahe te pratiṣṭhitāḥ
mahāvahe tvīśakṛtāḥ prajāhitakarāmbudāḥ
mahāparivahe meghāḥ kapālotthā maheśituḥ
mahāparivahānto 'yamṛtarddheḥ prāṅmarutpathaḥ
agnikanyā mātaraśca rudraśaktyā tvadhiṣṭhitāḥ
dvitīye tatpare siddhacāraṇā nijakarmajāḥ
turye devāyudhānyaṣṭau diggajāḥ pañcame punaḥ
ṣaṣṭhe garutmān anyasmin gaṅgānyatra vṛṣo vibhuḥ
dakṣastu navame brahmaśaktyā samadhiniṣṭhitaḥ
daśame vasavo rudrā ādityāśca marutpathe
navayojanasāhasro vigraho 'rkasya maṇḍalam
triguṇaṃ jñānaśaktiḥ sā tapatyarkatayā prabhoḥ
svarlokastu bhuvarlokāddhruvāntaṃ paribhāṣyate
sūryāllakṣeṇa śītāṃśuḥ kriyāśaktiḥ śivasya sā
candrāllakṣeṇa nākṣatraṃ tato lakṣadvayena tu
pratyekaṃ bhaumataḥ sūryasutānte pañcakaṃ viduḥ
saurāllakṣeṇa saptarṣivargastasmāddhruvastathā
brahmaivāpararūpeṇa brahmasthāne dhruvo 'calaḥ
medhībhūto vimānānāṃ sarveṣāmupari dhruvaḥ
atra baddhāni sarvāṇyapyūhyante 'nilamaṇḍale
svassapta mārutaskandhā āmeghādyāḥ pradhānataḥ
itaśca kratuhotrādi kṛtvā jñānavivarjitāḥ
svaryānti tatkṣaye lokaṃ mānuṣyaṃ puṇyaśeṣataḥ
evaṃ bhūmerdhruvāntaṃ syāllakṣāṇi daśa pañca ca
dve koṭī pañca cāśītirlakṣāṇi svargato mahān
mārkaṇḍādyā ṛṣimunisiddhāstatra pratiṣṭhitāḥ
nivartitādhikārāśca devā mahati saṃsthitāḥ
mahāntarāle tatrānye tvadhikārabhujo janāḥ
aṣṭau koṭyo mahallokājjano 'tra kapilādayaḥ
tiṣṭhanti sādhyāstatraiva bahavaḥ sukhabhāginaḥ
janāttapo'rkakoṭyo 'tra sanakādyā mahādhiyaḥ
prajāpatīnāṃ tatrādhikāro brahmātmajanmanām
brahmālayastu tapasaḥ satyaḥ ṣoḍaśa koṭayaḥ
tatra sthitaḥ sa svayambhūrviśvamāviṣkarotyadaḥ
satye vedāstathā cānye karmadhyānena bhāvitāḥ
ānandaniṣṭhāstatrordhve koṭir vairiñcamāsanam
brahmāsanātkoṭiyugmaṃ puraṃ viṣṇornirūpitam
dhyānapūjājapairviṣṇorbhaktā gacchanti tatpadam
vaiṣṇavātsaptakoṭībhirbhuvanaṃ parameśituḥ
rudrasya sṛṣṭisaṃhārakarturbrahmāṇḍavartmani
dīkṣājñānavihīnā ye liṅgārādhanatatparāḥ
te yāntyaṇḍāntare raudraṃ puraṃ nādhaḥ kadācana
tatsthāḥ sarve śivaṃ yānti rudrāḥ śrīkaṇṭhadīkṣitāḥ
adhikārakṣaye sākaṃ rudrakanyāgaṇena te
puraṃ puraṃ ca rudrordhvamuttarottaravṛddhitaḥ
brahmāṇḍādhaśca rudrordhvaṃ daṇḍapāṇeḥ puraṃ sa ca
śivecchayā dṛṇātyaṇḍaṃ mokṣamārgaṃ karoti ca
śarvarudrau bhīmabhavāvugro devo mahānatha
īśāna iti bhūrlokāt sapta lokeśvarāḥ śivāḥ
sthūlairviśeṣairārabdhāḥ sapta lokāḥ pare punaḥ
sūkṣmairiti guruścaiva rurau samyaṅnyarūpayat
ye brahmaṇādisarge svaśarīrānnirmitāḥ prabhūtākhyāḥ
sthūlāḥ pañca viśeṣāḥ saptāmī tanmayā lokāḥ
parato liṅgādhāraiḥ sūkṣmaistanmātrajairmahābhūtaiḥ
lokānāmāvaraṇairviṣṭabhya paraspareṇa gandhādyaiḥ
kālāgnerdaṇḍapāṇyantamaṣṭānavatikoṭayaḥ
ata ūrdhvaṃ kaṭāho 'ṇḍe sa ghanaḥ koṭiyojanam
pañcāśatkoṭayaścordhvaṃ bhūpṛṣṭhādadharaṃ tathā
evaṃ koṭiśataṃ bhūḥ syāt sauvarṇastaṇḍulastataḥ
śatarudrāvadhir huṃphaṭ bhedayettattu duḥśamam
pratidikkaṃ daśa daśetyevaṃ rudraśataṃ bahiḥ
brahmāṇḍādhārakaṃ tacca svaprabhāveṇa sarvataḥ
aṇḍasvarūpaṃ gurubhiścoktaṃ śrīrauravādiṣu
vyakterabhimukhībhūtaḥ pracyutaḥ śaktirūpataḥ
āvāpavān anirbhakto vastupiṇḍo 'ṇḍa ucyate
tamoleśānuviddhasya kapālaṃ sattvamuttaram
rajo'nuviddhaṃ nirmṛṣṭaṃ sattvamasyādharaṃ tamaḥ
vastupiṇḍa iti proktaṃ śivaśaktisamūhabhāk
aṇḍaḥ syāditi tadvyaktau saṃmukhībhāva ucyate
tathāpi śivamagnānāṃ śaktīnāmaṇḍatā bhavet
tadarthaṃ vākyamaparaṃ tā hi na cyutaśaktitaḥ
tanvakṣādau mā prasāṅkṣīdaṇḍateti padāntaram
tanvakṣādiṣu naivāste kasyāpy āvāpanaṃ yataḥ
tanvakṣasamudāyatve kathamekatvamityataḥ
anirbhakta iti proktaṃ sājātyaparidarśakam
vināpi vastupiṇḍākhyapadenaikaikaśo bhavet
tattveṣvaṇḍasvabhāvatvaṃ nanvevamapi kiṃ na tat
guṇatanmātrabhūtaughamaye tattve prasajyate
ucyate vastuśabdena tanvakṣabhuvanātmakam
rūpamuktaṃ yatastena tatsamūho 'ṇḍa ucyate
bhavecca tatsamūhatvaṃ patyurviśvavapurbhṛtaḥ
tadarthaṃ bhedakānyanyānyupāttānīti darśitam
tāvanmātrāsvavasthāsu māyādhīne 'dhvamaṇḍale
mā bhūdaṇḍatvamityāhuranye bhedakayojanam
itthamuktaviriñcāṇḍabhṛto rudrāḥ śataṃ hi yat
teṣāṃ sve patayo rudrā ekādaśa mahārciṣaḥ
ananto 'tha kapālyagnir yamanairṛtakau balaḥ
śīghro nidhīśo vidyeśaḥ śambhuḥ savīrabhadrakaḥ
madhu madhukṛtaḥ kadambaṃ kesarajālāni yadvadāvṛṇate
tadvatte śivarudrā brahmāṇḍamasaṃkhyaparivārāḥ
śarāṣṭaniyutaṃ koṭirityeṣāṃ saṃniveśanam
śrīkaṇṭhādhiṣṭhitāste ca sṛjanti saṃharanti ca
īśvaratvaṃ diviṣadāmiti rauravavārtike
siddhātantre tu hemāṇḍācchatakoṭer bahiḥ śatam
aṇḍānāṃ kramaśo dvidviguṇaṃ rūpyādiyojitam
teṣu krameṇa brahmāṇaḥ saṃsyurdviguṇajīvitāḥ
kṣīyante kramaśaste ca tadante tattvamammayam
dharāto 'tra jalādi syāduttarottarataḥ kramāt
daśadhāhaṃkṛtāntaṃ dhīstasyāḥ syācchatadhā tataḥ
sahasradhā vyaktamataḥ pauṃsnaṃ daśasahasradhā
niyatirlakṣadhā tasmāttasyāstu daśalakṣadhā
kalāntaṃ koṭidhā tasmānmāyā viddaśakoṭidhā
īśvaraḥ śatakoṭiḥ syāttasmātkoṭisahasradhā
sādākhyaṃ vyaśnute tacca śaktirvṛndena saṃkhyayā
vyāpinī sarvamadhvānaṃ vyāpya devī vyavasthitā
aprameyaṃ tataḥ śuddhaṃ śivatattvaṃ paraṃ viduḥ
jalādeḥ śivatattvāntaṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ kenacicchivāt
ṛte tataḥ śivajñānaṃ paramaṃ mokṣakāraṇam
tathā cāha mahādevaḥ śrīmatsvacchandaśāsane
nānyathā mokṣamāyāti paśurjñānaśatairapi
śivajñānaṃ na bhavati dīkṣām aprāpya śāṅkarīm
prāktanī pārameśī sā pauruṣeyī ca sā punaḥ
śatarudrordhvato bhadrakālyā nīlaprabhaṃ jayam
na yajñadānatapasā prāpyaṃ kālyāḥ puraṃ jayam
tadbhaktāstatra gacchanti tanmaṇḍalasudīkṣitāḥ
nirbījadīkṣayā mokṣaṃ dadāti parameśvarī
vidyeśāvaraṇe dīkṣāṃ yāvatīṃ kurute nṛṇām
tāvatīṃ gatimāyānti bhuvane 'tra niveśitāḥ
tataḥ koṭyā vīrabhadro yugāntāgnisamaprabhaḥ
vijayākhyaṃ puraṃ cāsya ye smaranto maheśvaram
jaleṣu maruṣu cāgnau śiraśchedena vā mṛtāḥ
te yānti bodhamaiśānaṃ vīrabhadraṃ mahādyutim
vairabhadrordhvataḥ koṭirviṣkambhādvistṛtaṃ tridhā
rudrāṇḍaṃ sālilaṃ tvaṇḍaṃ śakracāpākṛti sthitam
ā vīrabhadrabhuvanādbhadrakālyālayāttathā
trayodaśabhiranyaiśca bhuvanairupaśobhitam
tato bhuvaḥ sahādreḥ pūrgandhatanmātradhāraṇāt
mṛtā gacchanti tāṃ bhūmiṃ dharitryāḥ paramāṃ budhāḥ
abdheḥ puraṃ tatastvāpyaṃ rasatanmātradhāraṇāt
tataḥ śriyaḥ puraṃ rudrakrīḍāvataraṇeṣvatha
prayāgādau śrīgirau ca viśeṣānmaraṇena tat
sārasvataṃ puraṃ tasmācchabdabrahmavidāṃ padam
rudrocitāstā mukhyatvādrudrebhyo 'nyāstathā sthitāḥ
pureṣu bahudhā gaṅgā devādau śrīḥ sarasvatī
lakulādyamareśāntā aṣṭāvapsu surādhipāḥ
tatastu taijasaṃ tattvaṃ śivāgneratra saṃsthitiḥ
te cainaṃ vahnimāyānti vāhnīṃ ye dhāraṇāṃ śritāḥ
bhairavādiharīndvantaṃ taijase nāyakāṣṭakam
prāṇasya bhuvanaṃ vāyordaśadhā daśadhā tu tat
dhyātvā tyaktvātha vā prāṇān kṛtvā tatraiva dhāraṇām
taṃ viśanti mahātmāno vāyubhūtāḥ khamūrtayaḥ
bhīmādigayaparyantamaṣṭakaṃ vāyutattvagam
khatattve bhuvanaṃ vyomnaḥ prāpyaṃ tadvyomadhāraṇāt
vastrāpadāntaṃ sthāṇvādi vyomatattve surāṣṭakam
adīkṣitā ye bhūteṣu śivatattvābhimāninaḥ
jñānahīnā api prauḍhadhāraṇāste 'ṇḍato bahiḥ
dharābdhitejo'nilakhapuragā dīkṣitāśca vā
tāvatsaṃskārayogārthaṃ na paraṃ padamīhitum
tathāvidhāvatāreṣu mṛtāścāyataneṣu ye
tatpadaṃ te samāsādya kramādyānti śivātmatām
punaḥ punaridaṃ coktaṃ śrīmaddevyākhyayāmale
śrīkāmikāyāṃ kaśmīravarṇane coktavānvibhuḥ
sureśvarīmahādhāmni ye mriyante ca tatpure
brāhmaṇādyāḥ saṅkarāntāḥ paśavaḥ sthāvarāntagāḥ
rudrajātaya evaite ityāha bhagavāñchivaḥ
ākāśāvaraṇādūrdhvamahaṅkārādadhaḥ priye
tanmātrādimano'ntānāṃ purāṇi śivaśāsane
pañcavarṇayutaṃ gandhatanmātramaṇḍalaṃ mahat
ācchādya yojanānekakoṭibhiḥ sthitamantarā
evaṃ rasādimātrāṇāṃ maṇḍalāni svavarṇataḥ
śarvo bhavaḥ paśupatirīśo bhīma iti kramāt
tanmātreśā yadicchātaḥ śabdādyāḥ khādikāriṇaḥ
tataḥ sūryenduvedānāṃ maṇḍalāni vibhurmahān
ugraścetyeṣu patayastebhyo 'rkendū sayājakau
ityaṣṭau tanavaḥ śaṃbhoryāḥ parāḥ parikīrtitāḥ
aparā brahmaṇo 'ṇḍe tā vyāpya sarvaṃ vyavasthitāḥ
kalpe kalpe prasūyante dharādyāstābhya eva tu
tato vāgādikarmākṣayuktaṃ karaṇamaṇḍalam
agnīndraviṣṇumitrāḥ sabrahmāṇasteṣu nāyakāḥ
prakāśamaṇḍalaṃ tasmācchrutaṃ buddhyakṣapañcakam
digvidyudarkavaruṇabhuvaḥ śrotrādidevatāḥ
prakāśamaṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ sthitaṃ pañcārthamaṇḍalam
manomaṇḍalametasmāt somenādhiṣṭhitaṃ yataḥ
bāhyadeveṣvadhiṣṭhātā sāmyaiśvaryasukhātmakaḥ
manodevastato divyaḥ somo vibhurudīritaḥ
tato 'pi sakalākṣāṇāṃ yonerbuddhyakṣajanmanaḥ
sthūlādicchagalāntāṣṭayuktaṃ cāhaṅkṛteḥ puram
buddhitattvaṃ tato devayonyaṣṭakapurādhipam
paiśācaprabhṛtibrāhmaparyantaṃ tacca kīrtitam
etāni devayonīnāṃ sthānānyeva purāṇyataḥ
avatīryātmajanmānaṃ dhyāyantaḥ sambhavanti te
parameśaniyogācca codyamānāśca māyayā
niyāmitā niyatyā ca brahmaṇo 'vyaktajanmanaḥ
vyajyante tena sargādau nāmarūpairanekadhā
svāṃśenaiva mahātmāno na tyajanti svaketanam
uktaṃ ca śivatanāvidam adhikārapadasthitena guruṇā naḥ
aṣṭānāṃ devānāṃ śaktyāvirbhāvayonayo hyetāḥ
tanubhogāḥ punareṣāmadhaḥ prabhūtātmakāḥ proktāḥ
catvāriṃśattulyopabhogadeśādhikāni bhuvanāni
sādhanabhedātkevalamaṣṭakapañcakatayoktāni
etāni bhaktiyogaprāṇatyāgādigamyāni
teṣūmāpatireva prabhuḥ svatantrendriyo vikaraṇātmā
taratamayogena tato 'pi devayonyaṣṭakaṃ lakṣyaṃ tu
lokānāmakṣāṇi ca viṣayaparicchittikaraṇāni
gandhādermahadantādekādhikyena jātamaiśvaryam
aṇimādyātmakamasminpaiśācādye viriñcānte
jñātvaivaṃ śodhayedbuddhiṃ sārdhaṃ puryaṣṭakendriyaiḥ
krodheśāṣṭakamānīlaṃ saṃvartādyaṃ tato viduḥ
tejo'ṣṭakaṃ balādhyakṣaprabhṛtikrodhanāṣṭakāt
akṛtādi tato buddhau yogāṣṭakamudāhṛtam
svacchandaśāsane tattu mūle śrīpūrvaśāsane
yogāṣṭakapade yattu some śraikaṇṭhameva ca
tato māyāpuraṃ bhūyaḥ śrīkaṇṭhasya ca kathyate
tena dvitīyaṃ bhuvanaṃ tayoḥ pratyekamucyate
tatra māyāpuraṃ devyā yayā viśvamadhiṣṭhitam
pratikalpaṃ nāmabhedairbhaṇyate sā maheśvarī
umāpateḥ puraṃ paścānmātṛbhiḥ parivāritam
śrīkaṇṭha eva parayā mūrtyomāpatirucyate
brāhmyaiśī skandajā hārī vārāhyaindrī saviccikā
pītā śuklā pītanīle nīlā śuklāruṇā kramāt
agnīśasaumyayāmyāpyapūrvanairṛtagāstu tāḥ
aṃśena mānuṣe loke dhātrā tā hyavatāritāḥ
svacchandāstāḥ parāścānyāḥ pare vyomni vyavasthitāḥ
svacchandaṃ tā niṣevante saptadheyamumā yataḥ
umāpatipurasyordhvaṃ sthitaṃ mūrtyaṣṭakaṃ param
śarvādikaṃ yasya sṛṣṭirdharādyā yājakāntataḥ
tābhya īśānamūrtiryā sā merau sampratiṣṭhitā
śrīkaṇṭhaḥ sphaṭikādrau sā vyāptā tanvaṣṭakairjagat
ye yogaṃ saguṇaṃ śambhoḥ saṃyatāḥ paryupāsate
tanmaṇḍalaṃ vā dṛṣṭvaiva muktadvaitā hṛtatrayāḥ
guṇānām ādharauttaryācchuddhāśuddhatvasaṃsthiteḥ
tāratamyācca yogasya bhedātphalavicitratā
tato bhogaphalāvāptibhedādbhedo 'yamucyate
mūrtyaṣṭakopariṣṭāttu suśivā dvādaśoditāḥ
vāmādyekaśivāntāste kuṅkumābhāḥ sutejasaḥ
tadūrdhvaṃ vīrabhadrākhyo maṇḍalādhipatiḥ sthitaḥ
yattatsāyujyam āpannaḥ sa tena saha modate
tato 'pyaṅguṣṭhamātrāntaṃ mahādevāṣṭakaṃ bhavet
buddhitattvamidaṃ proktaṃ devayonyaṣṭakāditaḥ
mahādevāṣṭakānte tad yogāṣṭakamihoditam
tatra śraikaṇṭhamuktaṃ yat tasyaivomāpatistathā
mūrtayaḥ suśivā vīro mahādevāṣṭakaṃ vapuḥ
upariṣṭāddhiyo 'dhaśca prakṛterguṇasaṃjñitam
tattvaṃ tatra tu saṃkṣubdhā guṇāḥ prasuvate dhiyam
na vaiṣamyam anāpannaṃ kāraṇaṃ kāryasūtaye
guṇasāmyātmikā tena prakṛtiḥ kāraṇaṃ bhavet
nanvevaṃ sāpi saṃkṣobhaṃ vinā tānviṣamānguṇān
kathaṃ suvīta tatrādye kṣobhe syādanavasthitiḥ
sāṃkhyasya doṣa evāyaṃ yadi vā tena te guṇāḥ
avyaktamiṣṭāḥ sāmyaṃ tu saṅgamātraṃ na cetarat
asmākaṃ tu svatantreśatathecchākṣobhasaṃgatam
avyaktaṃ buddhitattvasya kāraṇaṃ kṣobhitā guṇāḥ
nanu tattveśvarecchāto yaḥ kṣobhaḥ prakṛteḥ purā
tadeva buddhitattvaṃ syāt kimanyaiḥ kalpitairguṇaiḥ
naitatkāraṇatārūpaparāmarśāvarodhi yat
kṣobhāntaraṃ tataḥ kāryaṃ bījocchūnāṅkurādivat
kramāttamorajaḥsattve gurūṇāṃ paṅktayaḥ sthitāḥ
tisro dvātriṃśadekātastriṃśadapyekaviṃśatiḥ
svajñanayogabalataḥ krīḍanto daiśikottamāḥ
trinetrāḥ pāśanirmuktāste 'trānugrahakāriṇaḥ
buddheśca guṇaparyantamubhe saptādhike śate
rudrāṇāṃ bhuvanānāṃ ca mukhyato 'nye tadantare
yogāṣṭakaṃ guṇaskandhe proktaṃ śivatanau punaḥ
yonīratītya gauṇe skandhe syuryogadātāraḥ
akṛtakṛtavibhuviriñcā harirguhaḥ kramavaśāttato devī
karaṇānyaṇimādiguṇāḥ kāryāṇi pratyayaprapañcaśca
avyaktādutpannā guṇāśca sattvādayo 'mīṣām
dharmajñānavirāgānaiśvaryaṃ tatphalāni vividhāni
yacchanti guṇebhyo 'mī puruṣebhyo yogadātāraḥ
tebhyaḥ parato bhuvanaṃ sattvādiguṇāsanasya devasya
sakalajagadekamāturbhartuḥ śrīkaṇṭhanāthasya
yenomāguhanīlabrahmaṛbhukṣakṛtākṛtādibhuvaneṣu
graharūpiṇyā śaktyā prābhvyādhiṣṭhāni bhūtāni
upasaṃjihīrṣuriha yaścaturānanapaṅkajaṃ samāviśya
dagdhvā caturo lokāñjanalokānnirmiṇoti punaḥ
yasyecchātaḥ sattvādiguṇaśarīrā visṛjati rudrāṇī
anukalpo rudrāṇyā vedī tatrejyate 'nukalpena
paśupatirindropendraviriñcairatha tadupalambhato devaiḥ
gandharvayakṣarākṣasapitṛmunibhiścitritāstathā yāgāḥ
guṇānāṃ yatparaṃ sāmyaṃ tadavyaktaṃ guṇordhvataḥ
krodheśacaṇḍasaṃvartā jyotiḥpiṅgalasūrakau
pañcāntakaikavīrau ca śikhodaścāṣṭa tatra te
gahanaṃ puruṣanidhānaṃ prakṛtirmūlaṃ pradhānamavyaktam
guṇakāraṇamityete māyāprabhavasya paryāyāḥ
yāvantaḥ kṣetrajñāḥ sahajāgantukamalopadigdhacitaḥ
te sarve 'tra vinihitā rudrāśca tadutthabhogabhujaḥ
mūḍhavivṛttavilīnaiḥ karaṇaiḥ kecittu vikaraṇakāḥ
akṛtādhiṣṭhānatayā kṛtyāśaktāni mūḍhāni
pratiniyataviṣayabhāñji sphuṭāni śāstre vivṛttāni
bhagnāni mahāpralaye sṛṣṭau notpāditāni līnāni
icchādhīnāni punarvikaraṇasaṃjñāni kāryamapyevam
puṃstattve tuṣṭinavakaṃ siddhayo 'ṣṭau ca tatpuraḥ
tāvatya evāṇimādibhuvanāṣṭakameva ca
atattve tattvabuddhyā yaḥ santoṣastuṣṭiratra sā
heye 'pyādeyadhīḥ siddhiḥ tathā coktaṃ hi kāpilaiḥ
ādhyātmikāścatasraḥ prakṛtyupādānakālabhāgyākhyāḥ
pañca viṣayoparamato 'rjanarakṣāsaṅgasaṃkṣayavighātaiḥ
ūhaḥ śabdo 'dhyayanaṃ duḥkhavighātāstrayaḥ suhṛtprāptiḥ
dānaṃ ca siddhayo 'ṣṭau siddheḥ pūrvo 'ṅkuśastrividhaḥ
aṇimādyūrdhvatastisraḥ paṅktayo guruśiṣyagāḥ
tatrāpi triguṇacchāyāyogāt tritvamudāhṛtam
nāḍīvidyāṣṭakaṃ cordhvaṃ paṅktīnāṃ syādiḍādikam
puṃsi nādamayī śaktiḥ prasarākhyā ca yatsthitā
na hyakartā pumānkartuḥ kāraṇatvaṃ ca saṃsthitam
akartaryapi vā puṃsi sahakāritayā sthite
śeṣakāryātmataiṣṭavyānyathā satkāryahānitaḥ
tasmāttathāvidhe kārye yā śaktiḥ puruṣasya sā
tāvanti rūpāṇyādāya pūrṇatāmadhigacchati
nāḍyaṣṭakordhve kathitaṃ vigrahāṣṭakamucyate
kāryaṃ heturduḥkhaṃ sukhaṃ ca vijñānasādhyakaraṇāni
sādhanamiti vigrahatāyugaṣṭakaṃ bhavati puṃstattve
bhuvanaṃ dehadharmāṇāṃ daśānāṃ vigrahāṣṭakāt
ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmākalkākrudho guroḥ
śuśrūṣāśaucasantoṣā ṛjuteti daśoditāḥ
puṃstattva eva gandhāntaṃ sthitaṃ ṣoḍaśakaṃ punaḥ
ārabhya dehapāśākhyaṃ puraṃ buddhiguṇāstataḥ
tatraivāṣṭāvahaṃkārastridhā kāmādikāstathā
pāśā āgantukagāṇeśavaidyeśvarabheditāḥ
trividhāste sthitāḥ puṃsi mokṣamārgoparodhakāḥ
yatkiṃcitparamādvaitasaṃvitsvātantryasundarāt
parācchivāduktarūpādanyattatpāśa ucyate
tadevaṃ puṃstvamāpanne pūrṇe 'pi parameśvare
tatsvarūpāparijñānaṃ citraṃ hi puruṣāstataḥ
uktānuktāstu ye pāśāḥ paratantroktalakṣaṇāḥ
te puṃsi sarve tāṃstatra śodhayanmucyate bhavāt
puṃsa ūrdhvaṃ tu niyatistatrasthāḥ śaṃkarā daśa
hemābhāḥ susitāḥ kālatattve tu daśa te śivāḥ
koṭiḥ ṣoḍaśasāhasraṃ pratyekaṃ parivāriṇaḥ
rāge vīreśabhuvanaṃ gurvantevāsināṃ puram
puraṃ cāśuddhavidyāyāṃ syācchaktinavakojjvalam
manonmanyantagāstāśca vāmādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ
kalāyāṃ syānmahādevatrayasya puramuttamam
tato māyā tripuṭikā mukhyato 'nantakoṭibhiḥ
ākrāntā sā bhagabilaiḥ proktaṃ śaivyāṃ tanau punaḥ
aṅguṣṭhamātraparyantaṃ mahādevāṣṭakaṃ niśi
cakrāṣṭakādhipatyena tathā śrīmālinīmate
vāmādyāḥ puruṣādau ye proktāḥ śrīpūrvaśāsane
te māyātattva evoktāstanau śaivyāmanantataḥ
kapālavratinaḥ svāṅgahotāraḥ kaṣṭatāpasāḥ
sarvābhayāḥ khaḍgadhārāvratāstattattvavedinaḥ
kramāttattattvamāyānti yatreśo 'nanta ucyate
uktaṃ ca tasya parataḥ sthānamanantādhipasya devasya
sthitivilayasargakarturguhābhagadvārapālasya
dharmānaṇimādiguṇāñjñānāni tapaḥsukhāni yogāṃśca
māyābilātpradatte puṃsāṃ niṣkṛṣya niṣkṛṣya
tacchaktīddhasvabalā guhādhikārāndhakāraguṇadīpāḥ
sarve 'nantapramukhā dīpyante śatabhavapramukhāntāḥ
so 'vyaktamadhiṣṭhāya prakaroti jaganniyogataḥ śambhoḥ
śuddhāśuddhasroto'dhikārahetuḥ śivo yasmāt
śivaguṇayoge tasmin mahati pade ye pratiṣṭhitāḥ prathamam
te 'nantāderjagataḥ sargasthitivilayakartāraḥ
māyābilamidamuktaṃ paratastu guhā jagadyoniḥ
utpattyā teṣvasyāḥ patiśaktikṣobhamanuvidhīyamāneṣu
yonivivareṣu nānākāmasamṛddheṣu bhagasaṃjñā
kāmayate patirenāmicchānuvidhāyinīṃ yadā devīm
pratibhagamavyaktādyāḥ prajāstadāsyāḥ prajāyante
teṣāmatisūkṣmāṇāmetāvattvaṃ na varṇyate vidhiṣu
avavarakāṇyekasmin yadvatsāle bahūni baddhāni
yonibilānyekasmiṃstadvanmāyāśiraḥsāle
māyāpaṭalaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ kuḍyaiḥ pihitāḥ parasparamadṛśyāḥ
nivasanti tatra rudrāḥ sukhinaḥ pratibilamasaṃkhyātāḥ
sthāne sāyujyagatāḥ sāmīpyagatāḥ pare salokasthāḥ
pratibhuvanamevamayaṃ nivāsināṃ gurubhiruddiṣṭaḥ
api sarvasiddhavācaḥ kṣīyerandīrghakālamudgīrṇāḥ
na punaryonyānantyāducyante srotasāṃ saṃkhyāḥ
tasmānnirayādyekaṃ yatproktaṃ dvārapālaparyantam
srotastenānyānyapi tulyavidhānāni vedyāni
avyaktakale guhayā prakṛtikalābhyāṃ vikāra ātmīyaḥ
otaḥ proto vyāptaḥ kalitaḥ pūrṇaḥ parikṣiptaḥ
madhye puṭatrayaṃ tasyā rudrāḥ ṣaḍadhare 'ntare
eka ūrdhve ca pañceti dvādaśaite nirūpitāḥ
gahanāsādhyau hariharadaśeśvarau trikalagopatī ṣaḍime
madhye 'nantaḥ kṣemo dvijeśavidyeśaviśvaśivāḥ
iti pañca teṣu pañcasu ṣaṭsu ca puṭageṣu tatparāvṛttyā
parivartate sthitiḥ kila devo 'nantastu sarvathā madhye
ūrdhvādharagakapālakapuṭaṣaṭkayugena tatparāvṛttyā
madhyato 'ṣṭābhirdiksthairvyāpto granthir mataṅgaśāstroktaḥ
śrīsāraśāsane punareṣā ṣaṭpuṭatayā vinirdiṣṭā
granthyākhyamidaṃ tattvaṃ māyākāryaṃ tato māyā
māyātattvaṃ vibhu kila gahanamarūpaṃ samastavilayapadam
tatra na bhuvanavibhāgo yukto granthāvasau tasmāt
māyātattvādhipatiḥ so 'nantaḥ samuditānvicāryāṇūn
yugapatkṣobhayati niśāṃ sā sūte saṃpuṭairanantaiḥ svaiḥ
tena kalādidharāntaṃ yaduktamāvaraṇajālamakhilaṃ tat
niḥsaṃkhyaṃ ca vicitraṃ māyaivaikā tvabhinneyam
uktaṃ śrīpūrvaśāstre ca dharāvyaktātmakaṃ dvayam
asaṃkhyātaṃ niśāśaktisaṃjñaṃ tvekasvarūpakam
pāśāḥ puroktāḥ praṇavāḥ pañca mānāṣṭakaṃ muneḥ
kulaṃ yoniśca vāgīśī yasyāṃ jāto na jāyate
dīkṣākāle 'dharādhvasthaśuddhau yaccādharādhvagam
anantasya samīpe tu tatsarvaṃ pariniṣṭhitam
sādhyo dātā damano dhyāno bhasmeti bindavaḥ pañca
pañcārthaguhyarudrāṅkuśahṛdayalakṣaṇaṃ ca savyūham
ākarṣādarśau cetyaṣṭakametatpramāṇānām
aluptavibhavāḥ sarve māyātattvādhikāriṇaḥ
māyāmayaśarīrāste bhogaṃ svaṃ paribhuñjate
pralayānte hyanantena saṃhṛtāste tvaharmukhe
anyānantaprasādena vibudhā api taṃ param
suptabuddhaṃ manyamānāḥ svatantrammanyatājaḍāḥ
svātmānameva jānanti hetuṃ māyāntarālagāḥ
ataḥ paraṃ sthitā māyā devī jantuvimohinī
devadevasya sā śaktiratidurghaṭakāritā
nirvairaparipanthinyā tayā bhramitabuddhayaḥ
idaṃ tattvamidaṃ neti vivadantīha vādinaḥ
