gurudevāgniśāstreṣu ye na bhaktā narādhamāḥ
satpathaṃ tānparityājya sotpathaṃ nayati dhruvam
asadyuktivicārajñāñchuṣkatarkāvalambinaḥ
bhramayatyeva tānmāyā hyamokṣe mokṣalipsayā
śivadīkṣāsinā chinnā śivajñānāsinā tathā
na prarohetpunarnānyo hetustacchedanaṃ prati
mahāmāyordhvataḥ śuddhā mahāvidyātha mātṛkā
vāgīśvarī ca tatrasthaṃ vāmādinavasatpuram
vāmā jyeṣṭhā raudrī kālī kalavikaraṇībalavikārike tathā
mathanī damanī manonmanī ca tridṛśaḥ pītāḥ samastāstāḥ
saptakoṭyo mukhyamantrā vidyātattve 'tra saṃsthitāḥ
ekaikārbudalakṣāṃśāḥ padmākārapurā iha
vidyārājñyastriguṇyādyāḥ sapta saptārbudeśvarāḥ
vidyātattvordhvamaiśaṃ tu tattvaṃ tatra kramordhvagam
śikhaṇḍyādyamanantāntaṃ purāṣṭakayutaṃ puram
śikhaṇḍī śrīgalo mūrtirekanetraikarudrakau
śivottamaḥ sūkṣmarudro 'nanto vidyeśvarāṣṭakam
kramādūrdhvordhvasaṃsthānaṃ saptānāṃ nāyako vibhuḥ
ananta eva dhyeyaśca pūjyaś cāpy uttarottaraḥ
mukhyamantreśvarāṇāṃ yat sārdhaṃ koṭitrayaṃ sthitam
tannāyakā ime tena vidyeśāścakravartinaḥ
uktaṃ ca gurubhiritthaṃ śivatanvādyeṣu śāsaneṣvetat
bhagabilaśatakalitaguhāmūrdhāsanago 'ṣṭaśaktiyugdevaḥ
gahanādyaṃ nirayāntaṃ sṛjati ca rudrāṃśca viniyuṅkte
uddharati manonmanyā puṃsasteṣveva bhavati madhyasthaḥ
te tenodastacitaḥ paratattvālocane 'bhiniviśante
sa punaradhaḥ pathavartiṣvadhikṛta evāṇuṣu śivena
avasitapativiniyogaḥ sārdhamanekātmamantrakoṭībhiḥ
nirvātyanantanāthastaddhāmāviśati sūkṣmarudrastu
anugṛhyāṇumapūrvaṃ sthāpayati patiḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ sthāne
ityaṣṭau paripāṭyā yāvaddhāmāni yāti gururekaḥ
tāvadasaṃkhyātānāṃ jantūnāṃ nirvṛtiṃ kurute
te 'ṣṭāvapi śaktyaṣṭakayogāmalajalaruhāsanāsīnāḥ
ālokayanti devaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ kāraṇaṃ paramam
taṃ bhagavantamanantaṃ dhyāyantaḥ svahṛdi kāraṇaṃ śāntam
saptānudhyāyantyapi mantrāṇāṃ koṭayaḥ śuddhāḥ
māyādiravīcyanto bhavastvanantādirucyate 'pyabhavaḥ
śivaśuddhaguṇādhīkārāntaḥ so 'pyeṣa heyaśca
atrāpi yato dṛṣṭānugrāhyāṇāṃ niyojyatā śaivī
iṣṭā ca tannivṛttirhyabhavastvadhare na bhūyate yasmāt
patyur apasarpati yataḥ kāraṇatā kāryatā ca siddhebhyaḥ
kañcukavacchivasiddhau tāvatibhavasaṃjñayātimadhyasthau
dharmajñānavirāgaiśyacatuṣṭayapuraṃ tu yat
rūpāvaraṇasaṃjñaṃ tattattve 'smin aiśvare viduḥ
vāmā jyeṣṭhā ca raudrīti bhuvanatrayaśobhitam
sūkṣmāvaraṇamākhyātamīśatattve gurūttamaiḥ
aiśātsādāśivaṃ jñānakriyāyugalamaṇḍitam
śuddhāvaraṇamityāhuruktā śuddhāvṛteḥ param
vidyāvṛtistato bhāvābhāvaśaktidvayojjvalā
śaktyāvṛtiḥ pramāṇākhyā tataḥ śāstre nirūpitā
śaktyāvṛtestu tejasvidhruveśābhyām alaṃkṛtam
tejasvyāvaraṇaṃ vedapurā mānāvṛtistataḥ
mānāvṛteḥ suśuddhāvṛtpuratritayaśobhitā
suśuddhāvaraṇādūrdhvaṃ śaivamekapuraṃ bhavet
śivāvṛterūrdhvamāhurmokṣāvaraṇasaṃjñitam
asyāṃ mokṣāvṛtau rudrā ekādaśa nirūpitāḥ
mokṣāvaraṇatastvekapuramāvaraṇaṃ dhruvam
ūrdhve dhruvāvṛtericchāvaraṇaṃ tatra te śivāḥ
īśvarecchāgṛhāntasthāstatpuraṃ caikamucyate
icchāvṛteḥ prabuddhākhyaṃ digrudrāṣṭakacarcitam
prabuddhāvaraṇādūrdhvaṃ samayāvaraṇaṃ mahat
bhuvanaiḥ pañcabhirgarbhīkṛtānantasamāvṛti
sāmayāt sauśivaṃ tatra sādākhyaṃ bhuvanaṃ mahat
tasminsadāśivo devastasya savyāpasavyayoḥ
jñānakriye parecchā tu śaktirutsaṅgagāminī
sṛṣṭyādipañcakṛtyāni kurute sa tayecchayā
pañca brahmāṇyaṅgaṣaṭkaṃ sakalādyaṣṭakaṃ śivāḥ
daśāṣṭādaśa rudrāśca taireva suśivo vṛtaḥ
sadyo vāmāghorau puruṣeśau brahmapañcakaṃ hṛdayam
mūrdhaśikhāvarmadṛgastramaṅgāni ṣaṭ prāhuḥ
sakalākalaśūnyaiḥ saha kalāḍhyakham alaṃkṛte kṣapaṇamantyam
kaṇṭhyauṣṭhyamaṣṭamaṃ kila sakalāṣṭakametadāmnātam
oṃ kāraśivau dīpto hetvīśadaśeśakau suśivakālau
sūkṣmasutejaḥśarvāḥ śivāḥ daśaite 'tra pūrvādeḥ
vijayo niḥśvāsaśca svāyambhuvo vahnivīrarauravakāḥ
mukuṭavisarendubinduprodgītā lalitasiddharudrau ca
santānaśivau parakiraṇapārameśā iti smṛtā rudrāḥ
sarveṣāmeteṣāṃ jñānāni viduḥ svatulyanāmāni
mantramunikoṭiparivṛtamatha vibhuvāmādirudratacchaktiyutam
tārādiśaktijuṣṭaṃ suśivāsanam atisitakajam asaṃkhyadalam
yaḥ śaktirudravargaḥ parivāre viṣṭare ca suśivasya
pratyekamasya nijanijaparivāre parārdhakoṭayo 'saṃkhyāḥ
māyāmalanirmuktāḥ kevalamadhikāramātrasaṃrūḍhāḥ
suśivāvaraṇe rudrāḥ sarvajñāḥ sarvaśaktisampūrṇāḥ
adhikārabandhavilaye śāntāḥ śivarūpiṇaḥ punarbhavinaḥ
ūrdhve bindvāvṛtirdīptā tatra tatra padmaṃ śaśiprabham
śāntyatītaḥ śivastatra tacchaktyutsaṅgabhūṣitaḥ
nivṛttyādikalāvargaparivārasamāvṛtaḥ
asaṃkhyarudratacchaktipurakoṭibhirāvṛtaḥ
śrīmanmataṅgaśāstre ca layākhyaṃ tattvamuttamam
pāribhāṣikamityetannāmnā bindurihocyate
caturmūrtimayaṃ śubhraṃ yattatsakalaniṣkalam
tasminbhogaḥ samuddiṣṭa ityatredaṃ ca varṇitam
nivṛttyādeḥ susūkṣmatvād dharādyārabdhadehatā
mātuḥ sphūrjanmahājñānalīnatvānna vibhāvyate
udriktataijasatvena hemno bhūparamāṇavaḥ
yathā pṛthaṅna bhāntyevamūrdhvādhorudradehagāḥ
bindūrdhve 'rdhenduretasya kalā jyotsnā ca tadvatī
kāntiḥ prabhā ca vimalā pañcaitā rodhikāstataḥ
rundhanī rodhanī roddhrī jñānabodhā tamopahā
etāḥ pañca kalāḥ prāhurnirodhinyāṃ gurūttamāḥ
ardhamātraḥ smṛto bindurvyomarūpī catuṣkalaḥ
tadardhamardhacandrastadaṣṭāṃśena nirodhikā
hetūnbrahmādikān runddhe rodhikāṃ tāṃ tyajettataḥ
nirodhikāmimāṃ bhittvā sādākhyaṃ bhuvanaṃ param
pararūpeṇa yatrāste pañcamantramahātanuḥ
ityardhendunirodhyantabindvāvṛtyūrdhvato mahān
nādaḥ kiñjalkasadṛśo mahadbhiḥ puruṣairvṛtaḥ
catvāri bhuvanānyatra dikṣu madhye ca pañcamam
indhikā dīpikā caiva rodhikā mocikordhvagā
madhye 'tra padmaṃ tatrordhvagāmī tacchaktibhirvṛtaḥ
nādordhvatastu sauṣumnaṃ tatra tacchaktibhṛtprabhuḥ
tadīśaḥ piṅgalelābhyāṃ vṛtaḥ savyāpasavyayoḥ
yā prabhoraṅkagā devī suṣumnā śaśisaprabhā
grathito 'dhvā tayā sarva ūrdhvaścādhastanastathā
nādaḥ suṣumnādhārastu bhittvā viśvamidaṃ jagat
adhaḥśaktyā vinirgacchedūrdhvaśaktyā ca mūrdhataḥ
nāḍyā brahmabile līnaḥ so 'vyaktadhvanirakṣaraḥ
nadansarveṣu bhūteṣu śivaśaktyā hyadhiṣṭhitaḥ
suṣumnordhve brahmabilasaṃjñayāvaraṇaṃ tridṛk
tatra brahmā sitaḥ śūlī pañcāsyaḥ śaśiśekharaḥ
tasyotsaṅge parā devī brahmāṇī mokṣamārgagā
roddhrī dātrī ca mokṣasya tāṃ bhittvā cordhvakuṇḍalī
śaktiḥ suptāhisadṛśī sā viśvādhāra ucyate
tasyāṃ sūkṣmā susūkṣmā ca tathānye amṛtāmite
madhyato vyāpinī tasyāṃ vyāpīśo vyāpinīdharaḥ
śaktitattvamidaṃ yasya prapañco 'yaṃ dharāntakaḥ
śivatattvaṃ tatastatra caturdikkaṃ vyavasthitāḥ
vyāpī vyomātmako 'nanto 'nāthastacchaktibhāginaḥ
madhye tvanāśritaṃ tatra devadevo hyanāśritaḥ
tacchaktyutsaṅgabhṛtsūryaśatakoṭisamaprabhaḥ
śivatattvordhvataḥ śaktiḥ parā sā samanāhvayā
sarveṣāṃ kāraṇānāṃ sā kartṛbhūtā vyavasthitā
bibhartyaṇḍānyanekāni śivena samadhiṣṭhitā
tadārūḍhaḥ śivaḥ kṛtyapañcakaṃ kurute prabhuḥ
samanā karaṇaṃ tasya hetukartur maheśituḥ
anāśritaṃ tu vyāpāre nimittaṃ heturucyate
tayādhitiṣṭhati vibhuḥ kāraṇānāṃ tu pañcakam
anāśrito 'nāthamayam anantaṃ khavapuḥ sadā
sa vyāpinaṃ prerayati svaśaktyā karaṇena tu
karmarūpā sthitā māyā yadadhaḥ śaktikuṇḍalī
nādabindvādikaṃ kāryamityādijagadudbhavaḥ
yatsadāśivaparyantaṃ pārthivādyaṃ ca śāsane
tatsarvaṃ prākṛtaṃ proktaṃ vināśotpattisaṃyutam
atha sakalabhuvanamānaṃ yanmahyaṃ nigaditaṃ nijairgurubhiḥ
tadvakṣyate samāsādbuddhau yenāśu saṃkrāmet
aṇḍasyāntaranantaḥ kālaḥ kūṣmāṇḍahāṭakau brahmaharī
rudrāḥ śataṃ savīraṃ bahirnivṛttistu sāṣṭaśatabhuvanā syāt
jalatejaḥsamīranabho'haṃkṛddhīmūlasaptake pratyekam
aṣṭau ṣaṭpañcāśadbhuvanā tena pratiṣṭheti kalā kathitā
atra prāhuḥ śodhyānaṣṭau kecinnijāṣṭakādhipatīn
anye tu samastānāṃ śodhyatvaṃ varṇayanti bhuvanānām
śrībhūtirājamiśrā guravaḥ prāhuḥ punarbahī rudraśatam
aṣṭāvantaḥ sākaṃ śarveṇetīdṛśī nivṛttiriyaṃ syāt
rudrāḥ kālī vīro dharābdhilakṣmyaḥ sarasvatī guhyam
ityaṣṭakaṃ jale 'gnau vahnyatiguhyadvayaṃ maruti vāyoḥ
svapuraṃ gayādi khe ca vyoma pavitrāṣṭakaṃ ca bhuvanayugam
abhimāne 'haṅkāracchagalādyaṣṭakamathāntarā nabho 'haṃkṛt
tanmātrārkenduśratipurāṣṭakaṃ buddhikarmadevānām
daśa tanmātrasamūhe bhuvanaṃ punarakṣavargavinipatite
manasaścetyabhimāne dvāviṃśatireva bhuvanānām
dhiyi daivīnāmaṣṭau kruttejoyogasaṃjñakaṃ trayaṃ tadumā
tatpatiratha mūrtyaṣṭakasuśivadvādaśakavīrabhadrāḥ syuḥ
tadatha mahādevāṣṭakamiti buddhau saptadaśa saṃkhyā
guṇatattve paṅktitrayamiti ṣaṭpañcāśataṃ purāṇi viduḥ
yadyapi guṇasāmyātmani mūle krodheśvarāṣṭakaṃ tathāpi dhiyi
tacchodhitamiti gaṇanāṃ na punaḥ prāptaṃ pratiṣṭhāyām
iti jalatattvānmūlaṃ tattvacaturviṃśatiḥ pratiṣṭhāyām
ambādituṣṭivargastārādyāḥ siddhayo 'ṇimādigaṇaḥ
guravo guruśiṣyā ṛṣivarga iḍādiśca vigrahāṣṭakayuk
gandhādivikārapuraṃ buddhiguṇāṣṭakamahaṃkriyā viṣayaguṇāḥ
kāmādisaptaviṃśakamāgantu tathā gaṇeśavidyeśamayau
iti pāśeṣu puratrayamitthaṃ puruṣe 'tra bhuvanaṣoḍaśakam
niyatau śaṅkaradaśakaṃ kāle śivadaśakamiti puradvitayam
rāge suhṛṣṭabhuvanaṃ guruśiṣyapuraṃ ca vitkalāyugale
bhuvanaṃ bhuvanaṃ niśi puṭapuratrayaṃ vākpuraṃ pramāṇapuram
iti saptaviṃśatipurā vidyā puruṣāditattvasaptakayuk
vāmeśarūpasūkṣmaṃ śuddhaṃ vidyātha śaktitejasvimitiḥ
suviśuddhiśivau mokṣadhuveṣisaṃbuddhasamayasauśivasaṃjñāḥ
saptadaśapurā śāntā vidyeśasadāśivapuratritayayuktā
bindvardhendunirodhyaḥ parasauśivamindhikādipurasauṣumne
paranādo brahmabilaṃ sūkṣmādiyutordhvakuṇḍalī śaktiḥ
vyāpivyomānantānāthānāśritapurāṇi pañca tataḥ
ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca paramamanāśritamatha samanābhuvanaṣoḍaśī yadi vā
bindvāvaraṇaṃ parasauśivaṃ ca pañcendhikādibhuvanāni
sauṣumnaṃ brahmabilaṃ kuṇḍalinī vyāpipañcakaṃ samanā
iti ṣoḍaśabhuvaneyaṃ tattvayugaṃ śāntyatītā syāt
śrīmanmataṅgaśāstre ca kramo 'yaṃ purapūgagaḥ
kālāgnirnarakāḥ khābdhiyutaṃ mukhyatayā śatam
kūṣmāṇḍaḥ saptapātālī saptalokī maheśvaraḥ
ityaṇḍamadhyaṃ tadbāhye śataṃ rudrā iti sthitāḥ
sthānānāṃ dviśatī bhūmiḥ saptapañcāśatā yutā
pañcāṣṭakasya madhyāddvātriṃśadbhūtacatuṣṭaye
tanmātreṣu ca pañca syurviśvedevāstato 'ṣṭakam
pañcamaṃ sendriye garve buddhau devāṣṭakaṃ guṇe
yogāṣṭakaṃ krodhasaṃjñaṃ mūle kāle sanaiyate
patadrugādyāścāṅguṣṭhamātrādyā rāgatattvagāḥ
dvādaśaikaśivādyāḥ syurvidyāyāṃ kalane daśa
vāmādyāstriśatī seyaṃ triparvaṇyabdhirasyayuk
śaivāḥ kecidihānantāḥ śraikaṇṭhā iti saṃgrahaḥ
yatra yadā parabhogān bubhukṣate tatra yojanaṃ kāryam
śodhanamatha taddhānau śeṣaṃ tvantargataṃ kāryam
ityāgamaṃ prathayituṃ darśitametadvikalpitaṃ tena
anye 'pi bahuvikalpāḥ svadhiyācāryaiḥ samabhyūhyāḥ
śrīpūrvaśāsane punaraṣṭādaśādhikaṃ śataṃ kathitam
tadiha pradhānamadhikaṃ saṃkṣepeṇocyate śodhyam
kālāgniḥ kūṣmāṇḍo narakeśo hāṭako 'tha bhūtalapaḥ
brahmā munilokeśo rudrāḥ pañcāntarālasthāḥ
adhare 'nantaḥ prācyāḥ kapālivahnyantanirṛtibalākhyāḥ
laghunidhipatividyādhipaśambhūrdhvāntaṃ savīrabhadrapati
ekādaśabhirbāhye brahmāṇḍaṃ pañcabhis tathāntarikaiḥ
iti ṣoḍaśapurametannivṛttikalayeha kalanīyam
lakulīśabhārabhūtī diṇḍyāṣāḍhī ca puṣkaranimeṣau
prabhāsasureśāviti salile pratyātmakaṃ saparivāre
bhairavakedāramahākālā madhyāmrajalpākhyāḥ
śrīśailahariścandrāviti guhyāṣṭakamidaṃ mahasi
bhīmendrāṭṭahāsavimalakanakhalanākhalakurusthitigayākhyāḥ
atiguhyāṣṭakametanmaruti ca satanmātrake ca sākṣe ca
sthāṇusuvarṇākhyau kila bhadro gokarṇako mahālayakaḥ
avimuktarudrakoṭī vastrāpada ityadaḥ pavitraṃ khe
sthūlasthūleśaśaṅkuśrutikālañjarāśca maṇḍalabhṛt
mākoṭāṇḍadvitayacchagalāṇḍā aṣṭakaṃ hyahaṅkāre
anye 'haṅkārāntastanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi cāpyāhuḥ
dhiyi yonyaṣṭakamuktaṃ prakṛtau yogāṣṭakaṃ kilākṛtaprabhṛti
iti saptāṣṭakabhuvanā pratiṣṭhitiḥ salilato hi mūlāntā
nari vāmo bhīmograu bhaveśavīrāḥ pracaṇḍagaurīśau
ajasānantaikaśivau vidyāyāṃ krodhacaṇḍayugmaṃ syāt
saṃvarto jyotiratho kalāniyatyāṃ ca sūrapañcāntau
vīraśikhīśaśrīkaṇṭhasaṃjñametattrayaṃ ca kāle syāt
samahātejā vāmo bhavodbhavaścaikapiṅgaleśānau
bhuvaneśapuraḥsarakāvaṅguṣṭha ime niśi sthitā hyaṣṭau
aṣṭāviṃśatibhuvanā vidyā puruṣānniśāntamiyam
hālāhalarudrakrudambikāghorikāḥ savāmāḥ syuḥ
vidyāyāṃ vidyeśāstvaṣṭāvīśe sadāśive pañca
vāmā jyeṣṭhā raudrī śaktiḥ sakalā ca śontayam
aṣṭādaśa bhuvanā syāt śāntyatītā tvabhuvanaiva
iti deśādhvavibhāgaḥ kathitaḥ śrīśambhunā samādiṣṭaḥ
atha tattvapravibhāgo vistarataḥ kathyate kramaprāptaḥ
yānyuktāni purāṇyamūni vividhair bhedair yadeṣvanvitaṃ rūpaṃ bhāti paraṃ prakāśaniviḍaṃ devaḥ sa ekaḥ śivaḥ
tatsvātantryarasātpunaḥ śivapadādbhede vibhāte paraṃ yadrūpaṃ bahudhānugāmi tadidaṃ tattvaṃ vibhoḥ śāsane
tathāhi kālasadanādvīrabhadrapurāntagam
dhṛtikāṭhinyagarimādyavabhāsāddharātmatā
evaṃ jalāditattveṣu vācyaṃ yāvatsadāśive
svasminkārye 'tha dharmaughe yadvāpi svasadṛgguṇe
āste sāmānyakalpena tananād vyāptṛbhāvataḥ
tattattvaṃ kramaśaḥ pṛthvīpradhānaṃ puṃśivādayaḥ
dehānāṃ bhuvanānāṃ ca na prasaṅgastato bhavet
śrīmanmataṅgaśāstrādau taduktaṃ parameśinā
tatraiṣāṃ darśyate dṛṣṭaḥ siddhayogīśvarīmate
kāryakāraṇabhāvo yaḥ śivecchāparikalpitaḥ
vastutaḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ karteśānaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ
asvatantrasya kartṛtvaṃ nahi jātūpapadyate
svatantratā ca cinmātravapuṣaḥ parameśituḥ
svatantraṃ ca jaḍaṃ ceti tadanyonyaṃ virudhyate
jāḍyaṃ pramātṛtantratvaṃ svātmasiddhimapi prati
na kartṛtvādṛte cānyat kāraṇatvaṃ hi labhyate
tasminsati hi tadbhāva ityapekṣaikajīvitam
nirapekṣeṣu bhāveṣu svātmaniṣṭhatayā katham
sa pūrvamatha paścātsa iti cetpūrvapaścimau
svabhāve 'natiriktau cetsama ityavaśiṣyate
bījamaṅkura ityasmin satattve hetutadvatoḥ
ghaṭaḥ paṭaśceti bhavet kāryakāraṇatā na kim
bījamaṅkurapatrāditayā pariṇameta cet
atatsvabhāvavapuṣaḥ sa svabhāvo na yujyate
sa tatsvabhāva iti cet tarhi bījāṅkurā nije
tāvatyeva na viśrāntau tadanyātyantasaṃbhavāt
tataśca citrākāro 'sau tāvānkaścitprasajyate
astu cet na jaḍe 'nyonyaviruddhākārasaṃbhavaḥ
krameṇa citrākāro 'stu jaḍaḥ kiṃ nu virudhyate
kramo 'kramo vā bhāvasya na svarūpādhiko bhavet
tathopalambhamātraṃ tau upalambhaśca kiṃ tathā
upalabdhāpi vijñānasvabhāvo yo 'sya so 'pi hi
kramopalambharūpatvāt krameṇopalabheta cet
tasya tarhi kramaḥ ko 'sau tadanyānupalambhataḥ
svabhāva iti cennāsau svarūpādadhiko bhavet
svarūpānadhikasyāpi kramasya svasvabhāvataḥ
svātantryādbhāsanaṃ syāccet kimanyadbrūmahe vayam
itthaṃ śrīśiva evaikaḥ karteti paribhāṣyate
kartṛtvaṃ caitadetasya tathāmātrāvabhāsanam
tathāvabhāsanaṃ cāsti kāryakāraṇabhāvagam
yathā hi ghaṭasāhityaṃ paṭasyāpyavabhāsate
tathā ghaṭānantaratā kiṃ tu sā niyamojjhitā
ato yanniyamenaiva yasmādābhātyanantaram
tattasya kāraṇaṃ brūmaḥ sati rūpānvaye 'dhike
niyamaśca tathārūpabhāsanāmātrasārakaḥ
bījādaṅkura ityevaṃ bhāsanaṃ nahi sarvadā
yogīcchānantarodbhūtatathābhūtāṅkuro yataḥ
iṣṭe tathāvidhākāre niyamo bhāsate yataḥ
svapne ghaṭapaṭādīnāṃ hetutadvatsvabhāvatā
bhāsate niyamenaiva bādhāśūnyena tāvati
tato yāvati yādrūpyānniyamo bādhavarjitaḥ
bhāti tāvati tādrūpyāddṛḍhahetuphalātmatā
tathābhūte ca niyame hetutadvattvakāriṇi
vastutaścinmayasyaiva hetutā taddhi sarvagam
ata eva ghaṭodbhūtau sāmagrī heturucyate
sāmagrī ca samagrāṇāṃ yadyekaṃ neṣyate vapuḥ
hetubhedānna bhedaḥ syāt phale taccāsamañjasam
yadyasyānuvidhatte tāmanvayavyatirekitām
tattasya hetu cetso 'yaṃ kuṇṭhatarko na naḥ priyaḥ
samagrāśca yathā daṇḍasūtracakrakarādayaḥ
dūrāśca bhāvinaścetthaṃ hetutveneti manmahe
yadi tatra bhavenmerurbhaviṣyanvāpi kaścana
na jāyeta ghaṭo nūnaṃ tatpratyūhavyapohitaḥ
yathā ca cakraṃ niyate deśe kāle ca hetutām
yāti karkisumervādyāstadvatsvasthāvadhi sthitāḥ
tathā ca teṣāṃ hetūnāṃ saṃyojanaviyojane
niyate śiva evaikaḥ svatantraḥ kartṛtāmiyāt
kumbhakārasya yā saṃvit cakradaṇḍādiyojane
śiva eva hi sā yasmāt saṃvidaḥ kā viśiṣṭatā
kaumbhakārī tu saṃvittiravacchedāvabhāsanāt
bhinnakalpā yadi kṣepyā daṇḍacakrādimadhyataḥ
tasmādekaikanirmāṇe śivo viśvaikavigrahaḥ
karteti puṃsaḥ kartṛtvābhimāno 'pi vibhoḥ kṛtiḥ
ata eva tathābhānaparamārthatayā sthiteḥ
kāryakāraṇabhāvasya loke śāstre ca citratā
māyāto 'vyaktakalayoriti rauravasaṃgrahe
kalādhvā vakṣyate śrīmacchāṃbhavājñānusārataḥ
yathā pūrvoktabhuvanamadhye nijanijaṃ gaṇam
anuyatparato bhinnaṃ tattvaṃ nāmeti bhaṇyate
tathā teṣvapi tattveṣu svavarge 'nugamātmakam
vyāvṛttaṃ paravargācca kaleti śivaśāsane
kecidāhuḥ punaryāsau śaktirantaḥ susūkṣmikā
tattvānāṃ sā kaletyuktā dharaṇyāṃ dhārikā yathā
atra pakṣadvaye vastu na bhinnaṃ bhāsate yataḥ
anugāmi na sāmānyamiṣṭaṃ naiyāyikādivat
anye vadanti dīkṣādau sukhasaṃgrahaṇārthataḥ
śivena kalpito vargaḥ kaleti samayāśrayaḥ
kṛtaśca devadevena samayo 'paramārthatām
na gacchatīti nāsatyo na cānyasamayodayaḥ
nivṛttiḥ pṛthivītattve pratiṣṭhāvyaktagocare
vidyā niśānte śāntā ca śaktyante 'ṇḍamidaṃ catuḥ
śāntātītā śive tattve kalātītaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ
nahyatra vargīkaraṇaṃ samayaḥ kalanāpi vā
yujyate sarvatodikkaṃ svātantryollāsadhāmani
svātantryāttu nijaṃ rūpaṃ boddhṛdharmādavicyutam
upadeśatadāveśaparamārthatvasiddhaye
bodhyatāmānayandevaḥ sphuṭameva vibhāvyate
yato 'taḥ śivatattve 'pi kalāsaṃgatirucyate
aṇḍaṃ ca nāma bhuvanavibhāgasthitikāraṇam
prāhurāvaraṇaṃ tacca śaktyantaṃ yāvadasti hi
yadyapi prāk śivākhye 'pi tattve bhuvanapaddhatiḥ
uktā tathāpyapratighe nāsmin āvṛtisaṃbhavaḥ
nanvevaṃ dharaṇīṃ muktvā śaktau prakṛtimāyayoḥ
api cāpratighatve 'pi kathamaṇḍasya saṃbhavaḥ
atrāsmadguravaḥ prāhuryatpṛthivyādipañcakam
pratyakṣamidamābhāti tato 'nyannāsti kiṃcana
meyatve sthūlasūkṣmatvānmānatve karaṇatvataḥ
kartṛtollāsataḥ kartṛbhāve sphuṭatayoditam
triṃśattattvaṃ vibhedātma tadabhedo niśā matā
kāryatvakaraṇatvādivibhāgagalane sati
vikāsotkasvatantratve śivāntaṃ pañcakaṃ jaguḥ
śrīmatkālottarādau ca kathitaṃ bhūyasā tathā
pañcaitāni tu tattvāni yairvyāptamakhilaṃ jagat
pañcamantratanau tena sadyojātādi bhaṇyate
īśānāntaṃ tatra tatra dharādigaganāntakam
śivatattvamataḥ śūnyātiśūnyaṃ syādanāśritam
yattu sarvāvibhāgātma svatantraṃ bodhasundaram
saptatriṃśaṃ tu tatprāhustattvaṃ paraśivābhidham
tasyāpyuktanayādvedyabhāve 'tra parikalpite
yadāste hyanavacchinnaṃ tadaṣṭātriṃśamucyate
na cānavasthā hyevaṃ syāddṛśyatāṃ hi mahātmabhiḥ
yadvedyaṃ kiṃcidābhāti tatkṣaye yatprakāśate
tattattvamiti nirṇītaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśaṃ hṛdi bhāsate
tatkiṃ na kiṃcidvā kiṃcidityākāṅkṣāvaśe vapuḥ
cidānandasvatantraikarūpaṃ taditi deśane
saptatriṃśaṃ samābhāti tatrākāṅkṣā ca nāparā
taccāpi kﾱptavedyatvaṃ yatra bhāti sa cinmayaḥ
aṣṭātriṃśattamaḥ so 'pi bhāvanāyopadiśyate
yadi nāma tataḥ saptatriṃśa eva punarbhavet
avibhāgasvatantratvacinmayatvādidharmatā
samaiva vedyīkaraṇaṃ kevalaṃ tvadhikaṃ yataḥ
dharāyāṃ guṇatattvānte māyānte kramaśaḥ sthitāḥ
gandho raso rūpamantaḥ sūkṣmabhāvakrameṇa tu
iti sthite naye śaktitattvānte 'pyasti saukṣmyabhāk
sparśaḥ ko 'pi sadā yasmai yoginaḥ spṛhayālavaḥ
tatsparśānte tu saṃvittiḥ śuddhacidvyomarūpiṇī
yasyāṃ rūḍhaḥ samabhyeti svaprakāśātmikāṃ parām
ato bindurato nādo rūpamasmādato rasaḥ
ityuktaṃ kṣobhakatvena spande sparśastu no tathā
mataṃ caitanmaheśasya śrīpūrve yadabhāṣata
dhārikāpyāyinī boddhrī pavitrī cāvakāśadā
ebhiḥ śabdairvyavaharan nivṛttyādernijaṃ vapuḥ
pañcatattvavidhiḥ proktastritattvamadhunocyate
vijñānākalaparyantamātmā vidyeśvarāntakam
śeṣe śivastritattve syādekatattve śivaḥ param
imau bhedāvubhau tattvabhedamātrakṛtāviti
tattvādhvaivāyamitthaṃ ca na ṣaḍadhvasthiteḥ kṣatiḥ
prakṛt pumānyatiḥ kālo māyā vidyeśasauśivau
śivaśca navatattve 'pi vidhau tattvādhvarūpatā
evamaṣṭādaśākhye 'pi vidhau nyāyaṃ vadetsudhīḥ
yatra yatra hi bhogecchā tatprādhānyopayogataḥ
anyāntarbhāvanātaśca dīkṣānantavibhedabhāk
tena ṣaṭtriṃśato yāvadekatattvavidhirbhavet
tattvādhvaiva sa devena prokto vyāsasamāsataḥ
ekatattvavidhiścaiṣa suprabuddhaṃ guruṃ prati
śiṣyaṃ ca gatabhogāśamuditaḥ śaṃbhunā yataḥ
bhedaṃ visphārya visphārya śaktyā svacchandarūpayā
svātmanyabhinne bhagavānnityaṃ viśramayan sthitaḥ
itthaṃ tryātmādhvano bhedaḥ sthūlasūkṣmaparatvataḥ
meyabhāgagataḥ proktaḥ puratattvakalātmakaḥ
adhunā mātṛbhāgasthaṃ rūpaṃ tredhā nirūpyate
yatpramāṇātmakaṃ rūpamadhvano mātṛbhāgagam
padaṃ hyavagamātmatvasamāveśāt tad ucyate
tadeva ca padaṃ mantraḥ prakṣobhātpracyutaṃ yadā
guptabhāṣī yato mātā tūṣṇīṃbhūto vyavasthitaḥ
tathāpi na vimarśātma rūpaṃ tyajati tena saḥ
pramāṇātmavimarśātmā mānavatkṣobhabhāṅnatu
mantrāṇāṃ ca padānāṃ ca tenoktaṃ trikaśāsane
abhinnameva svaṃ rūpaṃ niḥspandakṣobhite param
audāsīnyaparityāge prakṣobhānavarohaṇe
varṇādhvā mātṛbhāge syāt pūrvaṃ yā kathitā pramā
sā tu pūrṇasvarūpatvādavibhāgamayī yataḥ
tata ekaikavarṇatvaṃ tattve tattve kṣamāditaḥ
kṛtvā śaive pare proktāḥ ṣoḍaśārṇā visargataḥ
tatra śaktiparispandastāvān prāk ca nirūpitaḥ
saṃkalayyocyate sarvamadhunā sukhasaṃvide
padamantravarṇamekaṃ puraṣoḍaśakaṃ dhareti ca nivṛttiḥ
tattvārṇamagninayanaṃ rasaśarapuramastramantrapadamanyā
munitattvārṇaṃ dvikapadamantraṃ vasvakṣibhuvanamaparakalā
agnyarṇatattvamekakapadamantraṃ sainyabhuvanamiti turyā
ṣoḍaśa varṇāḥ padamantratattvamekaṃ ca śāntyatīteyam
abhinavaguptenāryātrayamuktaṃ saṃgrahāya śiṣyebhyaḥ
so 'yaṃ samasta evādhvā bhairavābhedavṛttimān
tatsvātantryātsvatantratvamaśnuvāno 'vabhāsate
tathāhi mātṛrūpastho mantrādhveti nirūpitaḥ
tathāhi cidvimarśena grastā vācyadaśā yadā
śivajñānakriyāyattamananatrāṇatatparā
aśeṣaśaktipaṭalīlīlālāmpaṭyapāṭavāt
cyutā mānamayādrūpāt saṃvinmantrādhvatāṃ gatā
pramāṇarūpatāmetya prayātyadhvā padātmatām
tathā hi māturviśrāntirvarṇānsaṃghaṭya tānbahūn
saṃghaṭṭanaṃ ca kramikaṃ saṃjalpātmakameva tat
vikalpasya svakaṃ rūpaṃ bhogāveśamayaṃ sphuṭam
ataḥ pramāṇatārūpaṃ padamasmadgururjagau
pramāṇarūpatāveśam aparityajya meyatām
gacchankalanayā yogādadhvā proktaḥ kalātmakaḥ
śuddhe prameyatāyoge sūkṣmasthūlatvabhāgini
tattvādhvabhuvanādhvatve krameṇānusaredguruḥ
prameyamānamātṝṇāṃ yadrūpamupari sthitam
pramātmātra sthito 'dhvāyaṃ varṇātmā dṛśyatāṃ kila
ucchalatsaṃvidāmātraviśrāntyāsvādayoginaḥ
sarvābhidhānasāmarthyād aniyantritaśaktayaḥ
sṛṣṭāḥ svātmasahotthe 'rthe dharāparyantabhāgini
āmṛśantaḥ svacidbhūmau tāvato 'rthānabhedataḥ
varṇaughāste pramārūpāṃ satyāṃ bibhrati saṃvidam
bālāstiryakpramātāro ye 'py asaṃketabhāginaḥ
te 'pyakṛtrimasaṃskārasārāmenāṃ svasaṃvidam
bhinnabhinnāmupāśritya yānti citrāṃ pramātṛtām
asyāṃ cākṛtrimānantavarṇasaṃvidi rūḍhatām
saṃketā yānti cette 'pi yāntyasaṃketavṛttitām
anayā tu vinā sarve saṃketā bahuśaḥ kṛtāḥ
aviśrāntatayā kuryuranavasthāṃ duruttarām
bālo vyutpādyate yena tatra saṃketamārgaṇāt
aṅgulyādeśane 'pyasya nāvikalpā tathā matiḥ
vikalpaḥ śabdamūlaśca śabdaḥ saṃketajīvitaḥ
tenānanto hyamāyīyo yo varṇagrāma īdṛśaḥ
saṃvidvimarśasacivaḥ sadaiva sa hi jṛmbhate
yata eva ca māyīyā varṇāḥ sūtiṃ vitenire
ye ca māyīyavarṇeṣu vīryatvena nirūpitāḥ
saṃketanirapekṣāste prameti parigṛhyatām
tathā hi paravākyeṣu śruteṣvāvriyate nijā
pramā yasya jaḍo 'sau no tatrārthe 'bhyeti mātṛtām
śukavatsa paṭhatyeva paraṃ tatkramitaikabhāk
svātantryalābhataḥ svavākyapramālābhe tu boddhṛtā
yasya hi svapramābodho vipakṣodbhedanigrahāt
vākyādivarṇapuñje sve sa pramātā vaśībhavet
yathā yathā cākṛtakaṃ tadrūpamatiricyate
tathā tathā camatkāratāratamyaṃ vibhāvyate
ādyāmāyīyavarṇāntarnimagne cottarottare
saṃkete pūrvapūrvāṃśamajjane pratibhābhidaḥ
ādyodrekamahattve 'pi pratibhātmani niṣṭhitāḥ
dhruvaṃ kavitvavaktṛtvaśālitāṃ yānti sarvataḥ
yāvaddhāmani saṃketanikārakalanojjhite
viśrāntaścinmaye kiṃ kiṃ na vetti kurute na vā
ata eva hi vāksiddhau varṇānāṃ samupāsyatā
sarvajñatvādisiddhau vā kā siddhiryā na tanmayī
taduktaṃ varadena śrīsiddhayogīśvarīmate
tena guptena guptāste śeṣā varṇāstviti sphuṭam
evaṃ māmātṛmānatvameyatvair yo 'vabhāsate
ṣaḍvidhaḥ svavapuḥśuddhau śuddhiṃ so 'dhvādhigacchati
ekena vapuṣā śuddhau tatraivānyaprakāratām
antarbhāvyācarecchuddhimanusaṃdhānavān guruḥ
anantarbhāvaśaktau tu sūkṣmaṃ sūkṣmaṃ tu śodhayet
tadviśuddhaṃ bījabhāvāt sūte nottarasaṃtatim
śodhanaṃ bahudhā tattadbhogaprāptyekatānatā
tadādhipatyaṃ tattyāgastacchivātmatvavedanam
tallīnatā tannirāsaḥ sarvaṃ caitatkramākramāt
ata eva ca te mantrāḥ śodhakāścitrarūpiṇaḥ
siddhāntavāmadakṣādau citrāṃ śuddhiṃ vitanvate
anuttaratrikānāmakramamantrāstu ye kila
te sarve sarvadāḥ kintu kasyacit kvāpi mukhyatā
ataḥ śodhakabhāvena śāstre śrīpūrvasaṃjñite
parāparādimantrāṇāmadhvanyuktā vyavasthitiḥ
śodhakatvaṃ ca mālinyā devīnāṃ tritayasya ca
devatrayasya vaktrāṇāmaṅgānāmaṣṭakasya ca
kiṃ vātibahunā dvāravāstvādhāragurukrame
lokapāstravidhau mantrān muktvā sarvaṃ viśodhakam
yaccaitadadhvanaḥ proktaṃ śodhyatvaṃ śoddhṛtā ca yā
sā svātantryācchivābhede yuktetyuktaṃ ca śāsane
sarvametadvibhātyeva parameśitari dhruve
pratibimbasvarūpeṇa na tu bāhyatayā yataḥ
cidvyomnyeva śive tattaddehādimatirīdṛśī
bhinnā saṃsāriṇāṃ rajjau sarpasragvīcibuddhivat
yataḥ prāgdehamaraṇasiddhāntaḥ svapnagocaraḥ
dehāntarādirmaraṇe kīdṛgvā dehasaṃbhavaḥ
svapne 'pi pratibhāmātrasāmānyaprathanābalāt
viśeṣāḥ pratibhāsante na bhāvyante 'pi te yathā
śālagrāmopalāḥ keciccitrākṛtibhṛto yathā
tathā māyādibhūmyantalekhācitrahṛdaścitaḥ
nagarārṇavaśailādyās tadicchānuvidhāyinaḥ
na svayaṃ sadasanto no kāraṇākāraṇātmakāḥ
niyateścirarūḍhāyāḥ samucchedātpravartanāt
arūḍhāyāḥ svatantro 'yaṃ sthitaścidvyomabhairavaḥ
ekacinmātrasampūrṇabhairavābhedabhāgini
evamasmīty anāmarśo bhedako bhāvamaṇḍale
sarvapramāṇairno siddhaṃ svapne kartrantaraṃ yathā
svasaṃvidaḥ svasiddhāyāstathā sarvatra budhyatām
cittacitrapurodyāne krīḍedevaṃ hi vetti yaḥ
ahameva sthito bhūtabhāvatattvapurairiti
evaṃ jāto mṛto 'smīti janmamṛtyuvicitratāḥ
ajanmanyamṛtau bhānti cittabhittau svanirmitāḥ
parehasaṃvidāmātraṃ paralokehalokate
vastutaḥ saṃvido deśaḥ kālo vā naiva kiṃcana
abhaviṣyadayaṃ sargo mūrtaścenna tu cinmayaḥ
tad avekṣyata tanmadhyāt kenaiko 'pi dharādharaḥ
bhūtatanmātravargāder ādhārādheyatākrame
ante saṃvinmayī śaktiḥ śivarūpaiva dhāriṇī
tasmātpratītirevetthaṃ kartrī dhartrī ca sā śivaḥ
tato bhāvāstatra bhāvāḥ śaktirādhārikā tataḥ
sāṃkalpikaṃ nirādhāramapi naiva patatyadhaḥ
svādhāraśaktau viśrāntaṃ viśvamitthaṃ vimṛśyatām
asyā ghanāham ityādirūḍhireva dharāditā
yāvadante cidasmīti nirvṛttā bhairavātmatā
maṇāvindrāyudhe bhāsa iva nīlādayaḥ śive
paramārthata eṣāṃ tu nodayo na vyayaḥ kvacit
deśe kāle 'tra vā sṛṣṭirityetadasamañjasam
cidātmanā hi devena sṛṣṭir dikkālayor api
jāgarābhimate sārdhahastatritayagocare
prahare ca pṛthak svapnāś citradikkālamāninaḥ
ata eva kṣaṇaṃ nāma na kiṃcidapi manmahe
kriyākṣaṇe vāpyekasmin bahvyaḥ saṃsyurdrutāḥ kriyāḥ
tena ye bhāvasaṃkocaṃ kṣaṇāntaṃ pratipedire
te nūnam enayā nāḍyā śūnyadṛṣṭyavalambinaḥ
tadya eṣa sato bhāvāñ śūnyīkartuṃ tathāsataḥ
sphuṭīkartuṃ svatantratvādīśaḥ so 'smatprabhuḥ śivaḥ
taditthaṃ parameśāno viśvarūpaḥ pragīyate
na tu bhinnasya kasyāpi dharāderupapannatā
uktaṃ caitatpuraiveti na bhūyaḥ pravivicyate
bhūyobhiścāpi bāhyārthadūṣaṇaiḥ pravyaramyata
taditthameṣa nirṇītaḥ kalādervistaro 'dhvanaḥ
athādhvano 'sya prakṛta upayogaḥ prakāśyate
itthamadhvā samasto 'yaṃ yathā saṃvidi saṃsthitaḥ
taddvārā śūnyadhīprāṇanāḍīcakratanuṣvatho
bahiśca liṅgamūrtyagnisthaṇḍilādiṣu sarvataḥ
tathā sthitaḥ samastaśca vyastaścaiṣa kramākramāt
āsaṃvittattvam ābāhyaṃ yo 'yamadhvā vyavasthitaḥ
tatra tatrocitaṃ rūpaṃ svaṃ svātantryeṇa bhāsayet
sarvaṃ sarvatra rūpaṃ ca tasyāpi na na bhāsate
nahyavaccheditāṃ kvāpi svapne 'pi viṣahāmahe
evaṃ viśvādhvasampūrṇaṃ kālavyāpāracitritam
deśakālamayaspandasadma dehaṃ vilokayet
tathā vilokyamāno 'sau viśvāntardevatāmayaḥ
dhyeyaḥ pūjyaśca tarpyaśca tadāviṣṭo vimucyate
itthaṃ ghaṭaṃ paṭaṃ liṅgaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ pustakaṃ jalam
yadvā kiṃcitkvacitpaśyettatra tanmayatāṃ vrajet
tatrārpaṇaṃ hi vastūnāmabhedenārcanaṃ matam
tathā sampūrṇarūpatvānusaṃdhir dhyānamucyate
sampūrṇatvānusaṃdhānam akampaṃ dārḍhyamānayan
tathāntarjalpayogena vimṛśañjapabhājanam
tatrārpitānāṃ bhāvānāṃ svakabhedavilāpanam
kurvaṃstadraśmisadbhāvaṃ dadyāddhomakriyāparaḥ
tathaivaṃ kurvataḥ sarvaṃ samabhāvena paśyataḥ
niṣkampatā vrataṃ śuddhaṃ sāmyaṃ nandiśikhoditam
tathārcanajapadhyānahomavratavidhikramāt
paripūrṇāṃ sthitiṃ prāhuḥ samādhiṃ guravaḥ purā
atra pūjājapādyeṣu bahirantardvayasthitau
dravyaughe na vidhiḥ ko 'pi na kāpi pratiṣiddhatā
kalpanāśuddhisaṃdhyādernopayogo 'tra kaścana
uktaṃ śrītrikasūtre ca jāyate yajanaṃ prati
avidhijño vidhijñaś cety evamādi suvistaram
yadā yathā yena yatra svā saṃvittiḥ prasīdati
tadā tathā tena tatra tattadbhogyaṃ vidhiśca saḥ
laukikālaukikaṃ sarvaṃ tenātra viniyojayet
niṣkampatve sakampastu kampaṃ nirhrāsayedbalāt
yathā yenābhyupāyena kramādakramato 'pi vā
vicikitsā galatyantastathāsau yatnavānbhavet
dhīkarmākṣagatā devīrniṣiddhaireva tarpayet
vīravrataṃ cābhinandediti bhargaśikhāvacaḥ
tathāhi śaṅkā mālinyaṃ glāniḥ saṃkoca ityadaḥ
saṃsārakārāgārāntaḥ sthūlasthūṇāghaṭāyate
mantrā varṇasvabhāvā ye dravyaṃ yatpāñcabhautikam
yaccidātma prāṇijātaṃ tatra kaḥ saṃkaraḥ katham
saṃkarābhāvataḥ keyaṃ śaṅkā tasyāmapi sphuṭam
na śaṅketa tathā śaṅkā vilīyetāvahelayā
śrīsarvācāravīrālīniśācarakramādiṣu
śāstreṣu vitataṃ caitattatra tatrocyate yataḥ
śaṅkayā jāyate glāniḥ śaṅkayā vighnabhājanam
uvācotpaladevaśca śrīmānasmadgurorguruḥ
sarvāśaṅkāśaniṃ mārgaṃ numo māheśvaraṃ tviti
anuttarapadāptaye tadidamāṇavaṃ darśitābhyupāyamativistarānnanu vidāṃkurudhvaṃ budhāḥ
atha putrakatvasiddhyai nirūpyate śivanirūpito 'tra vidhiḥ
yadā tu samayasthasya putrakatve niyojanam
gurutve sādhakatve vā kartumicchati daiśikaḥ
tadādhivāsaṃ kṛtvāhni dvitīye maṇḍalaṃ likhet
sāmudāyikayāge 'tha tathānyatra yathoditam
ṣaḍaṣṭataddviguṇitacaturviṃśatisaṃkhyayā
cakrapañcakamākhyātaṃ śāstre śrīpūrvasaṃjñite
dvātriṃśattaddviguṇitaṃ śrīmattraiśirase mate
asaṃkhyacakrasaṃbandhaḥ śrīsiddhādau nirūpitaḥ
tasmādyathātathā yāgaṃ yāvaccakreṇa saṃmitam
pūjayedyena tenātra triśūlatrayamālikhet
triśūlatritaye devītrayaṃ paryāyavṛttitaḥ
madhyasavyānyabhedena pūrṇaṃ sampūjitaṃ bhavet
vartanā maṇḍalasyāgre saṃkṣepādupadekṣyate
ālikhya maṇḍalaṃ gandhavastreṇaivāsya mārjanam
kṛtvā snāto guruḥ prāgvanmaṇḍalāgre 'tra devatāḥ
bāhyagāḥ pūjayeddvāradeśe ca dvāradevatāḥ
maṇḍalasya purobhāge tadaiśānadiśaḥ kramāt
āgneyyantaṃ gaṇeśādīn kṣetrapāntānprapūjayet
gaṇapatiguruparamākhyāḥ parameṣṭhī pūrvasiddhavākkṣetrapatiḥ
iti saptakamākhyātaṃ gurupaṅktividhau prapūjyamasmadgurubhiḥ
tata ājñāṃ gṛhītvā tu puṣpadhūpādipūjitam
pūjyamādhāraśaktyādi śūlamūlātprabhṛtyalam
śivāntaṃ sitapadmānte triśūlānāṃ traye kramāt
madhyaśūle madhyagaḥ syātsadbhāvaḥ parayā saha
vāme cāparayā sākaṃ navātmā dakṣagaṃ param
triśūle dakṣiṇe madhyaśṛṅgastho ratiśekharaḥ
syātparāparayā sākaṃ dakṣe bhairavasatpare
vāme triśūle madhyastho navātmāparayā saha
syātpare parayā sākaṃ vāmāre saṃśca bhairavaḥ
itthaṃ sarvagatatve śrīparādevyāḥ sthite sati
yāgo bhavet susampūrṇastadadhiṣṭhānamātrataḥ
ekaśūle 'pyato yāge cintayettadadhiṣṭhitam
avidhijño vidhānajña ityevaṃ trīśikoditam
tato madhye tathā dakṣe vāme śṛṅge ca sarvataḥ
lokapālāstraparyantamekātmatvena pūjayet
paratvena ca sarvāsāṃ devatānāṃ prapūjayet
śrīmantaṃ mātṛsadbhāvabhaṭṭārakamanāmayam
tato 'pi bhogayāgena vidyāṅgaṃ bhairavāṣṭakam
yāmalaṃ cakradevīśca svasthāne pūjayedbahiḥ
lokapālānastrayutāngandhapuṣpāsavādibhiḥ
pūjayetparayā bhaktyā vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ
tataḥ kumbhāstrakalaśīmaṇḍalasthānalātmanām
pañcānāmanusandhānaṃ kuryādadvayabhāvanāt
ye tu tāmadvayavyāptiṃ na vindanti śivātmikām
mantranāḍīprayogeṇa te viśantyadvaye pathi
svadakṣiṇena niḥsṛtya maṇḍalasthasya vāmataḥ
praviśyānyena niḥsṛtya kumbhasthe karkarīgate
vahnisthe ca krameṇetthaṃ yāvatsvasminsvavāmataḥ
mūlānusandhānabalāt prāṇatantūmbhane sati
itthamaikyasphurattātmā vyāptisaṃvitprakāśate
tato viśeṣapūjāṃ ca kuryādadvayabhāvitām
yacchivādvayapīyūṣasaṃsiktaṃ paramaṃ hi tat
tenārghapuṣpagandhāderāsavasya paśoratha
yā śivādvayatādṛṣṭiḥ sā śuddhiḥ paramīkṛtiḥ
nivedayedvibhoragre jīvāndhātūṃstadutthitān
siddhānasiddhānvyāmiśrān yadvā kiṃciccarācaram
dṛṣṭaprokṣitasaṃdraṣṭṛprālabdhopāttayojitaḥ
nirvāpito vīrapaśuḥ so 'ṣṭadhottaratottamaḥ
yathottaraṃ na dātavyamayogyebhyaḥ kadācana
śivopayuktaṃ hi havirna sarvo bhoktumarhati
yastu dīkṣāvihīno 'pi śivecchāvidhicoditaḥ
bhaktyāśnāti sa sampūrṇaḥ samayī syātsubhāvitaḥ
dṛṣṭo 'valokitaścaiva kiraṇeddhadṛgarpaṇāt
prokṣitaḥ kevalaṃ hyarghapātravipruḍbhirukṣitaḥ
saṃdraṣṭā darśitāśeṣasamyakpūjitamaṇḍalaḥ
prālabdha uktatritayasaṃskṛtaḥ so 'pi dhūnayet
kampeta prasravetstabdhaḥ pralīno vā yathottaram
upātto yāgasānnidhye śamitaḥ śastramārutaiḥ
yojitaḥ kāraṇatyāgakrameṇa śivayojanāt
nirvāpitaḥ kṛtābhyāsaguruprāṇamano'rpaṇāt
dakṣiṇenāgninā saumyakalājālavilāpanāt
tathāhyādau paraṃ rūpamekībhāvena saṃśrayet
tasmādāgneyacāreṇa jvālāmālāmucāviśet
paśorvāmena candrāṃśujālaṃ tāpena gālayet
nābhicakre 'tha viśrāmyetprāṇaraśmigaṇaiḥ saha
paro bhūtvā svaśaktyātra jīvaṃ jīvena veṣṭayet
svacitsūryeṇa saṃtāpya drāvayet kalāṃ kalām
tato drutaṃ kalājālaṃ prāpayyaikatvamātmani
samastatattvasampūrṇam āpyāyanavidhāyinam
unmūlayeta saṃrambhātkarmabaddhamamuṃ rasāt
tata unmūlanodveṣṭayogādvāmaṃ paribhraman
kuṇḍalyamṛtasampūrṇasvakaprāṇaprasevakaḥ
vāmāvartakramopāttahṛtpadmāmṛtakesaraḥ
hṛtkarṇikārūḍhilābhādojodhātuṃ vilāpitam
śuddhasomātmakaṃ sāramīṣallohitapītalam
ādāya karihastāgrasadṛśe prāṇavigrahe
niḥsṛtya jhaṭiti svātmavāmamārgeṇa saṃviśet
āpyāyayannapānākhyacandracakrahṛdambuje
sthitaṃ taddevatācakraṃ tena sāreṇa tarpayet
anena vidhinā sarvānrasaraktādikāṃstathā
dhātūnsamāharetsaṃghakramādekaikaśo 'thavā
kevalaṃ tvathavāgnīnduravisaṃghaṭṭamadhyagam
jyotīrūpamatha prāṇaśaktyākhyaṃ jīvamāharet
jīvaṃ samarasīkuryāddevīcakreṇa bhāvanāt
tadeva tarpaṇaṃ mukhyaṃ bhogyabhoktrātmataiva sā
agnisaṃpuṭaphullārṇatryaśrakālātmako mahān
piṇḍo raktādisāraughacālanākarṣaṇādiṣu
itthaṃ viśrāntiyogena ghaṭikārdhakrame sati
āvṛttiśatayogena paśornirvāpaṇaṃ bhavet
kṛtvā katipayaṃ kālaṃ tatrābhyāsam ananyadhīḥ
yathā cintāmaṇau proktaṃ tena rūpeṇa yogavit
niḥśaṅkaḥ siddhimāpnoti gopyaṃ tatprāṇavatsphuṭam
parokṣe 'pi paśāvevaṃ vidhiḥ syādyojanaṃ prati
praveśito yāgabhuvi hatastatraiva sādhitaḥ
cakrajuṣṭaśca tatraiva sa vīrapaśurucyate
yastvanyatrāpi nihataḥ sāmastyenāṃśato 'pivā
devāya vinivedayeta sa vai bāhyapaśurmataḥ
rājyaṃ lābho 'tha tatsthairyaṃ śive bhaktistadātmatā
śivajñānaṃ mantralokaprāptistatparivāratā
tatsāyujyaṃ paśoḥ sāmyādbāhyāder vīradharmaṇaḥ
puṣpādayo 'pi tallābhabhāginaḥ śivapūjayā
ekopāyena deveśo viśvānugrahaṇātmakaḥ
yāgenaivānugṛhṇāti kiṃ kiṃ yanna carācaram
tenāvīro 'pi śaṅkādiyuktaḥ kāruṇiko 'pica
na hiṃsābuddhimādadhyātpaśukarmaṇi jātucit
paśormahopakāro 'yaṃ tadātve 'pyapriyaṃ bhavet
vyādhicchedauṣadhatapoyojanātra nidarśanam
śrīmanmṛtyuñjaye proktaṃ pāśacchede kṛte paśoḥ
malatrayaviyogena śarīraṃ na prarohati
dharmādharmaughavicchedāccharīraṃ cyavate kila
tenaitanmāraṇaṃ noktaṃ dīkṣeyaṃ citrarūpiṇī
rūḍhapāśasya yaḥ prāṇairviyogo māraṇaṃ hi tat
iyaṃ tu yojanaiva syātpaśordevāya tarpaṇe
tasmāddevoktimāśritya paśūndadyādbahūniti
niveditaḥ punaḥprāptadeho bhūyoniveditaḥ
ṣaṭkṛtva itthaṃ yaḥ so 'tra ṣaḍjanmā paśuruttamaḥ
yathā pākakramācchuddhaṃ hema tadvatsa kīrtitaḥ
kāṃ siddhiṃ naiva vitaretsvayaṃ kiṃvā na mucyate
uktaṃ tvānandaśāstre yo mantrasaṃskāravāṃstyajet
samayānkutsayeddevīrdadyānmantrānvinā nayāt
dīkṣāmantrādikaṃ prāpya tyajetputrādimohitaḥ
tato manuṣyatāmetya punarevaṃ karotyapi
itthamekādisaptāntajanmāsau dvividho dvipāt
catuṣpādvā paśurdevīcarukārthaṃ prajāyate
dātrarpito 'sau taddvārā yāti sāyujyataḥ śivam
iti saṃbhāvya citraṃ tatpaśūnāṃ praviceṣṭitam
bhogyīcikīrṣitaṃ naiva kuryādanyatra taṃ paśum
nāpi naiṣa bhavedyogya iti buddhvāpasārayet
taṃ paśuṃ kiṃtu kāṅkṣā cedviśeṣe taṃ tu ḍhaukayet
tāvatastānpaśūndadyāttathācoktaṃ maheśinā
paśorvapāmedasī ca gālite vahnimadhyataḥ
arpayecchakticakrāya paramaṃ tarpaṇaṃ matam
hṛdantramuṇḍāṃsayakṛtpradhānaṃ vinivedayet
karṇikākuṇḍalīmajjaparśu mukhyataraṃ ca vā
tato 'gnau tarpaṇaṃ kuryānmantracakrasya daiśikaḥ
tannivedya ca devāya tato vijñāpayetprabhum
gurutvena tvayaivāhamājñātaḥ parameśvara
sākṣāt svapnopadeśād yairjapairgurumukhena vā
anugrāhyāstvayā śiṣyāḥ śivaśaktipracoditāḥ
tadete tadvidhāḥ prāptāstvamebhyaḥ kurvanugraham
samāveśaya māṃ svātmaraśmibhiryadahaṃ śivaḥ
evaṃ bhavatviti tataḥ śivoktimabhinandayet
śivābhinnamathātmānaṃ pañcakṛtyakaraṃ smaret
svātmanaḥ karaṇaṃ mantrānmūrtiṃ cānujighṛkṣayā
tato baddhvā sitoṣṇīṣaṃ hastayorarcayetkramāt
anyonyaṃ pāśadāhāya śuddhatattvavisṛṣṭaye
tejorūpeṇa mantrāṃśca śivahaste samarcayet
garbhāvaraṇagānaṅgaparivārāsanojjhitān
ātmānaṃ bhāvayetpaścādekakaṃ jalacandravat
kṛtyopādhivaśādbhinnaṃ ṣoḍhābhinnaṃ tu vastutaḥ
maṇḍalastho 'hamevāyaṃ sākṣī cākhilakarmaṇām
śuddhā hi draṣṭṛtā śambhormaṇḍale kalpitā mayā
homādhikaraṇatvena vahnāvahamavasthitaḥ
yadātmateddhā mantrāḥ syuḥ pāśaploṣavidhāvalam
sāmānyatejorūpāntarāhūtā bhuvaneśvarāḥ
tarpitāḥ śrāvitāścāṇornādhikāraṃ pratanvate
ā yāgāntamahaṃ kumbhe saṃsthito vighnaśāntaye
sāmānyarūpatā yena viśeṣāpyāyakāriṇī
śiṣyadehe ca tatpāśaśithilatvaprasiddhaye
sa hi svecchāvaśātpāśānvidhunvanniva vartate
sākṣātsvadehasaṃstho 'haṃ kartānugrahakarmaṇām
jñānakriyāsvatantratvāddīkṣākarmaṇi peśalaḥ
bhinnakāryākṛtivrātendriyacakrānusandhimān
eko yathāhaṃ vahnyādiṣaḍrūpo 'smi tathā sphuṭam
evamālocya yenaiṣo 'dhvanā dīkṣāṃ cikīrṣati
anusaṃhitaye śiṣyavarjaṃ pañcasu taṃ yajet
anusandhibalānte ca samāsavyāsabhedataḥ
kuryādatyantamabhyastamanyāntarbhāvapūritam
tato 'pi cintayā bhūyo 'nusaṃdadhyācchivātmatām
ahameva paraṃ tattvaṃ naca tadghaṭavat kvacit
mahāprakāśastattena mayi sarvamidaṃ jagat
naca tatkenacidbāhyapratibimbavadarpitam
kartāhamasya tannānyādhīnaṃ ca madadhiṣṭhitam
itthaṃbhūtamahāvyāptisaṃvedanapavitritaḥ
matsamatvaṃ gato janturmukta ityabhidhīyate
tāpanirgharṣasekādipāramparyeṇa vahnitām
yathāyogolako yāti gururevaṃ śivātmatām
tataḥ puraḥsthitaṃ yadvā purobhāvitavigraham
parokṣadīkṣaṇe yadvā darbhādyaiḥ kalpite mṛte
śiṣye vīkṣyārcya puṣpādyairnyasedadhvānamasya tam
yenādhvanā mukhyatayā dīkṣāmicchati daiśikaḥ
taṃ dehe nyasya tatrāntarbhāvyamanyaditi sthitiḥ
śodhyādhvani ca vinyaste tatraiva pariśodhakam
nyasedyathepsitaṃ mantraṃ śodhyaucityānusārataḥ
kvacicchodhyaṃ tvavinyasya śodhakanyāsamātrataḥ
svayaṃ śudhyati saṃśodhyaṃ śodhakasya prabhāvataḥ
aparaṃ parāparaṃ ca paraṃ ca vidhimicchayā
tadyojanānusāreṇa śritvā nyāsaḥ ṣaḍadhvanaḥ
lalāṭāntaṃ vedavasau randhrāntaṃ rasarandhrake
vasukhendau dvādaśāntamityeṣa trividho vidhiḥ
krameṇa kathyate dṛṣṭaḥ śāstre śrīpūrvasaṃjñite
tatra tattveṣu vinyāso gulphānte caturaṅgule
dharā jalādimūlāntaṃ pratyekaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ kramāt
rasaśrutyaṅgulaṃ nābherūrdhvamitthaṃ ṣaḍaṅgule
puṃsaḥ kalāntaṃ ṣaṭtattvīṃ pratyekaṃ tryaṅgule kṣipet
aṣṭādaśāṅgulaṃ tvevaṃ kaṇṭhakūpāvasānakam
sadāśivāntaṃ māyādicatuṣkaṃ caturaṅgule
pratyekamityabdhivasusaṃkhyamālikadeśataḥ
śivatattvaṃ tataḥ paścāt tejorūpam anākulam
sarveṣāṃ vyāpakatvena sabāhyābhyantaraṃ smaret
jalāddhyantaṃ sārdhayugmaṃ mūlaṃ tryaṅgulamityataḥ
dvādaśāṅgulatādhikyādvidhireṣa parāparaḥ
jalāddhyantaṃ tryaṅgule cedavyaktaṃ tu catuṣṭaye
taccaturviṃśatyādhikyātparo 'pyaṣṭaśate vidhiḥ
trividhonmānakaṃ vyaktaṃ vasudigbhyo ravikṣayāt
mayatantre tathācoktaṃ tattatsvaphalavāñchayā
navapañcacatustryekatattvanyāse svayaṃ dhiyā
nyāsaṃ prakalpayettāvattattvāntarbhāvacintanāt
kalāpañcakavedāṇḍanyāso 'nenaiva lakṣitaḥ
uktaṃ ca triśirastantre svādhārasthaṃ yathāsthitam
dvādaśāṅgulamutthānaṃ dehātītaṃ samaṃ tataḥ
dvāsaptatirdaśa dve ca dehasthaṃ śiraso 'ntataḥ
pādādārabhya suśroṇi anāhatapadāvadhi
dehātīte 'pi viśrāntyā saṃvitteḥ kalpanāvaśāt
dehatvamiti tasmātsyādutthānaṃ dvādaśāṅgulam
iti nirṇetumatraitaduktamaṣṭottaraṃ śatam
puranyāso 'tha gulphāntaṃ bhūḥ purāṇyatra ṣoḍaśa
tasmādekāṅgulavyāptyā pratyekaṃ lakulāditaḥ
dviraṇḍāntaṃ tryaṅgulaṃ tu chagalāṇḍamathābdhiṣu
devayogāṣṭake dve hi pratyekāṅgulapādataḥ
iti pradhānaparyantaṃ ṣaṭcatvāriṃśadaṅgulam
ṣaṭpañcāśatpurāṇītthaṃ prāgdharāyāṃ tu ṣoḍaśa
tato 'pyardhāṅgulavyāptyā ṣaṭpurāṇyaṅgulatraye
catvāri yugma ekasmin ekaṃ ca puramaṅgule
sarāge puṃspurāṇīśasaṃkhyānītthaṃ ṣaḍaṅgule
krodheśapuramekasmindvaye cāṇḍamiyaṃ ca vit
saṃvartajyotiṣorevaṃ kalātattvagayoḥ kramāt
śūrapañcāntapurayorniyatau caikayugmatā
śrīpūrvaśāstre taccoktaṃ parameśena śaṃbhunā
uttarādikramāddvyekabhedo vidyādike traye
asāratvātkramasyādau niyatiḥ parataḥ kalā
athavānyonyasaṃjñābhyāṃ tattvayorvyapadeśyatā
ekavīraśikheśaśrīkaṇṭhāḥ kāle trayastraye
kālasya pūrvaṃ vinyāso niyaterabhidhīyate
athavānyonyasaṃjñābhirvyapadeśo hi dṛśyate
evaṃ pumādiṣaṭtattvī vinyastāṣṭādaśāṅgule
tato 'pyaṅguṣṭhamātrāntaṃ māyātattvasthamaṣṭakam
pratyekamardhāṅgulataḥ syādaṅgulacatuṣṭaye
itthaṃ dvyakṣṇi purāṇyaṣṭāviṃśatiḥ puruṣānniśi
puratrayaṃ dvayostryaṃśanyūnāṅgulamiti kramāt
dvayordvayaṃ pañcapurī vaidyīye caturaṅgule
tata aiśapurāṇyaṣṭau catuṣke 'rdhāṅgulakramāt
tatastrīṇi dvaye dve ca dvayoritthaṃ catuṣṭaye
sādāśivaṃ pañcakaṃ syāditthaṃ vasvekakaṃ ravau
ṣoḍaśakaṃ rasaviśikhaṃ vasudvikaṃ vasuśaśīti puravargāḥ
vedā rasābdhi yugmākṣi ca ravayastatra cāṅgulāḥ kramaśaḥ
aṣṭādaśādhikaśataṃ purāṇi dehe 'tra caturaśītimite
vinyastāni taditthaṃ śeṣe tu vyāpakaṃ śivaṃ tattvam
iti vidhiraparaḥ kathitaḥ parāparākhyo rasaśrutisthāne
aṣṭaśaraṃ saṃkhyānaṃ khamunikṛtaṃ tatpare vidhau jñeyam
lakulāderyogāṣṭakaparyantasyātra bhuvanapūgasya
adhikīkuryādgaṇanāvaśena bhāgaṃ vidhidvaye kramaśaḥ
aparādividhitraitādatha nyāsaḥ padādhvanaḥ
pūrvaṃ daśapadī coktā svatantrā nyasyate yadā
tayaiva dīkṣā kāryā cettadeyaṃ nyāsakalpanā
tattvādimukhyatāyogāddīkṣāyāṃ tu padāvalī
tattattvādyanusāreṇa tatrāntarbhāvyate tathā
svapradhānatvayoge tu dīkṣāyāṃ padapaddhatim
nyasyetkrameṇa tattvādivadanānavalokinīm
caturṣvaṣṭāsu cāṣṭāsu daśasvatha daśasvatha
daśasvatho pañcadaśasvatha vedaśarenduṣu
dharāpadān navapadīṃ mātṛkāmālinīgatām
yojayedvyāptṛ daśamaṃ padaṃ tu śivasaṃjñitam
dharāpadaṃ varjayitvā pañca yāni padāni tu
vidhidvayaṃ syānnikṣipya dvādaśa dvādaśāṅgulān
mantrādhvano 'pyeṣa eva vidhirvinyāsayojane
vyāptimātraṃ hi bhidyetetyuktaṃ prāgeva tattathā
varṇādhvano 'tha vinyāsaḥ kathyate 'tra vidhitraye
ekaṃ caturṣu pratyekaṃ dvayoraṅgulayoḥ kramāt
trayoviṃśativarṇī syāt ṣaḍvarṇyekaikaśastriṣu
pratyekamatha catvāraścaturṣviti vilomataḥ
mālinīmātṛkārṇāḥ syurvyāptṛ śaivaṃ rasendutaḥ
varjayitvādyavarṇaṃ tu tattvavatsyādravīnravīn
tāṃ trayoviṃśatau varṇeṣvapyanyatsyādvidhidvayam
śrīpūrvaśāstre tenādau tattveṣūktaṃ vidhitrayam
atidiṣṭaṃ tu tadbhinnābhinnavarṇadvaye samam
dvividho 'pi hi varṇānāṃ ṣaḍvidho bheda ucyate
tattvamārgavidhānena jñātavyaḥ paramārthataḥ
upadeśātideśābhyāṃ yaduktaṃ tatpadādiṣu
bhūyo 'tidiṣṭaṃ tatraiva śāstre 'smaddhṛdayeśvare
padamantrakalādīnāṃ pūrvasūtrānusārataḥ
tritayatvaṃ prakurvīta tattvavarṇoktavartmanā
uktaṃ tatpadamantreṣu kalāsvatha nirūpyate
caturṣu rasavede dvāviṃśatau dvādaśasvatha
nivṛttyādyāścatasraḥ syurvyāptrī syācchāntyatītikā
dvitīyasyāṃ kalāyāṃ tu dvādaśa dvādaśāṅgulān
kramātkṣiptvā vidhidvaitaṃ parāparaparātmakam
caturaṇḍavidhistvādiśabdeneha pragṛhyate
kalācatuṣkavattena tasminvācyaṃ vidhitrayam
evaṃ ṣaḍvidhamadhvānaṃ śodhyaśiṣyatanau purā
nyasyaikatamamukhyatvānnyasyecchodhakasaṃmatam
adhvanyāsanamantraughaḥ śodhako hyeka āditaḥ
śabdarāśirmālinī ca samastavyastato dvidhā
ekavīratayā yadvā ṣaṭkaṃ yāmalayogataḥ
pañcavaktrī śaktitadvadbhedātṣoḍhā punardvidhā
ekākiyāmalatvenetyevaṃ sā dvādaśātmikā
ṣaḍaṅgī sakalānyatvāddvividhā vaktravatpunaḥ
dvādaśatvena guṇitā caturviṃśatibhedikā
aghorādyaṣṭake dve ca tṛtīyaṃ yāmalodayāt
mātṛsadbhāvamantraśca kevalaḥ śruticakragaḥ
ekadvitricaturbhedāttrayodaśabhidātmakaḥ
ekavīratayā so 'yaṃ caturdaśatayā sthitaḥ
anāmasaṃhṛtisthairyasṛṣṭicakraṃ caturvidham
devatābhirnijābhis tanmātṛsadbhāvabṛṃhitam
itthaṃ śodhakavargo 'yaṃ mantrāṇāṃ saptatiḥ smṛtā
ṣaḍardhaśāstreṣu śrīmatsāraśāstre ca kathyate
aghorādyaṣṭakeneha śodhanīyaṃ vipaścitā
athavaikākṣarāmantrair athavā mātṛkākramāt
bhairavīyahṛdā vāpi khecarīhṛdayena vā
bhairaveṇa mahādevi tvatha vaktrāṅgapañcakaiḥ
yena yena hi mantreṇa tantre 'smin udbhavaḥ kṛtaḥ
tenaiva dīkṣayenmantrī ityājñā pārameśvarī
evaṃ śodhakabhedena saptatiḥ kīrtitā bhidaḥ
śodhyanyāsaṃ vinā mantrairetairdīkṣā yadā bhavet
tadā saptatidhā jñeyā jananādivivarjitā
śodhyabhedo 'tha vaktavyaḥ saṃkṣepātso 'pi kathyate
ekatripañcaṣaṭtriṃśadbhedāttāttvaścaturvidhaḥ
pañcaikabhedāccādhvānastathaivāṇḍacatuṣṭayam
evaṃ daśavidhaṃ śodhyaṃ triṃśaddhā tadvidhitrayāt
śodhyaśodhakabhedena śatāni tvekaviṃśatiḥ
atrāpi nyāsayogena śodhye 'dhvani tathākṛteḥ
śataikaviṃśatibhidā jananādyujjhitā bhavet
jananādimayī tāvatyevaṃ śatadṛśi śrutiḥ
syātsaptatyadhikā sāpi dravyavijñānabhedataḥ
dvidheti pañcāśītiḥ syācchatānyadhikakhābdhikā
bhogamokṣānusandhānāddvividhā sā prakīrtitā
aśubhasyaiva saṃśuddhyā śubhasyāpyatha śodhanāt
dvidhā bhogaḥ śubhe śuddhiḥ kālatrayavibhedini
ekadvisāmastyavaśātsaptadhetyaṣṭadhā bhujiḥ
guruśiṣyakramātso 'pi dvidhetyevaṃ vibhidyate
pratyakṣadīkṣaṇe yasmāddvayorekānusaṃdhitaḥ
tādṛgdīkṣāphalaṃ pūrṇaṃ visaṃvāde tu viplavaḥ
parokṣamṛtadīkṣādau gururevānusandhimān
kriyājñānamahimnā taṃ śiṣyaṃ dhāmnīpsite nayet
avibhinne kriyājñāne karmaśuddhau tathaiva te
anusandhiḥ punarbhinnaḥ karma yasmāttadātmakam
śrīmatsvacchandaśāstre ca vāsanābhedataḥ phalam
śiṣyāṇāṃ ca guroścoktamabhinne 'pi kriyādike
bhogasya śodhakācchodhyādanusandheśca tādṛśāt
vaicitryamasti bhedasya vaicitryaprāṇatā yataḥ
tathāhi vaktrairyasyādhvā śuddhastaireva yojitaḥ
bhoktumiṣṭe kvacittattve sa bhoktā tadbalānvitaḥ
śubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ cātra sadbhāve bhogacitratā
tādṛgeva bhavetkarmaśuddhau tvanyaiva citratā
bhogaśca sadya utkrāntyā dehenaivātha saṃgataḥ
tadaivābhyāsato vāpi dehānte vetyasau catuḥ
prāktanāṣṭabhidā yogāddvātriṃśadbheda ucyate
mokṣa eko 'pi bījasya samayākhyasya tādṛśam
bālādikaṃ jñātaśīghramaraṇaṃ śaktivarjitam
vṛddhaṃ voddiśya śaktaṃ vā śodhanāśodhanāddvidhā
sadya utkrāntitastraidhaṃ sā cāsannamṛtau guroḥ
kāryetyājñā maheśasya śrīmadgahvarabhāṣitā
dṛṣṭvā śiṣyaṃ jarāgrastaṃ vyādhinā paripīḍitam
utkramayya tatastvenaṃ paratattve niyojayet
pañcatriṃśadamī bhedā gurorvā guruśiṣyayoḥ
uktadvaividhyakalanātsaptatiḥ parikīrtitāḥ
etairbhedaiḥ puroktāṃstānbhedāndīkṣāgatānguruḥ
hatvā vadetprasaṃkhyānaṃ svabhyastajñānasiddhaye
pañcāśītiśatī yā catvāriṃśatsamuttarā kathitā
tāṃ saptatyā bhittvā dīkṣābhedānsvayaṃ kalayet
pañcakamiha lakṣāṇāṃ ca saptanavatiḥ sahasraparisaṃkhyā
aṣṭau śatāni dīkṣābhedo 'yaṃ mālinītantre
saptatidhā śoddhṛgaṇastriṃśaddhā śodhya ekatattvādiḥ
sāṇḍaḥ ṣaḍadhvarūpastathetikartavyatā caturbhedā
dravyajñānamayī sā jananādivivarjitātha tadyuktā
pañcatriṃśaddhā punareṣā bhogāpavargasandhānāt
yasmāddvātriṃśaddhā bhogaḥ śubhaśuddhyaśuddhikālabhidā
mokṣastredhā dviguṇā saptatiritikāryatābhedāḥ
śodhanaśodhyavibhedāditikartavyatvabhedataścaiṣā
dīkṣā bahudhā bhinnā śodhyavihīnā tu saptatidhā
mantrāṇāṃ sakaletarasāṅganiraṅgādibhedasaṃkalanāt
śyodhyasya ca tattvādeḥ pañcadaśādyuktabhedaparigaṇanāt
bhedānāṃ parigaṇanā na śakyate kartumityasaṃkīrṇāḥ
bhedāḥ saṃkīrṇāḥ punaranye bhūyastvakāriṇo bahudhā
śodhakaśodhyādīnāṃ dvitrādivibhedasadbhāvāt
bhoge sādhye yadyadbahu kartavyaṃ tadāśrayenmatimān
kāraṇabhūyastvaṃ kila phalabhūyastvāya kiṃ citram
apavarge natu bhedastenāsminvāsanādṛḍhatvajuṣā
alpāpyāśrayaṇīyā kriyātha vijñānamātre vā
abhinavaguptaguruḥ punarāha hi sati vittadeśakālādau
apavarge 'pi hi vistīrṇakarmavijñānasaṃgrahaḥ kāryaḥ
cidvṛttervaicitryāccāñcalye 'pi krameṇa sandhānāt
tasmiṃstasminvastuni rūḍhiravaśyaṃ śivātmikā bhavati
tattvamidametadātmakam etasmāt proddhṛto mayā śiṣyaḥ
itthaṃ kramasaṃvittau mūḍho 'pi śivātmako bhavati
kramikatathāvidhaśivatānugrahasubhagaṃ ca daiśikaṃ paśyan
śiśurapi tadabhedadṛśā bhaktibalāccābhyupaiti śivabhāvam
yadyapi vikalpavṛtterapi mokṣaṃ dīkṣayaiva dehānte
śāstre provāca vibhustathāpi dṛḍhavāsanā yuktā
mokṣe 'pyasti viśeṣaḥ kriyālpabhūyastvajaḥ salokādiḥ
iti kecittadayuktaṃ sa vicitro bhoga eva kathitaḥ syāt
saṃskāraśeṣavartanajīvitamadhye 'sya samayalopādyam
nāyāti vighnajālaṃ kriyābahutvaṃ mumukṣostat
yasmāt sabījadīkṣāsaṃskṛtapuruṣasya samayalopādye
bhukte bhogānmokṣo naivaṃ nirbījadīkṣāyām
iti kecinmanyante yuktaṃ taccāpi yatsmṛtaṃ śāstre
samayollaṅghanāddevi kravyādatvaṃ śataṃ samāḥ
tasmāduruśiṣyamatau śivabhāvanirūḍhivitaraṇasamartham
kramikaṃ tattvoddharaṇādi karma mokṣe 'pi yuktamativitatam
yastu sadā bhāvanayā svabhyastajñānavānguruḥ sa śiśoḥ
apavargāya yathecchaṃ yaṃ kaṃcidupāyamanutiṣṭhet
evaṃ śiṣyatanau śodhyaṃ nyasyādhvānaṃ yathepsitam
śodhakaṃ mantramupari nyasyettattvānusārataḥ
dvayormātṛkayostattvasthityā varṇakramaḥ purā
kathitastaṃ tathā nyasyettattattattvaviśuddhaye
varṇādhvā yadyapi proktaḥ śodhyaḥ pāśātmakastu saḥ
māyīyaḥ śodhakastvanyaḥ śivātmā paravāṅmayaḥ
uvāca sadyojyotiśca vṛttau svāyambhuvasya tat
bāḍhameko hi pāśātmā śabdo 'nyaśca śivātmakaḥ
tasmāttasyaiva varṇasya yuktā śodhakaśodhyatā
śrīpūrvaśāstre cāpyuktaṃ te tairāliṅgitā iti
sadyojātādivaktrāṇi hṛdādyaṅgāni pañca ca
ṣaṭkṛtvo nyasya ṣaṭtriṃśannyāsaṃ kuryāddharāditaḥ
parāparāyā vailomyāddharāyāṃ syātpadatrayam
tato jalādahaṅkāre pañcāṣṭakasamāśrayāt
padāni pañca dhīmūlapuṃrāgākhye traye trayam
ekaṃ tvaśuddhavitkāladvaye caikaṃ niyāmake
kalāmāyādvaye caikaṃ padamuktamiha kramāt
vidyeśvarasadāśaktiśiveṣu padapañcakam
ekonaviṃśatiḥ seyaṃ padānāṃ syātparāparā
sārdhaṃ caikaṃ caikaṃ sārdhaṃ dve dve śaśī dṛgatha yugmam
trīṇi dṛgabdhiścandraḥ śrutiḥ śaśī pañca vidhumahaścandrāḥ
ekānnaviṃśatau syādakṣarasaṃkhyā padeṣviyaṃ devyāḥ
haldvayayutavasucitraguparisaṃkhyātasvavarṇāyāḥ
mūlāntaṃ sārdhavarṇaṃ syānmāyāntaṃ varṇamekakam
śaktyantamekam aparānyāse vidhirudīritaḥ
māyāntaṃ haltataḥ śaktiparyante svara ucyate
niṣkale śivatattve vai paro nyāsaḥ paroditaḥ
parāparāpadānyeva hyaghoryādyaṣṭakadvaye
mantrāstadanusāreṇa tattveṣvetaddvayaṃ kṣipet
piṇḍākṣarāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ varṇasaṃkhyā vibhedataḥ
avyaktāntaṃ svare nyasyā śeṣaṃ śeṣeṣu yojayet
bījāni sarvatattveṣu vyāptṛtvena prakalpayet
piṇḍānāṃ bījavannyāsamanye tu pratipedire
akṛte vātha śodhyasya nyāse vastubalāt sthiteḥ
śodhakanyāsamātreṇa sarvaṃ śodhyaṃ viśudhyati
śrīmanmṛtyuñjayādau ca kathitaṃ parameṣṭhinā
adhunā nyāsamātreṇa bhūtaśuddhiḥ prajāyate
dehaśuddhyarthamapyetattulyametena vastutaḥ
anyaprakaraṇoktaṃ yadyuktaṃ prakaraṇāntare
jñāpakatvena sākṣādvā tatkiṃ nānyatra gṛhyate
mālinīmātṛkāṅgasya nyāso yo 'rcāvidhau purā
proktaḥ kevalasaṃśoddhṛmantranyāse sa eva tu
tripadī dvayordvayoḥ syātpratyekamathāṣṭasu śrutipadāni
dikcandracandrarasaraviśaraśaradṛgdṛṅmṛgāṅkaśaśigaṇane
aṅgulamāne devyā aṣṭādaśa vaibhavena padamanyat
aparaṃ mānamidaṃ syāt kevalaśodhakamanunyāse
turyapadātpadaṣaṭke mānadvitayaṃ parāparaparākhyam
dvādaśakaṃ dvādaśakaṃ tattvopari pūrvavattvanyat
kevalaśodhakamantranyāsābhiprāyato mahādevaḥ
tattvakramoditamapi nyāsaṃ punarāha tadviruddhamapi
niṣkale padamekārṇaṃ yāvattrīṇi tu pārthive
ityādinā tattvagatakramanyāsa udīritaḥ
punaśca mālinītantre vargavidyāvibhedataḥ
dvidhā padānītyuktvākhyannyāsamanyādṛśaṃ vibhuḥ
ekaikaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ jñeyaṃ tatra pūrvaṃ padatrayam
aṣṭāṅgulāni catvāri daśāṅgulamataḥ param
dvyaṅgule dve pade cānye ṣaḍaṅgulamataḥ param
dvādaśāṅgulamanyacca dve 'nye pañcāṅgule pṛthak
padadvayaṃ catuṣparva tathānye dve dviparvaṇī
evaṃ parāparādevyāḥ svatantro nyāsa ucyate
vidyādvayaṃ śiṣyatanau vyāptṛtvenaiva yojayet
iti darśayituṃ nāsya pṛthaṅnyāsaṃ nyarūpayat
evaṃ śodhakamantrasya nyāse tadraśmiyogataḥ
pāśajālaṃ vilīyeta taddhyānabalato guroḥ
śodhyatattve samastānāṃ yonīnāṃ tulyakālataḥ
jananādbhogataḥ karmakṣaye syādapavṛktatā
dehaistāvadbhirasyāṇościtraṃ bhokturapi sphuṭam
mano'nusandhirno viśvasaṃyogapravibhāgavat
niyatyā manaso dehamātre vṛttistataḥ param
nānusandhā yataḥ saikasvāntayuktākṣakalpitā
pradeśavṛtti ca jñānamātmanastatra tatra tat
bhogyajñānaṃ nānyadeheṣvanusandhānamarhati
yadā tu manasastasya dehavṛtterapi dhruvam
yogamantrakriyādeḥ syādvaimalyaṃ tadvidā tadā
yathāmalaṃ mano dūrasthitamapyāśu paśyati
tathā pratyayadīkṣāyāṃ tattadbhuvanadarśanam
jananādiviyuktāṃ tu yadā dīkṣāṃ cikīrṣati
tadāsmāduddharāmīti yuktamūhaprakalpanam
yadā śodhyaṃ vinā śoddhṛnyāsastatrāpi mantrataḥ
jananādikramaṃ kuryāttattvasaṃśleṣavarjitam
ekākiśoddhṛnyāse ca jananādivivarjane
tacchoddhṛsaṃpuṭaṃ nāma kevalaṃ parikalpayet
dravyayogena dīkṣāyāṃ tilājyākṣatataṇḍulam
tattanmantreṇa juhuyājjanmayogaviyogayoḥ
yadā vijñānadīkṣāṃ tu kuryācchiṣyaṃ tadā bhṛśam
tanmantrasaṃjalpabalāt paśyed ā cāvikalpakāt
vikalpaḥ kila saṃjalpamayo yatsa vimarśakaḥ
mantrātmāsau vimarśaśca śuddho 'pāśavatātmakaḥ
nityaś cānādivaradaśivābhedopakalpitaḥ
tadyogāddaiśikasyāpi vikalpaḥ śivatāṃ vrajet
śrīsāraśāstre tadidaṃ parameśena bhāṣitam
arthasya pratipattiryā grāhyagrāhakarūpiṇī
sā eva mantraśaktistu vitatā mantrasantatau
parāmarśasvabhāvetthaṃ mantraśaktirudāhṛtā
parāmarśo dvidhā śuddhāśuddhatvānmantrabhedakaḥ
uktaṃ śrīpauṣkare 'nye ca brahmaviṣṇvādayo 'ṇḍagāḥ
prādhānikāḥ sāñjanāste sāttvarājasatāmasāḥ
tairaśuddhaparāmarśāt tanmayībhāvito guruḥ
vaiṣṇavādiḥ paśuḥ prokto na yogyaḥ patiśāsane
ye mantrāḥ śuddhamārgasthāḥ śivabhaṭṭārakādayaḥ
śrīmanmataṅgādidṛśā tanmayo hi guruḥ śivaḥ
nanu svatantrasaṃjalpayogādastu vimarśitā
prākkutaḥ sa vimarśāccetkutaḥ so 'pi nirūpaṇe
ādyastathāvikalpatvapradaḥ syādupadeṣṭṛtaḥ
yaḥ saṃkrānto 'bhijalpaḥ syāttasyāpyanyopadeṣṭṛtaḥ
pūrvapūrvakramāditthaṃ ya evādiguroḥ purā
saṃjalpo hyabhisaṃkrāntaḥ so 'dyāpyastīti gṛhyatām
yastathāvidhasaṃjalpabalātko 'pi svatantrakaḥ
vimarśaḥ kalpyate so 'pi tadātmaiva suniścitaḥ
ghaṭakumbha itītthaṃ vā yadi bhedo nirūpyate
so 'pyanyakalpanādāyī hyanādṛtyaḥ prayatnataḥ
paṇāyate karotīti vikalpasyocitau sphuṭam
karapāṇyabhijalpau tau saṃkīryetāṃ kathaṃ kila
śabdācchabdāntare tena vyutpattirvyavadhānataḥ
vyavahārāttu sā sākṣāccitropākhyāvimarśinī
tadvimarśodayaḥ prācyasvavimarśamayaḥ sphuret
yāvadbālasya saṃvittirakṛtrimavimarśane
tena tanmantraśabdārthaviśeṣotthaṃ vikalpanam
śabdāntarotthādbhedena paśyatā mantra ādṛtaḥ
yaccāpi bījapiṇḍāderuktaṃ prāgbodharūpakam
tattasyaiva kuto 'nyasya tatkasmādanyakalpanā
etadarthaṃ guroryatnāllakṣaṇe tatra tatra tat
lakṣaṇaṃ kathitaṃ hyeṣa mantratantraviśāradaḥ
tena mantrārthasaṃbodhe mantravārtikamādarāt
ūhāpohaprayogaṃ vā sarvathā gururācaret
mantrārthavidabhāve tu sarvathā mantratanmayam
guruṃ kuryāt tadabhyāsāttatsaṃkalpamayo hyasau
tatsamānābhisaṃjalpo yadā mantrārthabhāvanāt
gurorbhavettadā sarvasāmye ko bheda ucyatām
aṃśenāpyatha vaiṣamye na tato 'rthakriyā hi sā
gomayātkīṭataḥ kīṭa ityevaṃ nyāyato yadā
saṃjalpāntarato 'pyarthakriyāṃ tāmeva paśyati
tadaiṣa satyasaṃjalpaḥ śiva eveti kathyate
sa yadvakti tadeva syānmantro bhogāpavargadaḥ
naiṣo 'bhinavaguptasya pakṣo mantrārpitātmanaḥ
yo 'rthakriyāmāha bhinnāṃ kīṭayorapi tādṛśoḥ
mantrārpitamanāḥ kiṃcidvadanyattu viṣaṃ haret
tanmantra eva śabdaḥ sa paraṃ tatra ghaṭādivat
kāntāsaṃbhogasaṃjalpasundaraḥ kāmukaḥ sadā
tatsaṃskṛto 'pyanyadeṣa kurvansvātmani tṛpyati
tathā tanmantrasaṃjalpabhāvito 'nyadapi bruvan
anicchurapi tadrūpastathā kāryakaro dhruvam
vikalpayannapyekārthaṃ yato 'nyadapi paśyati
viṣāpahārimantrādītyuktaṃ śrīpūrvaśāsane
yadi vā viṣanāśe 'pi hetubhedādvicitratā
dhātvāpyāyādikānantakāryabhedādbhaviṣyati
tadevaṃ mantrasaṃjalpavikalpābhyāsayogataḥ
bhāvyavastusphuṭībhāvaḥ saṃjalpahrāsayogataḥ
vastveva bhāvayatyeṣa na saṃjalpamimaṃ punaḥ
gṛhṇāti bhāsanopāyaṃ bhāte tatra tu tena kim
evaṃ saṃjalpanirhrāse suparisphuṭatātmakam
akṛttrimavimarśātma sphuredvastvavikalpakam
nirvikalpā ca sā saṃvidyadyathā paśyati sphuṭam
tattathaiva tathātmatvādvastuno 'pi bahiḥsthiteḥ
viśeṣatas tvamāyīyaśivatābhedaśālinaḥ
mokṣe 'bhyupāyaḥ saṃjalpo bandhamokṣau tataḥ kila
vikalpe 'pi guroḥ samyagabhinnaśivatājuṣaḥ
avikalpakaparyantapratīkṣā nopayujyate
tadvimarśasvabhāvā hi sā vācyā mantradevatā
mahāsaṃvitsamāsannetyuktaṃ śrīgamaśāsane
nikaṭasthā yathā rājñāmanyeṣāṃ sādhayantyalam
siddhiṃ rājopagāṃ śīghramevaṃ mantrādayaḥ parām
uktābhiprāyagarbhaṃ taduktaṃ śrīmālinīmate
mantrāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kasmādityukte munibhiḥ kila
yogamekatvamicchanti vastuno 'nyena vastunā
tadvastu jñeyamityuktaṃ heyatvādiprasiddhaye
tatprasiddhyai śivenoktaṃ jñānaṃ yadupavarṇitam
sabījayogasaṃsiddhyai mantralakṣaṇamapyalam
na cādhikāritā dīkṣāṃ vinā yoge 'sti śāṅkare
kriyājñānavibhedena sā ca dvedhā nigadyate
dvividhā sā prakartavyā tena caitadudāhṛtam
naca yogādhikāritvam ekamevānayā bhavet
api mantrādhikāritvaṃ muktiśca śivadīkṣayā
anenaitadapi proktaṃ yogī tattvaikyasiddhaye
mantramevāśrayenmūlaṃ nirvikalpāntamādṛtaḥ
mantrābhyāsena bhogaṃ vā mokṣaṃ vāpi prasādhayan
tatrādhikāritālabdhyai dīkṣāṃ gṛhṇīta daiśikāt
tena mantrajñānayogabalādyadyatprasādhayet
tatsyādasyānyatattve 'pi yuktasya guruṇā śiśoḥ
dīkṣā hyasyopayujyeta saṃskriyāyāṃ sa saṃskṛtaḥ
svabalenaiva bhogaṃ vā mokṣaṃ vā labhate budhaḥ
tena vijñānayogādibalī prāk samayī bhavan
putrako vā na tāvānsyādapitu svabalocitaḥ
yastu vijñānayogādivandhyaḥ so 'ndho yathā pathi
daiśikāyatta eva syādbhoge muktau ca sarvathā
dīkṣā ca kevalā jñānaṃ vināpi nijamāntaram
mocikaiveti kathitaṃ yuktyā cāgamataḥ purā
yastu dīkṣākṛtāmevāpekṣya yojanikāṃ śiśuḥ
sphuṭībhūtyai taducitaṃ jñānaṃ yogamathāśritaḥ
so 'pi yatraiva yuktaḥ syāttanmayatvaṃ prapadyate
gurudīkṣāmantraśāstrādhīnasarvasthitis tataḥ
duṣṭānāmeva sarveṣāṃ bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyatām
karmaṇāṃ śodhanaṃ kāryaṃ bubhukṣorna śubhātmanām
yaḥ punarlaukikaṃ bhogaṃ rājyasvargādikaṃ śiśuḥ
tyaktvā lokottaraṃ bhogamīpsustasya śubheṣvapi
tatra dravyamayīṃ dīkṣāṃ kurvannājyatilādikaiḥ
karmāsya śodhayāmīti juhuyāddaiśikottamaḥ
jñānamayyāṃ tu dīkṣāyāṃ tad viśudhyati saṃdhitaḥ
guroḥ svasaṃvidrūḍhasya balāttatprakṣayo bhavet
yadāsyāśubhakarmāṇi śuddhāni syustadā śubham
svatāratamyāśrayaṇādadhvamadhye prasūtidam
śubhapākakramopāttaphalabhogasamāptitaḥ
yatraiṣa yojitastatstho bhāvikarmakṣaye kṛte
bhāvināṃ cādyadehasthadehāntaravibhedinām
aśubhāṃśaviśuddhau syād bhogasyaivānupakṣayaḥ
bhuñjānasyāsya satataṃ bhogānmāyālayāntataḥ
na duḥkhaphaladaṃ dehādyadhvamadhye 'pi kiṃcana
tato māyālaye bhuktasamastasukhabhogakaḥ
niṣkale sakale vaiti layaṃ yojanikābalāt
iti prameyaṃ kathitaṃ dīkṣā kāle guroryathā
atha bhairavatādātmyadāyinīṃ prakriyāṃ bruve
evaṃ maṇḍalakumbhāgniśiṣyasvātmasu pañcasu
gṛhītvā vyāptimaikyena nyasyādhvānaṃ ca śiṣyagam
karmamāyāṇumalinatrayaṃ bāhau gale tathā
śikhāyāṃ ca kṣipetsūtragranthiyogena daiśikaḥ
tasyātadrūpatābhānaṃ malo granthiḥ sa kīrtyate
itipratītidārḍhyārthaṃ bahirgranthyupakalpanam
bāhū karmāspadaṃ viṣṇurmāyātmā galasaṃśritaḥ
adhovahā śikhāṇutvaṃ tenetthaṃ kalpanā kṛtā
naraśaktiśivākhyasya trayasya bahubhedatām
vaktuṃ tristriguṇaṃ sūtraṃ granthaye parikalpayet
tejojalānnatritayaṃ tredhā pratyekamapyadaḥ
śrutyante ke 'pyataḥ śuklakṛṣṇaraktaṃ prapedire
tato 'gnau tarpitāśeṣamantre cidvyomamātrake
sāmānyarūpe tattvānāṃ kramācchuddhiṃ samācaret
tatra svamantrayogena dharāmāvāhayetpurā
iṣṭvā puṣpādibhiḥ sarpistilādyairatha tarpayet
tattattvavyāpikāṃ paścānmāyātattvādhidevatām
māyāśaktiṃ svamantreṇāvāhyābhyarcya pratarpayet
āvāhane mātṛkārṇaṃ mālinyarṇaṃ ca pūjane
kuryāditi guruḥ prāha svarūpāpyāyanadvayāt
tāro varṇo 'tha saṃbuddhipadaṃ tvāmityataḥ param
uttamaikayutaṃ karmapadaṃ dīpakamapyataḥ
tubhyaṃ nāma caturthyantaṃ tato 'pyucitadīpakam
ityūhamantrayogena tattatkarma pravartayet
āvāhanānantaraṃ hi karma sarvaṃ nigadyate
āvāhanaṃ ca saṃbodhaḥ svasvabhāvavyavasthiteḥ
bhāvasyāhaṃmayasvātmatādātmyāveśyamānatā
śāktī bhūmiśca saivoktā yasyāṃ mukhyāsti pūjyatā
abhātatvād abhedācca nahyasau nṛśivātmanoḥ
jaḍābhāseṣu tattveṣu saṃvitsthityai tato guruḥ
āvāhanavibhaktiṃ prāk kṛtvā turyavibhaktitaḥ
namaskārāntatāyogātpūrṇāṃ sattāṃ prakalpayet
tataḥ pūrṇasvabhāvatvaṃ tadrūpodrekayogataḥ
dhyeyodreko bhaved dhyātṛprahvībhāvavaśād yataḥ
āvāhyeṣṭvā pratarpyeti śrīsvacchande nirūpitam
anenaiva pathāneyamityasmadguravo jaguḥ
paratvena tu yatpūjyaṃ tatsvatantracidātmakam
anavacchitprakāśatvānna prakāśyaṃ tu kutracit
tasya hyetat prapūjyatvadhyeyatvādi yadullaset
tasyaiva tatsvatantratvaṃ yātidurghaṭakāritā
saṃbodharūpe tattasmin kathaṃ saṃbodhanā bhavet
prakāśanāyāṃ na syātprakāśasya prakāśatā
saṃbodhanavibhaktyaiva vinā karmādiśaktitām
svātantryāttaṃ darśayituṃ tatrohamimamācaret
devamāvāhayāmīti tato devāya dīpakam
prāgyuktyā pūrṇatādāyi namaḥsvāhādikaṃ bhavet
nutiḥ pūrṇatvam agnīndusaṃghaṭṭāpyāyatā param
āpyāyakaṃ ca procchālaṃ vauṣaḍādi pradīpayet
tatra bāhye 'pi tādātmyaprasiddhaṃ karma codyate
yadi karmapadaṃ tanno gurur abhyūhayet kvacit
anābhāsitatadvastubhāsanāya niyujyate
mantraḥ kiṃ tena tatra syātsphuṭaṃ yatrāvabhāsi tat
tena prokṣaṇasaṃsekajapādividhiṣu dhruvam
tatkarmābhyūhanaṃ kuryātpratyuta vyavadhātṛtām
bahistathātmatābhāve kāryaṃ karmapadohanam
tṛptāvāhutihutabhukpāśaploṣacchidādiṣu
yatroddiṣṭe vidhau paścāttadanantaiḥ kriyātmakaiḥ
aṃśaiḥ sādhyaṃ na tatroho dīkṣaṇādividhiṣviva
tataḥ śiṣyasya tattattvasthāne 'streṇa pratāḍanam
kṛtvātha śivahastena hṛdayaṃ parimarśayet
tataḥ svanāḍīmārgeṇa hṛdayaṃ prāpya vai śiśoḥ
śiṣyātmanā sahaikatvaṃ gatvādāya ca taṃ hṛdā
puṭitaṃ haṃsarūpākhyaṃ tatra saṃhāramudrayā
kuryādātmīyahṛdayasthitamapyavabhāsakam
śiṣyadehasya tejobhī raśmimātrāviyogataḥ
svabandhasthānacalanāt svatantrasthānalābhataḥ
svakarmāparatantratvāt sarvatrotpattimarhati
tenātmahṛdayānītaṃ prākkṛtvā pudgalaṃ tataḥ
māyāyāṃ taddharātattvaśarīrāṇyasya saṃsṛjet
tatrāsya garbhādhānaṃ ca yuktaṃ puṃsavanādibhiḥ
garbhaniṣkrāmaparyantairekāṃ kurvīta saṃskriyām
jananaṃ bhogabhoktṛtvaṃ militvaikātha saṃskriyā
tato 'sya teṣu bhogeṣu kuryāttanmayatāṃ layam
tatastattattvapāśānāṃ vicchedaṃ samupācaret
saṃskārāṇāṃ catuṣke 'smin aparāṃ ca parāparām
mantrāṇāṃ pañcadaśakaṃ parāṃ vā yojayetkramāt
pivanyādyaṣṭakaṃ śastrādikaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ parā tathā
iti pañcadaśaite syuḥ kramāllīnatvasaṃskṛtau
aparāmantramuktvā prāgamukātmana ityatha
garbhādhānaṃ karomīti punarmantraṃ tameva ca
svāhāntamuccarandadyādāhutitritayaṃ guruḥ
paraṃ parāparāmantramamukātmana ityatha
jātasya bhogabhoktṛtvaṃ karomyatha parāparām
ante svāheti proccārya vitarettisra āhutīḥ
uccārya pivanīmantramamukātmana ityatha
bhoge layaṃ karomīti punarmantraṃ tameva ca
svāhāntamāhutīstisro dadyādājyatilādibhiḥ
eṣa eva vamanyādau vidhiḥ pañcadaśāntake
pūrvaṃ parātmakaṃ mantramamukātmana ityatha
pāśācchedaṃ karomīti parāmantraḥ punastataḥ
huṃ svāhā phaṭ samuccārya dadyāttisro 'pyathāhutīḥ
saṃskārāṇāṃ catuṣke 'sminye mantrāḥ kathitā mayā
teṣu karmapadātpūrvaṃ dharātattvapadaṃ vadet
tato dharātattvapatimāmantryeṣṭvā pratarpya ca
śivābhimānasaṃrabdho gururevaṃ samādiśet
tattveśvara tvayā nāsya putrakasya śivājñayā
pratibandhaḥ prakartavyo yātuḥ padamanāmayam
tato yadi samīheta dharātattvāntarālagam
pṛthak śodhayituṃ mantrī bhuvanādyadhvapañcakam
aparāmantrataḥ prāgvattisrastisrastadāhutīḥ
dadyātpuraṃ śodhayāmītyūhayuktaṃ prasannadhīḥ
evaṃ kalāmantrapadavarṇeṣvapi vicakṣaṇaḥ
tisrastisro hutīrdadyāt pṛthak sāmastyato 'pivā
tataḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ dattvā parayā vauṣaḍantayā
aparāmantrataḥ śiṣyamuddhṛtyātmahṛdaṃ nayet
yadā tvekena śuddhena tadantarbhāvacintanāt
na pṛthak śodhayettattvanāthasaṃśravaṇātparam
tadā pūrṇāṃ vitīryāṇumutkṣipyātmani yojayet
tātsthyātmasaṃsthyayogāya tayaivāparayāhutīḥ
sakarmapadayā dadyāditi kecittu manvate
anye tu guravaḥ prāhurbhāvanāmayamīdṛśam
nātra bāhyāhutirdeyā daiśikasya pṛthak punaḥ
dadyādvā yadi no doṣaḥ syādupāyaḥ sa bhāvane
evaṃ prāktanatātsthyātmasaṃsthatve yojayedguruḥ
tataḥ śiṣyahṛdaṃ neyaḥ sa ātmā tāvato 'dhvanaḥ
śuddhastaddārḍhyasiddhyai ca pūrṇā syātparayā punaḥ
mahāpāśupataṃ pūrvaṃ vilomasya viśuddhaye
juhomi punarastreṇa vauṣaḍanta iti kṣipet
punaḥ pūrṇāṃ tato māyāmabhyarcyātha visarjayet
dharātattvaṃ viśuddhaṃ sajjalena śuddharūpiṇā
bhāvayenmiśritaṃ vāri śuddhiyogyaṃ tato bhavet
tathā tattatpurātattvamiśraṇāduttarottaram
sarvā śivībhavettattvāvalī śuddhānyathā pṛthak
pṛthaktvaṃ ca malo māyābhidhānastasya saṃbhave
karmakṣaye 'pi no muktirbhavedvidyeśvarādivat
tato 'pi jalatattvasya vahnau vyomni cidātmake
āhvānādyakhilaṃ yāvattejasyasya vimiśraṇam
evaṃ kramātkalātattve śuddhe pāśaṃ bhujāśritam
chindyātkalā hi sā kiṃcitkartṛtvonmīlanātmikā
karmākhyamalajṛmbhātmā taṃ ca granthiṃ srugagragam
pūrṇāhutyā samaṃ vahnimantratejasi nirdahet
mantro hi viśvarūpaḥ sannupāśrayavaśāttathā
vyaktarūpastato vahnau pāśaploṣavidhāyakaḥ
pluṣṭo līnasvabhāvo 'sau pāśastaṃ prati śambhuvat
parameśamahātejaḥśeṣamātratvam aśnute
karmapāśe 'tra hotavye pūrṇayāsya śubhāśubham
aśubhaṃ vā bhavadbhūtaṃ bhāvi vātha samastakam
dahāmi phaṭtrayaṃ vauṣaḍiti pūrṇāṃ vinikṣipet
evaṃ māyāntasaṃśuddhau kaṇṭhapāśaṃ ca homayet
pūrṇasya tasya māyākhyaṃ pāśabhedaprathātmakam
dahāmi phaṭtrayaṃ vauṣaḍiti pūrṇāṃ kṣipedguruḥ
nirbījā yadi kāryā tu tadātraivāparāṃ kṣipet
pūrṇāṃ samayapāśākhyabījadāhapadānvitām
gurau deve tathā śāstre bhaktiḥ kāryāsya nahyasau
samayaḥ śaktipātasya svabhāvo hyeṣa no pṛthak
māyānte śuddhimāyāte vāgīśī yā purābhavat
māyā śaktimayī saiva vidyāśaktitvamaśnute
tacchuddhavidyāmāhūya vidyāśaktiṃ niyojayet
evaṃ krameṇa saṃśuddhe sadāśivapade 'pyalam
śikhāṃ granthiyutāṃ chittvā malamāṇavakaṃ dahet
yato 'dhikārabhogākhyau dvau pāśau tu sadāśive
ityuktyāṇavapāśo 'tra māyīyastu niśāvadhiḥ
śiṣyo yathocitaṃ snāyādācāmeddaiśikaḥ svayam
āṇavākhye vinirdagdhe hyadhovāhiśikhāmale
tataḥ prāguktasakalaprameyaṃ paricintayan
śiṣyadehādimātmīyadehaprāṇādiyojitam
kṛtvātmadehaprāṇāderviśvamantaranusmaret
uktaprakriyayā caivaṃ dṛḍhabuddhir ananyadhīḥ
prāṇasthaṃ deśakālādhvayugaṃ prāṇaṃ ca śaktigam
tāṃ ca saṃvidgatāṃ śuddhāṃ saṃvidaṃ śivarūpiṇīm
śiṣyasaṃvidabhinnāṃ ca mantravahnyādyabhedinīm
dhyāyan prāgvatprayogeṇa śivaṃ sakalaniṣkalam
dvyātmakaṃ vā kṣipetpūrṇāṃ praśāntakaraṇena tu
uktaṃ traiśirase tantre sarvasaṃpūraṇātmakam
mūlādudayagatyā tu śivenduparisaṃplutam
janmāntamadhyakuharamūlasrotaḥsamutthitam
śivārkaraśmibhistīvraiḥ kṣubdhaṃ jñānāmṛtaṃ tu yat
tena saṃtarpayetsamyak praśāntakaraṇena tu
śūnyadhāmābjamadhyasthaprabhākiraṇabhāsvaraḥ
ādheyādhāraniḥspandabodhaśāstraparigrahaḥ
janmādheyaprapañcaikasphoṭasaṃghaṭṭaghaṭṭanaḥ
mūlasthānātsamārabhya kṛtvā someśamantagam
khamivātiṣṭhate yāvatpraśāntaṃ tāvaducyate
uktaṃ śrīpūrvaśāstre ca srucamāpūrya sarpiṣā
kṛtvā śiṣyaṃ tathātmasthaṃ mūlamantramanusmaran
śivaṃ śaktiṃ tathātmānaṃ śiṣyaṃ sarpistathānalam
ekīkurvañchanair gacched dvādaśāntam ananyadhīḥ
tatra kumbhakamāsthāya dhyāyansakalaniṣkalam
tiṣṭhettāvadanudvigno yāvadājyakṣayo bhavet
evaṃ yuktaḥ pare tattve guruṇā śivamūrtinā
na bhūyaḥ paśutāmeti dagdhamāyānibandhanaḥ
dehapāte punaḥ prepsed yadi tattveṣu kutracit
bhogān samastavyastatvabhedairante paraṃ padam
tadā tattattvabhūmau tu tatsaṃkhyāyām ananyadhīḥ
punaryojanikāṃ kuryātpūrṇāhutyantareṇa tu
muktipradā bhogamokṣapradā vā yā prakīrtitā
dīkṣā sā syāt sabījatvanirbījātmatayā dvidhā
bāle nirjñātamaraṇe tvaśakte vā jarādibhiḥ
kāryā nirbījikā dīkṣā śaktipātabalodaye
nirbījāyāṃ sāmayāṃstu pāśānapi viśodhayet
kṛtanirbījadīkṣastu devāgnigurubhaktibhāk
iyataiva śivaṃ yāyāt sadyo bhogān vibhujya vā
śrīmaddīkṣottare coktaṃ cāre ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgule
tattvāny āpādamūrdhāntaṃ bhuvanāni tyajetkramāt
tuṭimātraṃ niṣkalaṃ tadadehaṃ tad ahaṃparam
śaktyā tatra kṣipāmyenamiti dhyāyaṃstu dīkṣayet
sabījāyāṃ tu dīkṣāyāṃ samayānna viśodhayet
viśeṣastvayametasyāṃ yāvajjīvaṃ śiśorguruḥ
śeṣavṛttyai śuddhatattvasṛṣṭiṃ kurvīta pūrṇayā
abhinnācchivasaṃbodhajaladheryugapatsphurat
pūrṇāṃ kṣipaṃstattvajālaṃ dhyāyedbhārūpakaṃ sṛtam
viśuddhatattvasṛṣṭiṃ vā kuryātkumbhābhiṣecanāt
tathā dhyānabalādeva yadvā pūrṇābhiṣecanaiḥ
pṛthivī sthirarūpāsya śivarūpeṇa bhāvitā
sthirīkaroti tāmeva bhāvanāmiti śudhyati
jalamāpyāyayatyenāṃ tejo bhāsvaratāṃ nayet
marudānandasaṃsparśaṃ vyoma vaitatyamāvahet
evaṃ tanmātravargo 'pi śivatāmaya iṣyate
parānandamahāvyāptir aśeṣamalavicyutiḥ
śive gantṛtvamādānamupādeyaśivastutiḥ
śivāmodabharāsvādadarśanasparśanānyalam
tadākarṇanamityevamindriyāṇāṃ viśuddhatā
saṃkalpādhyavasāmānāḥ prakāśo raktisaṃsthitī
śivātmatvena yatseyaṃ śuddhatā mānasādike
niyamo rañjanaṃ kartṛbhāvaḥ kalanayā saha
vedanaṃ heyavastvaṃśaviṣaye suptakalpatā
itthaṃ śivaikyarūḍhasya ṣaṭkañcukagaṇo 'pyayam
śuddha eva pumān prāptaśivabhāvo viśudhyati
vidyeśādiṣu tattveṣu naiva kācidaśuddhatā
ityevaṃ śuddhatattvānāṃ sṛṣṭyā śiṣyo 'pi tanmayaḥ
bhaveddhyetatsūcitaṃ śrīmālinīvijayottare
bandhamokṣāvubhāvetāvindriyāṇi jagurbudhāḥ
nigṛhītāni bandhāya vimuktāni vimuktaye
etāni vyāpake bhāve yadā syurmanasā saha
muktāni kvāpi viṣaye rodhādbandhāya tāni tu
ityevaṃ dvividho bhāvaḥ śuddhāśuddhaprabhedataḥ
indriyāṇāṃ samākhyātaḥ siddhayogīśvare mate
śrīmān vidyāgurustvāha pramāṇastutidarśane
samastamantrairdīkṣāyāṃ niyamastveṣa kathyate
māyāntaśuddhau sarvāḥ syuḥ kriyā hyaparayā sadā
dvyātmayā sakalānte tu niṣkale parayaiva tu
īśānte ca pivanyādi sakalānte 'ṅgapañcakam
ityevaṃ vidhimālocya karma kuryādgurūttamaḥ
purādhvani hutīnāṃ yā saṃkhyeyaṃ tattvavarṇayoḥ
tāmeva dviguṇīkuryāt padādhvani caturguṇām
kramānmantrakalāmārge dviguṇā dviguṇā kramāt
yāvattritattvasaṃśuddhau syādviṃśatiguṇā tataḥ
pratikarma bhavetṣaṣṭirāhutīnāṃ tritattvake
ekatattve śataṃ prāhurāhutīnāṃ tu sāṣṭakam
vilomakarmaṇā sākaṃ yāḥ pūrṇāhutayaḥ smṛtāḥ
tāsāṃ sarvādhvasaṃśuddhau saṃkhyānyatvaṃ na kiṃcana
ityeṣā kathitā dīkṣā jananādisamanvitā
atha saṃkṣiptadīkṣeyaṃ śivatāpattidocyate
na rajo nādhivāso 'tra na bhūkṣetraparigrahaḥ
yatra tatra pradeśe tu pūjayitvā guruḥ śivam
adhvānaṃ manasā dhyātvā dīkṣayettattvapāragaḥ
jananādivihīnāṃ tu yena yenādhvanā guruḥ
kuryātsa ekatattvāntāṃ śivabhāvaikabhāvitaḥ
parāmantrastato 'syeti tattvaṃ saṃśodhayāmyatha
svāheti pratitattvaṃ syācchuddhe pūrṇāhutiṃ kṣipet
evaṃ mantrāntaraiḥ kuryātsamastairathavoktavat
parāsaṃpuṭitaṃ nāma svāhāntaṃ prathamāntakam
śataṃ sahasraṃ sāṣṭaṃ vā tena śaktyaiva homayet
tataḥ pūrṇeti saṃśodhyahīnamuttamamīdṛśam
dīkṣākarmoditaṃ tatra tatra śāstre maheśinā
pratyekaṃ mātṛkāyugmavarṇaistattvāni śodhayet
yadi vā piṇḍamantreṇa sarvamantreṣvayaṃ vidhiḥ
yathā yathā ca svabhyastajñānastanmayatātmakaḥ
gurustathā tathā kuryāt saṃkṣiptaṃ karma nānyathā
śrībrahmayāmale coktaṃ saṃkṣipte 'pi hi bhāvayet
vyāptiṃ sarvādhvasāmānyāṃ kiṃtu yāge na vistaraḥ
atanmayībhūtamiti vikṣiptaṃ karma saṃdadhat
kramāttādātmyametīti vikṣiptaṃ vidhimācaret
saṃkṣipto vidhirukto 'yaṃ kṛpayā yaḥ śivoditaḥ
dīkṣottare kairaṇe ca tatra tatrāpi śāsane
atha sadyaḥsamutkrāntipradā dīkṣā nirūpyate
tatkṣaṇāccopabhogādvā dehapāte śivaṃ vrajet
ityuktyā mālinīśāstre sūcitāsau maheśinā
dehapāte samīpasthe śaktipātasphuṭatvataḥ
āsādya śāṃkarīṃ dīkṣāṃ tasmāddīkṣākṣaṇātparam
śivaṃ vrajedityartho 'tra pūrvāparavivecanāt
vyākhyātaḥ śrīmatāsmākaṃ guruṇā śambhumūrtinā
yadā hyāsannamaraṇe śaktipātaḥ prajāyate
tatra mande 'tha gurvādisevayāyuḥ kṣayaṃ vrajet
athavā bandhumitrādidvārā sāsya vibhoḥ patet
pūrvaṃ vā samayī naiva parāṃ dīkṣāmavāptavān
āptadīkṣo 'pi vā prāṇāñjihāsuḥ kleśavarjitam
antyāngurustadā kuryāt sadya utkrāntidīkṣaṇam
natvapakvamale nāpi śeṣakārmikavigrahe
kuryādutkramaṇaṃ śrīmadgahvare ca nirūpitam
dṛṣṭvā śiṣyaṃ jarāgrastaṃ vyādhinā paripīḍitam
utkramayya tatastvenaṃ paratattve niyojayet
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatve kāmacāravidhānataḥ
pūrvoktamarthajātaṃ śrīśambhunātra nirūpitam
vidhiṃ pūrvoditaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvā samayaśuddhitaḥ
kṣurikāmasya vinyasyejjvalantīṃ marmakartarīm
kṛtvā pūrvoditaṃ nyāsaṃ kālānalasamaprabham
saṃhṛtikramataḥ sārdhaṃ sṛkchindiyugalena tu
āgneyīṃ dhāraṇāṃ kṛtvā sarvamarmapratāpanīm
pūrayedvāyunā dehamaṅguṣṭhānmastakāntakam
tamutkṛṣya tato 'ṅguṣṭhādūrdhvāntaṃ vakṣyamāṇayā
kṛntenmarmāṇi randhrāntāt kālarātryā visarjayet
anena kramayogena yojito hutivarjitaḥ
samayyapyeti tāṃ dīkṣāmiti śrīmālinīmate
ṣoḍaśādhāraṣaṭcakralakṣyatrayakhapañcakāt
kvacidanyataratrātha prāguktapaśukarmavat
praviśya mūlaṃ kandādeśchindannaikyavibhāvanāt
pūrṇāhutiprayogeṇa sveṣṭe dhāmni niyojayet
jñānatriśūlaṃ saṃdīptaṃ dīptacakratrayojjvalam
cintayitvāmunā tasya vedanaṃ bodhanaṃ bhramam
dīpanaṃ tāḍanaṃ todaṃ calanaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ
kandādicakragaṃ kuryādviśeṣeṇa hṛdambuje
dvādaśānte tataḥ kṛtvā binduyugmagate kṣipet
nirlakṣye vā pare dhāmni saṃyuktaḥ parameśvaraḥ
na tasya kuryātsaṃskāraṃ kaṃcidityāha gahvare
devaḥ kimasya pūrṇasya śrāddhādyairiti bhāvitaḥ
śrīmaddīkṣottare tveṣa vidhirvahnipuṭīkṛtaḥ
haṃsaḥ pumānadhastasya rudrabindusamanvitaḥ
śiṣyadehe niyojyaitadanudvignaḥ śataṃ japet
utkramyordhvanimeṣeṇa śiṣya itthaṃ paraṃ vrajet
eṣa eva vidhiḥ śrīmatsiddhayogīśvarīmate
iyam utkrāmaṇī dīkṣā kartavyā yogino guroḥ
anabhyastaprāṇacāraḥ kathamenāṃ kariṣyati
vakṣyamāṇāṃ brahmavidyāṃ sakalāṃ niṣkalombhitām
karṇe 'sya vā paṭhedbhūyo bhūyo vāpyatha pāṭhayet
svayaṃ ca karma kurvīta tattvaśuddhyādikaṃ guruḥ
mantrakriyābalātpūrṇāhutyetthaṃ yojayetpare
yogābhyāsam akṛtvāpi sadya utkrāntidāṃ guruḥ
jñānamantrakriyādhyānabalātkartuṃ bhavetprabhuḥ
anayotkramyate śiṣyo balādevaikakaṃ kṣaṇam
kālasyollaṅghya bhogo hi kṣaṇiko 'syāstu kiṃ tataḥ
sadya utkrāntidā cānyā yasyāṃ pūrṇāhutiṃ tadā
dadyādyadāsya prāṇāḥ syurdhruvaṃ niṣkramaṇecchavaḥ
vināpi kriyayā bhāvibrahmavidyābalādguruḥ
karṇajāpaprayogeṇa tattvakañcukajālataḥ
niḥsārayanyathābhīṣṭe sakale niṣkale dvaye
tattve vā yatra kutrāpi yojayetpudgalaṃ kramāt
samayī putrako vāpi paṭhedvidyāmimāṃ tathā
tatpāṭhāttu samayyuktāṃ rudrāṃśāpattimaśnute
etau jape cādhyayane yasmādadhikṛtāvubhau
nādhyāpanopadeśe vā sa eṣo 'dhyayanādṛte
paṭhatostvanayorvastusvabhāvāttasya sā gatiḥ
yathā niṣiddhabhūtādikarmā mantraṃ smaransvayam
āviṣṭe 'pi kvacinnaiti lopaṃ kartṛtvavarjanāt
yathā ca vācayañśāstraṃ samayī śūnyaveśmani
na lupyate tadantaḥsthaprāṇivargopakārataḥ
tathā svayaṃ paṭhanneṣa vidyāṃ vastusvabhāvataḥ
tasminmukte na lupyeta yataḥ kiṃcitkaro 'tra saḥ
nanu cādīkṣitāgre sa noccarecchāstrapaddhatim
hanta kuḍyāgrato 'pyasya niṣedhastvatha kathyate
paryudāsena yaḥ śrotumavadhārayituṃ kṣamaḥ
sa evātra niṣiddho no kuḍyakīṭapatatriṇaḥ
tarhi pāṣāṇatulyo 'sau vilīnendriyavṛttikaḥ
tasyāgre paṭhatastasya niṣedhollaṅghanā katham
sa tu vastusvabhāvena galitākṣo 'pi budhyate
akṣānapekṣayaivāntaścicchaktyā svaprakāśayā
prāgdehaṃ kila tityakṣur nottaraṃ cādhitaṣṭhivān
madhye prabodhakabalāt pratibudhyet pudgalaḥ
mantrāḥ śabdamayāḥ śuddhavimarśātmatayā svayam
arthātmanā cāvabhāntas tadarthapratibodhakāḥ
tenāsya galitākṣasya prabodho jāyate svayam
svacitsamānajātīyamantrāmarśanasaṃnidheḥ
yathā hyalpajavo vāyuḥ sajātīyavimiśritaḥ
javī tathātmā saṃsuptāmarśo 'pyevaṃ prabudhyate
prabuddhaḥ sa ca saṃjāto na cādīkṣita ucyate
dīkṣā hi nāma saṃskāro na tvanyatso 'sti cāsya hi
ata eva nijaṃ śāstraṃ paṭhati kvāpi sāmaye
tacchrutvā ko 'pi dhanyaścenmucyate nāsya sā kṣatiḥ
śāstranindāṃ maiṣa kārṣīddvayoḥ pātityadāyinīm
ityevaṃparam etannādīkṣitāgre paṭhediti
yathā ca samayī kāṣṭhe loṣṭe vā mantrayojanām
kurvaṃstasmiṃścalatyeti na lopaṃ tadvadatra hi
yato 'sya pratyayaprāptiprepsoḥ samayinastathā
pravṛttasya svabhāvena tasminmukte na vai kṣatiḥ
sādhakastu sadā sādhye phale niyatiyantraṇāt
makṣikāśrutamantro 'pi prāyaścittaucitīṃ caret
itthaṃ sadyaḥsamutkrāntiryoktā tāmājñayā guroḥ
samayyādirapi proktakāle proktārthasiddhaye
svayaṃ kuryātsamabhyastaprāṇacāragamāgamaḥ
akṛtādhikṛtirvāpi guruḥ samayaśuddhaye
adhastanapadāvastho natu jñāneddhacetanaḥ
itīyaṃ sadya utkrāntiḥ sūcitā mālinīmate
svayaṃ vā guruṇā vātha kāryatvena maheśinā
sarvaṃ bhogaṃ virūpaṃ tu matvā dehaṃ tyajedyadi
tadā tena krameṇāśu yojitaḥ samayī śivaḥ
ukteyaṃ sadya utkrāntiryā gopyā prāṇavadbudhaiḥ
atha dīkṣāṃ bruve mūḍhajanāśvāsapradāyinīm
trikoṇe vahnisadane vahnivarṇojjvale 'bhitaḥ
vāyavyapuranirdhūte kare savye sujājvale
bījaṃ kiṃcidgṛhītvaitattathaiva hṛdayāntare
kare ca dahyamānaṃ saccintayettajjapaikayuk
vahnidīpitaphaṭkāradhoraṇīdāhapīḍitam
bījaṃ nirbījatāmeti svasūtikaraṇākṣamam
taptaṃ naitatprarohāya tenaiva pratyayena tu
malamāyākhyakarmāṇi mantradhyānakriyābalāt
dagdhāni na svakāryāya nirbījapratyayaṃ tvimam
sa śrīmānsuprasanno me śaṃbhunātho nyarūpayat
bījasyāpyatra kāryā ca yojanā kṛpayā guroḥ
yato dīkṣā sudīptatvātsthāvarāṇyapi mocayet
yo gurur japahomārcādhyānasiddhatvam ātmani
jñātvā dīkṣāṃ carettasya dīkṣā sapratyayā smṛtā
avadhūte nirācāre tattvajñe natvayaṃ vidhiḥ
sācāraiḥ kriyate dīkṣā yā dṛṣṭapratyayānvitā
nirācāreṇa dīkṣāyāṃ pratyayastu na gadyate
jñānaṃ svapratyayaṃ yasmānna phalāntaramarhati
dhyānādi tu phalātsādhyamiti siddhāmatoditam
tulāśuddhiparīkṣāṃ vā kuryātpratyayayoginīm
yathā śrītantrasadbhāve kathitā parameśinā
śrīpūrvaśāstre 'pyeṣā ca sūcitā parameśinā
ānanda udbhavaḥ kampo nidrā ghūrṇiśca pañcamī
ityevaṃvadatā śaktitāratamyābhidhāyinā
udbhavo laghubhāvena dehagrahatirohiteḥ
deho hi pārthivo mukhyastadā mukhyatvamujhati
bhāvilāghavamantreṇa śiṣyaṃ dhyātvā samutplutam
karmāṇi tatrāśeṣāṇi pūrvoktānyācaredguruḥ
uktā seyaṃ tulāśuddhidīkṣā pratyayadāyinī
parokṣasaṃsthitasyātha dīkṣākarma nigadyate
bhuktimuktiprasiddhyarthaṃ nīyate sadguruṃ prati
ityasminmālinīvākye pratiḥ sāṃmukhyavācakaḥ
sāṃmukhyaṃ cāsya śiṣyasya tatkṛpāspadatātmakam
tamārādhyeti vacanaṃ kṛpāhetūpalakṣaṇam
tatsaṃbandhāttataḥ kaścittatkṣaṇādapavṛjyate
ityasyāyamapi hyartho mālinīvākyasanmaṇeḥ
tatkṣaṇāditi nāsyāsti yiyāsādikṣaṇāntaram
kiṃtvevameva karuṇānighnastaṃ gururuddharet
gurusevākṣīṇatanordīkṣām aprāpya pañcatām
gatasyātha svayaṃ mṛtyukṣaṇoditatathāruceḥ
athavādharatantrādidīkṣāsaṃskārabhāginaḥ
prāptasāmayikasyātha parāṃ dīkṣām avindataḥ
ḍimbāhatasya yogeśībhakṣitasyābhicārataḥ
mṛtasya guruṇā yantratantrādinihatasya vā
bhraṣṭasvasamayasyātha dīkṣāṃ prāptavato 'pyalam
bandhubhāryāsuhṛtputragāḍhābhyarthanayogataḥ
svayaṃ tadviṣayotpannakaruṇābalato 'pi vā
vijñātatanmukhāyātaśaktipātāṃśadharmaṇaḥ
gururdīkṣāṃ mṛtoddhārīṃ kurvīta śivadāyinīm
śrīmṛtyuñjayasiddhādau taduktaṃ parameśinā
adīkṣite nṛpatyādāvalase patite mṛte
bālāturastrīvṛddhe ca mṛtoddhāraṃ prakalpayet
vidhiḥ sarvaḥ pūrvamuktaḥ sa tu saṃkṣipta iṣyate
gurvādipūjārahito bāhye bhogāya sā yataḥ
adhivāsacarukṣetraṃ śayyāmaṇḍalakalpane
nopayogyatra tacchiṣyasaṃskriyāsvapnadṛṣṭaye
mantrasaṃnidhisaṃtṛptiyogāyātra tu maṇḍalam
bhūyodine ca devārcā sākṣānnāsyopakāri tat
kriyopakaraṇasthānamaṇḍalākṛtimantrataḥ
dhyānayogaikatadbhaktijñānatanmayabhāvataḥ
tatpraviṣṭasya kasyāpi śiṣyāṇāṃ ca gurostathā
ekādaśaite kathitāḥ saṃnidhānāya hetavaḥ
uttarottaramutkṛṣṭāstathā vyāmiśraṇāvaśāt
kriyātibhūyasī puṣpādyuttamaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam
ekaliṅgādi ca sthānaṃ yatrātmā samprasīdati
maṇḍalaṃ tritriśūlābjacakraṃ yanmantramaṇḍale
anāhūte 'pi dṛṣṭaṃ satsamayitvaprasādhanam
taduktaṃ mālinītantre siddhaṃ samayamaṇḍalam
yena saṃdṛṣṭamātreti siddhamātrapadadvayāt
ākṛtirdīptarūpā yā mantrastadvatsudīptikaḥ
śiṣṭaṃ spaṣṭamato neha kathitaṃ vistarātpunaḥ
kṛtvā maṇḍalamabhyarcya tatra devaṃ kuśairatha
gomayenākṛtiṃ kuryācchiṣyavattāṃ nidhāpayet
tatastasyāṃ śodhyamekamadhvānaṃ vyāptibhāvanāt
prakṛtyantaṃ vinikṣipya punarenaṃ vidhiṃ caret
mahājālaprayogeṇa sarvasmādadhvamadhyataḥ
cittamākṛṣya tatrasthaṃ kuryāttadvidhirucyate
mūlādhārādudetya prasṛtasuvitatānantanāḍyadhvadaṇḍaṃ vīryeṇākramya nāsāgaganaparigataṃ vikṣipan vyāptumīṣṭe
yāvad dhūmābhirāmapracitataraśikhājālakenādhvacakraṃ saṃchādyābhīṣṭajīvānayanamiti mahājālanāmā prayogaḥ
etenācchādanīyaṃ vrajati paravaśaṃ saṃmukhīnatvamādau paścād ānīyate cetsakalamatha tato 'pyadhvamadhyādyatheṣṭam
ākṛṣṭāvuddhṛtau vā mṛtajanaviṣaye karṣaṇīye 'tha jīve yogaḥ śrīśaṃbhunāthāgamaparigamito jālanāmā mayoktaḥ
ciravighaṭite senāyugme yathāmilite punarhayagajanaraṃ svāṃ svāṃ jātiṃ rasādabhidhāvati
karaṇapavanairnāḍīcakraistathaiva samāgatairnijanijarasād ekībhāvyaṃ svajālavaśīkṛtaiḥ
mahājālasamākṛṣṭo jīvo vijñānaśālinā
svaḥpretatiryaṅnirayāṃs tadaivaiṣa vimuñcati
tajjñānamantrayogāptaḥ puruṣaścaiṣa kṛtrimam
yogīva sādhyahṛdayāttadā tādātmyamujhati
sthāvarādidaśāś citrās tatsalokasamīpatāḥ
tyajecceti na citraṃ sa evaṃ yaḥ karmaṇāpi vā
adhikāriśarīratvānmānuṣye tu śarīragaḥ
na tadā mucyate dehāddehānte tu śivaṃ vrajet
tasmindehe tu kāpy asya jāyate śāṅkarī parā
bhaktirūhācca vijñānādācāryādvāpyasevitāt
taddehasaṃsthito 'pyeṣa jīvo jālabalādimam
dārbhādidehaṃ vyāpnoti svādhiṣṭhityāpyacetayan
yogamantrakriyājñānabhūyobalavaśātpunaḥ
manuṣyadehamapyeṣa tadaivāśu vimuñcati
suptakalpo 'pyadeho 'pi yo jīvaḥ so 'pi jālataḥ
ākṛṣṭo dārbhamāyāti dehaṃ phalamayaṃ ca vā
jātīphalādi yatkiṃcittena vā dehakalpanā
antarbahirdvayaucityāttadatrotkṛṣṭamucyate
tato jālakramānītaḥ sa jīvaḥ suptavatsthitaḥ
manoviśiṣṭadehādisāmagrīprāptyabhāvataḥ
na spandate na jānāti na vakti na kilecchati
tādṛśasyaiva saṃskārān sarvān prāgvatprakalpayet
nirbījadīkṣāyogena sarvaṃ kṛtvā puroditam
vidhiṃ yojanikāṃ pūrṇāhutyā sākaṃ kṣipecca tam
dārbhādidehe mantrāgnāvarpite pūrṇayā saha
muktapāśaḥ śivaṃ yāti punarāvṛttivarjitaḥ
sapratyayā tviyaṃ yatra spandate darbhajā tanuḥ
tatra prāṇamanomantrārpaṇayogāttathā bhavet
sābhyāsasya tadapyuktaṃ balāśvāsi na tatkṛte
mṛtoddhāroditaireva yathāsaṃbhūti hetubhiḥ
jīvatparokṣadīkṣāpi kāryā nirbījikā tu sā
tasyāṃ darbhākṛtiprāyakalpane jālayogataḥ
saṃkalpamātreṇākarṣo jīvasya mṛtibhītitaḥ
śiṣṭaṃ prāgvat kuśādyutthākāraviploṣavarjitam
pārimityādanaiśvaryātsādhye niyatiyantraṇāt
jālākṛṣṭirvinābhyāsaṃ rāgadveṣānna jāyate
parokṣa evātulyābhirdīkṣābhiryadi dīkṣitaḥ
tatrottaraṃ syādbalavatsaṃskārāya tvadhastanam
bhuktiyojanikāyāṃ tu bhūyobhirgurubhistathā
kṛtāyāṃ bhogavaicitryaṃ hetuvaicitryayogataḥ
parokṣadīkṣaṇe māyottīrṇe bhogāya yojayet
bhogānīpsā durlabhā hi satī vā bhogahānaye
uktaṃ hi svānyasaṃvittyoḥ svasaṃvidbalavattarā
bādhakatve bādhikāsau sāmyaudāsīnyayostathā
śrīmān dharmaśivo 'pyāha pārokṣyāṃ karmapaddhatau
parokṣadīkṣaṇe samyak pūrṇāhutividhau yadi
agniś ciṭiciṭāśabdaṃ sadhūmaṃ pratimuñcati
dhatte nīlāmbudacchāyāṃ muhurjvalati śāmyati
vistaro ghorarūpaśca mahīṃ dhāvati cāpyadhaḥ
dhvāṃkṣādyaśravyaśabdo vā tadā taṃ lakṣayedguruḥ
brahmahatyādibhiḥ pāpaistatsaṅgaiścopapātakaiḥ
tadā tasya na kartavyā dīkṣāsmin akṛte vidhau
navātmā phaṭpuṭāntaḥsthaḥ punaḥ pañcaphaḍanvitaḥ
amukasyeti pāpāni dahāmyanu phaḍaṣṭakam
iti sāhasriko homaḥ kartavyastilataṇḍulaiḥ
ante pūrṇā ca dātavyā tato 'smai dīkṣayā guruḥ
parayojanaparyantaṃ kuryāttattvaviśodhanam
pratyakṣe 'pi sthitasyāṇoḥ pāpino bhagavanmayīm
śaktiṃ prāptavato jyeṣṭhāmevameva vidhiṃ caret
yadi vā daiśikaḥ samyaṅ na dīptastasya tatpurā
prāyaścittaistathā dānaiḥ prāṇāyāmaiśca śodhanam
kṛtvā vidhimimāṃ cāpi dīkṣāṃ kuryādaśaṅkitaḥ
sarvathā vartamāno 'pi tattvavinmocayetpaśūn
icchayaiva śivaḥ sākṣāttasmāttaṃ pūjayetsadā
śāṭhyaṃ tatra na kāryaṃ ca tatkṛtvādho vrajecchiśuḥ
na punaḥ kīrtayettasya pāpaṃ kīrtayitā vrajet
nirayaṃ varjayettasmāditi dīkṣottare vidhiḥ
