eṣā parokṣadīkṣā dvidhoditā jīvaditarabhedena
athocyate śeṣavṛttirjīvatāmupayoginī
dīkṣā bahuprakāreyaṃ śrāddhāntā yā prakīrtitā
sā saṃskriyāyai mokṣāya bhogāyāpi dvayāya vā
tatra saṃskārasiddhyai yā dīkṣā sākṣānna mocanī
anusaṃdhivaśādyā ca sākṣānmoktrī sabījikā
tayobhayyā dīkṣitā ye teṣāmājīvavartanam
vaktavyaṃ putrakādīnāṃ tanmayatvaprasiddhaye
bubhukṣorvā mumukṣorvā svasaṃvidguruśāstrataḥ
pramāṇādyā saṃskriyāyai dīkṣā hi guruṇā kṛtā
tataḥ sa saṃskṛtaṃ yogyaṃ jñātvātmānaṃ svaśāsane
taduktavastvanuṣṭhānaṃ bhuktyai muktyai ca sevate
ācāryapratyayādeva yo 'pi syādbhuktimuktibhāk
tatpratyūhodayadhvastyai brūyāttasyāpi vartanam
svasaṃvidgurusaṃvittyostulyapratyayabhāgapi
śeṣavṛttyā samādeśyas tadvighnādipraśāntaye
yaḥ sarvathā parāpekṣāmujjhitvā tu sthito nijāt
pratyayādyo 'pi cācāryapratyayādeva kevalāt
tau sāṃsiddhikanirbījau ko vadeccheṣavṛttaye
kramāttanmayatopāyagurvarcanaratau tu tau
tatraiṣāṃ śeṣavṛttyarthaṃ nityanaimittike dhruve
kāmyavarjaṃ yataḥ kāmāś citrāś citrābhyupāyakāḥ
tatra nityo vidhiḥ sandhyānuṣṭhānaṃ devatāvraje
gurvagniśāstrasahite pūjā bhūtadayetyayam
naimittikastu sarveṣāṃ parvaṇāṃ pūjanaṃ japaḥ
viśeṣavaśataḥ kiṃca pavitrakavidhikramaḥ
ācāryasya ca dīkṣeyaṃ bahubhedā vivecitā
vyākhyādikaṃ ca tattasyādhikaṃ naimittikaṃ dhruvam
tatrādau śiśave brūyād gurur nityavidhiṃ sphuṭam
tadyogyatāṃ samālokya vitatāvitatātmanām
mukhyetarādimantrāṇāṃ vīryavyāptyādiyogyatām
dṛṣṭvā śiṣye tamevāsmai mūlamantraṃ samarpayet
tacchāstradīkṣito hyeṣa niryantrācāraśaṅkitaḥ
na mukhye yogya ityanyasevātaḥ syāttu yogyatā
sādhakasya bubhukṣostu sādhakībhāvino 'pivā
puṣpapātavaśātsiddho mantro 'rpyaḥ sādhyasiddhaye
vitate guṇabhūte vā vidhau diṣṭe punarguruḥ
jñātvāsmai yogyatāṃ sāraṃ saṃkṣiptaṃ vidhimācaret
tatraiṣa niyamo yadyan māntraṃ rūpaṃ na tadguruḥ
likhitvā prathayecchiṣye viśeṣādūrdhvaśāsane
mantrā varṇātmakāste ca parāmarśātmakāḥ sa ca
gurusaṃvidabhinnaś cet saṃkrāmetsā tataḥ śiśau
lipisthitastu yo mantro nirvīryaḥ so 'tra kalpitaḥ
saṃketabalato nāsya pustakātprathate mahaḥ
pustakādhītavidyāścetyuktaṃ siddhāmate tataḥ
ye tu pustakalabdhe 'pi mantre vīryaṃ prajānate
te bhairavīyasaṃskārāḥ proktāḥ sāṃsiddhikā iti
iti jñātvā guruḥ samyak paramānandaghūrṇitaḥ
tādṛśe tādṛśe dhāmni pūjayitvā vidhiṃ caret
yathānyaśiṣyānuṣṭhānaṃ nānyaśiṣyeṇa budhyate
tathā kuryādgururguptihānirdoṣavatī yataḥ
devīnāṃ tritayaṃ śuddhaṃ yadvā yāmalayogataḥ
devīmekāmatho śuddhāṃ vadedvā yāmalātmikām
tatra mantraṃ sphuṭaṃ vaktrādguruṇopāṃśu coditam
avadhāryā pravṛttestamabhyasyenmanasā svayam
tataḥ suśikṣitāṃ sthānadehāntaḥśodhanatrayīm
nyāsaṃ dhyānaṃ japaṃ mudrāṃ pūjāṃ kuryātprayatnataḥ
tatra prabhāte saṃbudhya sveṣṭāṃ prāgdevatāṃ smaret
kṛtāvaśyakakartavyaḥ śuddho bhūtvā tato gṛham
āśrityottaradigvaktraḥ sthānadehāntaratraye
śuddhiṃ vidhāya mantrāṇāṃ yathāsthānaṃ niveśanam
mudrāpradarśanaṃ dhyānaṃ bhedābhedasvarūpataḥ
dehāsudhīvyomabhūṣu manasā tatra cārcanam
japaṃ cātra yathāśakti devāyaitannivedanam
tanmayībhāvasiddhyarthaṃ pratisandhyaṃ samācaret
anye tu prāgudakpaścāddaśadikṣu catuṣṭayīm
sandhyānāmāhuretacca tāntrikīyaṃ na no matam
yāsau kālādhikāre prāk sandhyā proktā catuṣṭayī
tāmevāntaḥ samādhāya sāndhyaṃ vidhimupācaret
sandhyācatuṣṭayīkṛtyamekasyāmathavā śiśuḥ
kuryāt svādhyāyavijñānagurukṛtyāditatparaḥ
sandhyādhyānoditānantatanmayībhāvayuktitaḥ
tatsaṃskāravaśātsarvaṃ kālaṃ syāttanmayo hyasau
tato yatheṣṭakāle 'sau pūjāṃ puṣpāsavādibhiḥ
sthaṇḍilādau śiśuḥ kuryādvibhavādyanurūpataḥ
suśuddhaḥ sanvidhiṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvāntarajapāntakam
arghapātraṃ purā yadvadvidhāya sveṣṭamantrataḥ
tena sthaṇḍilapuṣpādi sarvaṃ saṃprokṣayedbudhaḥ
tatastatraiva saṃkalpya dvārāsanagurukramam
pūjayecchivatāviṣṭaḥ svadehārcāpuraḥsaram
tatastatsthaṇḍilaṃ vīdhravyomasphaṭikanirmalam
bodhātmakaṃ samālokya tatra svaṃ devatāgaṇam
pratibimbatayā paśyedbimbatvena ca bodhataḥ
etadāvāhanaṃ mukhyaṃ vyajanānmarutāmiva
sarvago 'pi marudyadvadvyajanenopajīvitaḥ
arthakṛtsarvagaṃ mantracakraṃ rūḍhestathā bhavet
catuṣkapañcāśikayā tadetattattvamucyate
śrīnirmaryādaśāstre ca tadetadvibhunoditam
devaḥ sarvagato deva nirmaryādaḥ kathaṃ śivaḥ
āvāhyate kṣamyate vety evaṃ pṛṣṭo 'bravīdvibhuḥ
vāsanāvāhyate devi vāsanā ca visṛjyate
paramārthena devasya nāvāhanavisarjane
āvāhito mayā devaḥ sthaṇḍile ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ
pūjitaḥ stuta ityevaṃ hṛṣṭvā devaṃ visarjayet
prāṇinām aprabuddhānāṃ santoṣajananāya vai
āvāhanādikaṃ teṣāṃ pravṛttiḥ kathamanyathā
kālena tu vijānanti pravṛttāḥ patiśāsane
anukrameṇa devasya prāptiṃ bhuvanapūrvikām
jñānadīpadyutidhvastasamastājñānasaṃcayāḥ
kuto vānīyate devaḥ kutra vā nīyate 'pi saḥ
sthūlasūkṣmādibhedena sa hi sarvatra saṃsthitaḥ
āvāhite mantragaṇe puṣpāsavanivedanaiḥ
dhūpaiśca tarpaṇaṃ kāryaṃ śraddhābhaktibalocitaiḥ
dīptānāṃ śaktinādādimantrāṇāmāsavaiḥ palaiḥ
raktaiḥ prāk tarpaṇaṃ paścāt puṣpadhūpādivistaraiḥ
āgatasya tu mantrasya na kuryāttarpaṇaṃ yadi
haratyardhaśarīraṃ sa ityuktaṃ kila śambhunā
yadyadevāsya manasi vikāsitvaṃ prayacchati
tenaiva kuryātpūjāṃ sa iti śambhorviniścayaḥ
sādhakānāṃ bubhukṣūṇāṃ vidhirniyatiyantritaḥ
mumukṣūṇāṃ tattvavidāṃ sa eva tu nirargalaḥ
kārye viśeṣamādhitsurviśiṣṭaṃ kāraṇaṃ spṛśet
raktakarpāsatūlecchustulyatadbījapuñjavat
santi bhoge viśeṣāśca vicitrāḥ kāraṇeritāḥ
deśakālānusandhānaguṇadravyakriyādibhiḥ
svalpā kriyā bhūyasī vā hṛdayāhlādadāyibhiḥ
bāhyaiḥ saṃkalpajairvāpi kārakaiḥ parikalpitā
mumukṣorna viśeṣāya naiḥśreyasavidhiṃ prati
nahi brahmaṇi śaṃsanti bāhulyālpatvadurdaśāḥ
citaḥ svātantryasāratvāt tasyānandaghanatvataḥ
kriyā syāttanmayībhūtyai hṛdayāhlādadāyibhiḥ
śivābhedabharādbhāvavargaḥ cyotati yaṃ rasam
tameva parame dhāmni pūjanāyārpayedbudhaḥ
stotreṣu bahudhā caitanmayā proktaṃ nijāhnike
adhiśayya pāramārthikabhāvaprasaraprakāśamullasati
yā paramāmṛtadṛk tvāṃ tayārcayante rahasyavidaḥ
kṛtvādhāradharāṃ camatkṛtirasaprokṣākṣaṇakṣālitāmāttairmānasataḥ svabhāvakusumaiḥ svāmodasaṃdohibhiḥ
ānandāmṛtanirbharasvahṛdayānarghārghapātrakramāt tvāṃ devyā saha dehadevasadane devārcaye 'harniśam
nānāsvādarasāmimāṃ trijagatīṃ hṛccakrayantrārpitām ūrdhvādhyastavivekagauravabharānniṣpīḍya niḥṣyanditam
yatsaṃvitparamāmṛtaṃ mṛtijarājanmāpahaṃ jṛmbhate tena tvāṃ haviṣā pareṇa parame saṃtarpaye 'harniśam
iti ślokatrayopāttamarthamantarvibhāvayan
yena kenāpi bhāvena tarpayeddevatāgaṇam
mudrāṃ pradarśayetpaścānmanasā vāpi yogataḥ
vacasā mantrayogena vapuṣā saṃniveśataḥ
kṛtvā japaṃ tataḥ sarvaṃ devatāyai samarpayet
taccoktaṃ kartṛtātattvanirūpaṇavidhau purā
tato visarjanaṃ kāryaṃ bodhaikātmyaprayogataḥ
kṛtvā vā vahnigāṃ mantratṛptiṃ proktavidhānataḥ
dvārapīṭhaguruvrātasamarpitanivedanāt
ṛte 'nyatsvayamaśnīyādagādhe 'mbhasyatha kṣipet
prāṇino jalajāḥ pūrvadīkṣitāḥ śambhunā svayam
vidhinā bhāvinā śrīmanmīnanāthāvatāriṇā
mārjāramūṣikādyair yad adīkṣaiś cāpi bhakṣitam
tacchaṅkātaṅkadānena vyādhaye narakāya ca
atastattvavidā dhvastaśaṅkātaṅko 'pi paṇḍitaḥ
prakaṭaṃ nedṛśaṃ kuryāllokānugrahavāñchayā
śrīmanmatamahāśāstre taduktaṃ vibhunā svayam
svayaṃ tu śaṅkāsaṅkocaniṣkāsanaparāyaṇaḥ
bhavettathā yathānyeṣāṃ śaṅkā no manasi sphuret
mārjayitvā tataḥ snānaṃ puṣpeṇātha prapūjayet
puṣpādi sarvaṃ tatsthaṃ tadagādhāmbhasi nikṣipet
uktaḥ sthaṇḍilayāgo 'yaṃ nityakarmaṇi śambhunā
